User:
Συνέχισε εδώ τον κώδικα από το προηγούμενο chat
Kimi:
Βλέπω ότι στο προηγούμενο chat δημιουργούσαμε το Manus-Win11 Agent Framework. Θα συνεχίσω από εκεί που σταματήσαμε, ενσωματώνοντας όλες τις βελτιώσεις που ζήτησες:
Συνέχεια: Manus-Win11 Agent Framework
1. AI Model Router (ai_router.py)
Επιλογή βέλτιστου μοντέλου ανά εργασία με token cost optimization:
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""AI Model Router - Intelligent model selection with cost optimization"""import osimport jsonimport hashlibimport timefrom enum import Enumfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, Listfrom pathlib import Pathimport asyncioclass TaskType(Enum):    CODE_GENERATION = "code_generation"    CODE_REVIEW = "code_review"    DEBUGGING = "debugging"    ARCHITECTURE = "architecture"    DOCUMENTATION = "documentation"    ANALYSIS = "analysis"    CREATIVE = "creative"    CHAT = "chat"class ModelTier(Enum):    PREMIUM = "premium"      # GPT-4, Kimi K2.5, Claude 3.5    STANDARD = "standard"    # GPT-3.5, DeepSeek V3    FAST = "fast"            # Lightweight models    LOCAL = "local"          # Local LLMs@dataclassclass ModelConfig:    name: str    provider: str    cost_per_1k_tokens: float    context_window: int    strengths: List[TaskType]    tier: ModelTier    api_key_env: str        def estimate_cost(self, input_tokens: int, output_tokens: int) -> float:        return (input_tokens + output_tokens) * self.cost_per_1k_tokens / 1000class ModelRouter:    """Intelligent routing to optimal AI models with caching and cost tracking"""        MODELS = {        "kimi-k2.5": ModelConfig(            name="Kimi K2.5",            provider="moonshot",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.015,            context_window=256000,            strengths=[TaskType.CODE_GENERATION, TaskType.ARCHITECTURE,                       TaskType.CODE_REVIEW, TaskType.ANALYSIS],            tier=ModelTier.PREMIUM,            api_key_env="KIMI_API_KEY"        ),        "deepseek-chat": ModelConfig(            name="DeepSeek V3",            provider="deepseek",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.002,            context_window=64000,            strengths=[TaskType.CODE_GENERATION, TaskType.DEBUGGING,                       TaskType.ANALYSIS],            tier=ModelTier.STANDARD,            api_key_env="DEEPSEEK_API_KEY"        ),        "deepseek-reasoner": ModelConfig(            name="DeepSeek R1",            provider="deepseek",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.003,            context_window=64000,            strengths=[TaskType.DEBUGGING, TaskType.ARCHITECTURE,                       TaskType.ANALYSIS],            tier=ModelTier.PREMIUM,            api_key_env="DEEPSEEK_API_KEY"        ),        "claude-3-5-sonnet": ModelConfig(            name="Claude 3.5 Sonnet",            provider="anthropic",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.003,            context_window=200000,            strengths=[TaskType.CODE_REVIEW, TaskType.CREATIVE,                       TaskType.DOCUMENTATION],            tier=ModelTier.PREMIUM,            api_key_env="ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"        ),        "gpt-4o-mini": ModelConfig(            name="GPT-4o Mini",            provider="openai",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.00015,            context_window=128000,            strengths=[TaskType.CHAT, TaskType.DOCUMENTATION],            tier=ModelTier.FAST,            api_key_env="OPENAI_API_KEY"        )    }        def __init__(self, cache_dir: str = "./cache"):        self.cache_dir = Path(cache_dir)        self.cache_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)        self.cost_tracker = CostTracker()        self.response_cache = ResponseCache(cache_dir)        self.fallback_chain = ["kimi-k2.5", "deepseek-chat", "claude-3-5-sonnet"]            def select_model(self, task_type: TaskType,                     complexity: str = "medium",                    budget_constraint: Optional[float] = None) -> str:        """Select optimal model based on task and constraints"""                candidates = []        for model_id, config in self.MODELS.items():            if task_type in config.strengths:                score = self._calculate_score(config, complexity)                candidates.append((model_id, config, score))                # Sort by score descending        candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[2], reverse=True)                # Apply budget constraint        if budget_constraint:            candidates = [                (m, c, s) for m, c, s in candidates                 if c.cost_per_1k_tokens <= budget_constraint            ]                return candidates[0][0] if candidates else "kimi-k2.5"        def _calculate_score(self, config: ModelConfig, complexity: str) -> float:        """Calculate suitability score for model"""        base_scores = {            "low": 1.0,            "medium": 1.5,            "high": 2.0        }                complexity_multiplier = base_scores.get(complexity, 1.0)                # Higher context window = better for complex tasks        context_score = min(config.context_window / 100000, 2.0)                # Cost efficiency (inverse)        cost_score = 1.0 / (config.cost_per_1k_tokens * 100 + 1)                return (complexity_multiplier * context_score * cost_score)        async def generate_with_fallback(self,                                    prompt: str,                                   task_type: TaskType,                                   max_retries: int = 3) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Generate with automatic fallback on failure"""                # Check cache first        cache_key = self._generate_cache_key(prompt, task_type)        cached = await self.response_cache.get(cache_key)        if cached:            return {"content": cached, "cached": True, "model": "cache"}                model_id = self.select_model(task_type)        errors = []                for attempt in range(max_retries):            try:                model_config = self.MODELS[model_id]                result = await self._call_model(model_config, prompt)                                # Cache successful response                await self.response_cache.set(cache_key, result["content"])                                # Track cost                self.cost_tracker.log_usage(                    model_id,                     result["input_tokens"],                    result["output_tokens"]                )                                return {                    "content": result["content"],                    "model": model_id,                    "cost": result["cost"],                    "cached": False                }                            except Exception as e:                errors.append(f"{model_id}: {str(e)}")                # Try fallback model                current_idx = self.fallback_chain.index(model_id)                if current_idx < len(self.fallback_chain) - 1:                    model_id = self.fallback_chain[current_idx + 1]                else:                    break                raise Exception(f"All models failed: {'; '.join(errors)}")        def _generate_cache_key(self, prompt: str, task_type: TaskType) -> str:        """Generate deterministic cache key"""        content = f"{task_type.value}:{prompt}"        return hashlib.sha256(content.encode()).hexdigest()[:32]        async def _call_model(self, config: ModelConfig, prompt: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Call specific model API (placeholder for actual implementation)"""        # Implementation would use actual API clients        passclass ResponseCache:    """Semantic caching for LLM responses"""        def __init__(self, cache_dir: str, ttl: int = 86400):        self.cache_dir = Path(cache_dir)        self.ttl = ttl  # 24 hours default            async def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[str]:        cache_file = self.cache_dir / f"{key}.json"        if not cache_file.exists():            return None                    data = json.loads(cache_file.read_text())        if time.time() - data["timestamp"] > self.ttl:            cache_file.unlink()            return None                    return data["content"]        async def set(self, key: str, content: str):        cache_file = self.cache_dir / f"{key}.json"        data = {            "timestamp": time.time(),            "content": content        }        cache_file.write_text(json.dumps(data))class CostTracker:    """Track and optimize API costs"""        def __init__(self, log_file: str = "costs.json"):        self.log_file = Path(log_file)        self.daily_budget = float(os.getenv("DAILY_AI_BUDGET", "10.0"))        self.usage_today = 0.0            def log_usage(self, model: str, input_tokens: int, output_tokens: int):        """Log API usage"""        cost = (input_tokens + output_tokens) * 0.001  # Simplified        self.usage_today += cost                entry = {            "timestamp": time.time(),            "model": model,            "input_tokens": input_tokens,            "output_tokens": output_tokens,            "cost": cost        }                # Append to log        logs = []        if self.log_file.exists():            logs = json.loads(self.log_file.read_text())        logs.append(entry)        self.log_file.write_text(json.dumps(logs[-1000:]))  # Keep last 1000            def get_stats(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Get cost statistics"""        if not self.log_file.exists():            return {"total": 0, "today": self.usage_today}                    logs = json.loads(self.log_file.read_text())        total = sum(e["cost"] for e in logs)                return {            "total": total,            "today": self.usage_today,            "budget_remaining": self.daily_budget - self.usage_today,            "by_model": self._aggregate_by_model(logs)        }        def _aggregate_by_model(self, logs: List[Dict]) -> Dict[str, float]:        """Aggregate costs by model"""        result = {}        for entry in logs:            model = entry["model"]            result[model] = result.get(model, 0) + entry["cost"]        return result
2. Notification System (notifications.py)
Telegram & Slack integration:
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""Notification System - Multi-channel alerts for agent status"""import osimport asyncioimport aiohttpfrom enum import Enumfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Optional, Listfrom datetime import datetimeclass NotificationLevel(Enum):    INFO = "info"    SUCCESS = "success"    WARNING = "warning"    ERROR = "error"    CRITICAL = "critical"@dataclassclass Notification:    title: str    message: str    level: NotificationLevel    timestamp: datetime    project_id: Optional[str] = None    metadata: Optional[dict] = Noneclass NotificationManager:    """Unified notification system supporting multiple channels"""        def __init__(self):        self.telegram_token = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN")        self.telegram_chat_id = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID")        self.slack_webhook = os.getenv("SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL")        self.channels = []                if self.telegram_token:            self.channels.append(TelegramChannel(self.telegram_token, self.telegram_chat_id))        if self.slack_webhook:            self.channels.append(SlackChannel(self.slack_webhook))                    self.channels.append(LogChannel())  # Always log locally        async def notify(self, notification: Notification):        """Send notification to all configured channels"""        tasks = [channel.send(notification) for channel in self.channels]        await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)        async def notify_project_start(self, project_id: str, description: str):        """Notify project initiation"""        await self.notify(Notification(            title="🚀 Project Started",            message=f"Project {project_id}: {description}",            level=NotificationLevel.INFO,            timestamp=datetime.now(),            project_id=project_id        ))        async def notify_checkpoint(self, project_id: str, message: str):        """Notify checkpoint reached (waiting for user input)"""        await self.notify(Notification(            title="⏸️ Checkpoint Reached",            message=message,            level=NotificationLevel.WARNING,            timestamp=datetime.now(),            project_id=project_id        ))        async def notify_completion(self, project_id: str, results: str):        """Notify project completion"""        await self.notify(Notification(            title="✅ Project Completed",            message=f"Project {project_id} finished successfully\nResults: {results}",            level=NotificationLevel.SUCCESS,            timestamp=datetime.now(),            project_id=project_id        ))        async def notify_error(self, project_id: str, error: str, critical: bool = False):        """Notify error occurrence"""        await self.notify(Notification(            title="❌ Error Occurred" if not critical else "🚨 CRITICAL ERROR",            message=f"Project {project_id}: {error}",            level=NotificationLevel.CRITICAL if critical else NotificationLevel.ERROR,            timestamp=datetime.now(),            project_id=project_id        ))class TelegramChannel:    """Telegram Bot integration"""        def __init__(self, token: str, chat_id: str):        self.token = token        self.chat_id = chat_id        self.base_url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{token}"        async def send(self, notification: Notification):        """Send message via Telegram"""        emoji_map = {            NotificationLevel.INFO: "ℹ️",            NotificationLevel.SUCCESS: "✅",            NotificationLevel.WARNING: "⚠️",            NotificationLevel.ERROR: "❌",            NotificationLevel.CRITICAL: "🚨"        }                emoji = emoji_map.get(notification.level, "📌")        text = f"{emoji} *{notification.title}*\n\n{notification.message}"                if notification.project_id:            text += f"\n\n`Project: {notification.project_id}`"                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            url = f"{self.base_url}/sendMessage"            payload = {                "chat_id": self.chat_id,                "text": text,                "parse_mode": "Markdown",                "disable_notification": notification.level not in                     [NotificationLevel.ERROR, NotificationLevel.CRITICAL]            }                        try:                async with session.post(url, json=payload) as resp:                    if resp.status != 200:                        print(f"Telegram notification failed: {await resp.text()}")            except Exception as e:                print(f"Telegram error: {e}")class SlackChannel:    """Slack Webhook integration"""        def __init__(self, webhook_url: str):        self.webhook_url = webhook_url        async def send(self, notification: Notification):        """Send message via Slack"""        color_map = {            NotificationLevel.INFO: "#36a64f",            NotificationLevel.SUCCESS: "#28a745",            NotificationLevel.WARNING: "#ffc107",            NotificationLevel.ERROR: "#dc3545",            NotificationLevel.CRITICAL: "#721c24"        }                payload = {            "attachments": [{                "color": color_map.get(notification.level, "#808080"),                "title": notification.title,                "text": notification.message,                "footer": f"Manus-Win11 Agent | Project: {notification.project_id or 'N/A'}",                "ts": int(notification.timestamp.timestamp())            }]        }                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            try:                async with session.post(self.webhook_url, json=payload) as resp:                    if resp.status != 200:                        print(f"Slack notification failed: {await resp.text()}")            except Exception as e:                print(f"Slack error: {e}")class LogChannel:    """Local logging channel"""        async def send(self, notification: Notification):        """Log to file"""        from pathlib import Path        import json                log_file = Path("notifications.log")        entry = {            "timestamp": notification.timestamp.isoformat(),            "level": notification.level.value,            "title": notification.title,            "message": notification.message,            "project_id": notification.project_id        }                with open(log_file, "a") as f:            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + "\n")
3. Project State Manager (state_manager.py)
Resume capability και checkpoint system:
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""Project State Manager - Persistent state for resumable operations"""import jsonimport pickleimport sqlite3from enum import Enumfrom dataclasses import dataclass, asdictfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, Listfrom pathlib import Pathfrom datetime import datetimeimport asyncioclass ProjectStatus(Enum):    PENDING = "pending"    RUNNING = "running"    PAUSED = "paused"  # Waiting for user input    COMPLETED = "completed"    FAILED = "failed"@dataclassclass Checkpoint:    id: str    timestamp: datetime    description: str    requires_input: bool    input_prompt: Optional[str] = None    resolved: bool = False    user_response: Optional[str] = None@dataclassclass ProjectState:    project_id: str    status: ProjectStatus    created_at: datetime    updated_at: datetime    current_task: Optional[str] = None    completed_tasks: List[str] = None    context: Dict[str, Any] = None    checkpoints: List[Checkpoint] = None    error_log: List[str] = None    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = None        def __post_init__(self):        if self.completed_tasks is None:            self.completed_tasks = []        if self.context is None:            self.context = {}        if self.checkpoints is None:            self.checkpoints = []        if self.error_log is None:            self.error_log = []        if self.metadata is None:            self.metadata = {}class StateManager:    """SQLite-based persistent state management"""        def __init__(self, db_path: str = "projects.db"):        self.db_path = db_path        self._init_db()        def _init_db(self):        """Initialize database schema"""        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            conn.execute("""                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (                    project_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,                    state BLOB,                    updated_at TIMESTAMP                )            """)                        conn.execute("""                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS checkpoints (                    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,                    project_id TEXT,                    timestamp TIMESTAMP,                    data BLOB,                    FOREIGN KEY (project_id) REFERENCES projects(project_id)                )            """)                        conn.commit()        def save_state(self, state: ProjectState):        """Save project state to database"""        state.updated_at = datetime.now()                with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            conn.execute(                "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO projects (project_id, state, updated_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?)",                (state.project_id, pickle.dumps(state), state.updated_at)            )            conn.commit()        def load_state(self, project_id: str) -> Optional[ProjectState]:        """Load project state from database"""        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            cursor = conn.execute(                "SELECT state FROM projects WHERE project_id = ?",                 (project_id,)            )            row = cursor.fetchone()                        if row:                return pickle.loads(row[0])            return None        def list_projects(self, status: Optional[ProjectStatus] = None) -> List[Dict]:        """List all projects, optionally filtered by status"""        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            if status:                cursor = conn.execute(                    "SELECT project_id, updated_at FROM projects WHERE json_extract(state, '$.status') = ?",                    (status.value,)                )            else:                cursor = conn.execute("SELECT project_id, updated_at FROM projects")                        return [{"project_id": row[0], "updated_at": row[1]} for row in cursor.fetchall()]        def create_checkpoint(self, project_id: str, description: str,                         requires_input: bool = False,                         input_prompt: Optional[str] = None) -> Checkpoint:        """Create a new checkpoint"""        checkpoint = Checkpoint(            id=f"{project_id}_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}",            timestamp=datetime.now(),            description=description,            requires_input=requires_input,            input_prompt=input_prompt        )                state = self.load_state(project_id)        if state:            state.checkpoints.append(checkpoint)            state.status = ProjectStatus.PAUSED if requires_input else state.status            self.save_state(state)                return checkpoint        def resolve_checkpoint(self, project_id: str, checkpoint_id: str,                           user_response: str):        """Resolve a pending checkpoint with user input"""        state = self.load_state(project_id)        if not state:            return False                for cp in state.checkpoints:            if cp.id == checkpoint_id:                cp.resolved = True                cp.user_response = user_response                state.status = ProjectStatus.RUNNING                self.save_state(state)                return True        return False        def get_pending_checkpoints(self, project_id: str) -> List[Checkpoint]:        """Get all unresolved checkpoints for a project"""        state = self.load_state(project_id)        if not state:            return []                return [cp for cp in state.checkpoints if not cp.resolved]        def archive_completed(self, days_old: int = 30):        """Archive projects completed more than N days ago"""        cutoff = datetime.now().timestamp() - (days_old * 86400)                with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            conn.execute(                "DELETE FROM projects WHERE updated_at < ? AND json_extract(state, '$.status') = ?",                (cutoff, ProjectStatus.COMPLETED.value)            )            conn.commit()class ResumableTask:    """Decorator/Context manager for resumable operations"""        def __init__(self, state_manager: StateManager, project_id: str,                  task_name: str, notifier=None):        self.state_manager = state_manager        self.project_id = project_id        self.task_name = task_name        self.notifier = notifier        self.state = None        async def __aenter__(self):        self.state = self.state_manager.load_state(self.project_id)                if not self.state:            self.state = ProjectState(                project_id=self.project_id,                status=ProjectStatus.RUNNING,                created_at=datetime.now(),                updated_at=datetime.now()            )                # Check if task already completed        if self.task_name in self.state.completed_tasks:            print(f"Task {self.task_name} already completed, skipping...")            return None                self.state.current_task = self.task_name        self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                return self        async def __aexit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):        if exc_type is None:            # Success - mark task complete            self.state.completed_tasks.append(self.task_name)            self.state.current_task = None            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)        else:            # Failure - log error            self.state.error_log.append(f"{datetime.now()}: {str(exc_val)}")            self.state.status = ProjectStatus.FAILED            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                        if self.notifier:                await self.notifier.notify_error(                    self.project_id,                     str(exc_val),                    critical=True                )                return False  # Don't suppress exceptions        async def checkpoint(self, description: str, input_prompt: Optional[str] = None):        """Create a checkpoint that may require user input"""        requires_input = input_prompt is not None                cp = self.state_manager.create_checkpoint(            self.project_id, description, requires_input, input_prompt        )                if self.notifier and requires_input:            await self.notifier.notify_checkpoint(                self.project_id,                f"{description}\n\nInput required: {input_prompt}"            )                # Wait for resolution if input required        while requires_input and not cp.resolved:            await asyncio.sleep(1)            # Reload to check for updates            pending = self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(self.project_id)            for p in pending:                if p.id == cp.id and p.resolved:                    return p.user_response                        # Timeout or check mechanism could go here                return cp
4. Enhanced Agent Core (agent_core_v2.py)
Ενσωμάτωση όλων των νέων δυνατοτήτων:
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""Manus-Win11 Agent Core v2.0Enhanced with AI routing, notifications, and resume capability"""import asyncioimport osfrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, Callablefrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom ai_router import ModelRouter, TaskTypefrom notifications import NotificationManagerfrom state_manager import StateManager, ResumableTask, ProjectStatus@dataclassclass AgentConfig:    project_id: str    description: str    auto_resume: bool = True    notification_channels: list = None    daily_budget: float = 10.0    max_retries: int = 3class ManusAgent:    """    Advanced autonomous agent with:    - Intelligent AI model selection    - Multi-channel notifications    - Resumable project execution    - Cost optimization    """        def __init__(self, config: AgentConfig):        self.config = config        self.router = ModelRouter()        self.notifier = NotificationManager()        self.state_manager = StateManager()        self.tools = {}  # Registered tools                # Load existing state or create new        self.state = self.state_manager.load_state(config.project_id)        if not self.state:            self.state = self.state_manager.create_project(config.project_id, config.description)        def register_tool(self, name: str, handler: Callable):        """Register a tool for the agent to use"""        self.tools[name] = handler        async def run(self, task_plan: list):        """Execute task plan with resume capability"""                # Notify start        await self.notifier.notify_project_start(            self.config.project_id,            self.config.description        )                try:            for task in task_plan:                task_name = task["name"]                                # Check if already completed                if task_name in self.state.completed_tasks:                    continue                                async with ResumableTask(                    self.state_manager,                    self.config.project_id,                    task_name,                    self.notifier                ) as rt:                                        if rt is None:  # Already completed                        continue                                        # Execute task with appropriate AI model                    result = await self._execute_task(task)                                        # Create checkpoint if specified                    if task.get("checkpoint"):                        user_input = await rt.checkpoint(                            task.get("checkpoint_desc", "Checkpoint reached"),                            task.get("input_prompt")                        )                        # Use user input for next steps                        if user_input:                            task["context"]["user_input"] = user_input                        # Mark complete            self.state.status = ProjectStatus.COMPLETED            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                        await self.notifier.notify_completion(                self.config.project_id,                f"Completed {len(self.state.completed_tasks)} tasks"            )                    except Exception as e:            await self.notifier.notify_error(                self.config.project_id,                str(e),                critical=True            )            raise        async def _execute_task(self, task: Dict) -> Any:        """Execute single task with AI assistance"""        task_type = TaskType(task.get("type", "analysis"))                # Generate prompt from task        prompt = self._build_prompt(task)                # Get AI response with fallback        response = await self.router.generate_with_fallback(            prompt,            task_type,            max_retries=self.config.max_retries        )                # Execute any tool calls        if "tool" in task and task["tool"] in self.tools:            tool_result = await self.tools[task["tool"]](response["content"])            return {"ai_response": response, "tool_result": tool_result}                return response        def _build_prompt(self, task: Dict) -> str:        """Build optimized prompt for task"""        base_prompt = f"""Task: {task['name']}Description: {task.get('description', '')}Context: {task.get('context', {})}Requirements:{chr(10).join(f'- {req}' for req in task.get('requirements', []))}Provide a detailed response suitable for automated processing."""        return base_prompt        async def pause_and_wait(self, reason: str, prompt: str) -> str:        """Pause execution and wait for user input"""        cp = self.state_manager.create_checkpoint(            self.config.project_id,            reason,            requires_input=True,            input_prompt=prompt        )                await self.notifier.notify_checkpoint(            self.config.project_id,            f"{reason}\n\nRequired input: {prompt}"        )                # Poll for resolution        while True:            await asyncio.sleep(2)            pending = self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(self.config.project_id)            for p in pending:                if p.id == cp.id and p.resolved:                    return p.user_response        def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Get current project status"""        return {            "project_id": self.config.project_id,            "status": self.state.status.value,            "progress": len(self.state.completed_tasks),            "current_task": self.state.current_task,            "pending_checkpoints": len(                self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(self.config.project_id)            ),            "cost_stats": self.router.cost_tracker.get_stats()        }# Usage Exampleasync def main():    config = AgentConfig(        project_id="web_scraper_001",        description="Build automated web scraper with validation",        daily_budget=5.0    )        agent = ManusAgent(config)        task_plan = [        {            "name": "analyze_requirements",            "type": "analysis",            "description": "Analyze scraping requirements",            "requirements": ["Identify target sites", "Determine data structure"]        },        {            "name": "design_architecture",            "type": "architecture",            "description": "Design scraper architecture",            "checkpoint": True,            "checkpoint_desc": "Architecture design complete",            "input_prompt": "Please review the proposed architecture. Approve? (yes/modify/cancel)"        },        {            "name": "implement_scraper",            "type": "code_generation",            "description": "Implement the scraper code",            "tool": "code_writer"        }    ]        await agent.run(task_plan)    print(agent.get_status())if __name__ == "__main__":    asyncio.run(main())
5. CLI Interface (cli.py)
Command line interface για διαχείριση:
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""Manus-Win11 CLI - Command line interface for agent management"""import clickimport asynciofrom rich.console import Consolefrom rich.table import Tablefrom rich.panel import Panelfrom agent_core_v2 import ManusAgent, AgentConfigfrom state_manager import StateManager, ProjectStatusconsole = Console()@click.group()def cli():    """Manus-Win11 Agent Framework CLI"""    pass@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.argument("description")@click.option("--budget", default=10.0, help="Daily AI budget")def create(project_id: str, description: str, budget: float):    """Create new project"""    config = AgentConfig(        project_id=project_id,        description=description,        daily_budget=budget    )    agent = ManusAgent(config)    console.print(Panel(f"Created project: {project_id}", style="green"))@cli.command()def list():    """List all projects"""    sm = StateManager()    projects = sm.list_projects()        table = Table(title="Active Projects")    table.add_column("Project ID", style="cyan")    table.add_column("Status", style="magenta")    table.add_column("Last Updated", style="green")        for proj in projects:        state = sm.load_state(proj["project_id"])        table.add_row(            proj["project_id"],            state.status.value if state else "unknown",            str(proj["updated_at"])        )        console.print(table)@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")def status(project_id: str):    """Check project status"""    config = AgentConfig(project_id=project_id, description="")    agent = ManusAgent(config)    stats = agent.get_status()        console.print(Panel.fit(        f"Status: {stats['status']}\n"        f"Progress: {stats['progress']} tasks completed\n"        f"Current: {stats['current_task'] or 'None'}\n"        f"Pending Checkpoints: {stats['pending_checkpoints']}\n"        f"Cost Today: ${stats['cost_stats']['today']:.4f}",        title=f"Project: {project_id}"    ))@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.argument("checkpoint_id")@click.argument("response")def resolve(project_id: str, checkpoint_id: str, response: str):    """Resolve a pending checkpoint"""    sm = StateManager()    if sm.resolve_checkpoint(project_id, checkpoint_id, response):        console.print(f"[green]Checkpoint {checkpoint_id} resolved[/green]")    else:        console.print(f"[red]Failed to resolve checkpoint[/red]")@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")def resume(project_id: str):    """Resume a paused project"""    # Implementation would reload state and continue execution    console.print(f"[yellow]Resuming {project_id}...[/yellow]")if __name__ == "__main__":    cli()

Θέλεις να προσθέσω κάποιο συγκεκριμένο κομμάτι ή να εξηγήσω περισσότερο κάποια λειτουργία;
User:
Ενημέρωσε τα αρχεία με τις λειτουργίες του κώδικα και οδηγίες χρήσης
Kimi:
Θα ενημερώσω όλα τα αρχεία με πλήρη documentation, docstrings, και οδηγίες χρήσης. Δημιουργώ επίσης ένα ολοκληρωμένο README και examples.
1. AI Router (ai_router.py) - Πλήρως Ενημερωμένο
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""ai_router.py - Intelligent AI Model Selection & Cost OptimizationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Επιλογή βέλτιστου AI μοντέλου ανάλογα με τον τύπο εργασίας2. Αυτόματο fallback σε εναλλακτικά μοντέλα σε περίπτωση αποτυχίας3. Caching αποκρίσεων για μείωση κόστους4. Παρακολούθηση κόστους και προϋπολογισμού5. Υποστήριξη πολλαπλών providers (Kimi, DeepSeek, Anthropic, OpenAI)Υποστηριζόμενα Μοντέλα:------------------------ Kimi K2.5: Καλύτερο για code generation, architecture, analysis- DeepSeek V3: Οικονομικό για code generation και debugging  - DeepSeek R1: Reasoning model για complex analysis- Claude 3.5 Sonnet: Code review, creative tasks, documentation- GPT-4o Mini: Fast, φθηνό για chat και simple tasksΟδηγίες Χρήσης:---------------1. Βασική Χρήση:    router = ModelRouter()    result = await router.generate_with_fallback(        prompt="Write a Python function...",        task_type=TaskType.CODE_GENERATION    )    print(result["content"])2. Με Budget Constraint:    model_id = router.select_model(        task_type=TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,        budget_constraint=0.005  # max $0.005 per 1k tokens    )3. Παρακολούθηση Κόστους:    stats = router.cost_tracker.get_stats()    print(f"Σημερινό κόστος: ${stats['today']}")4. Καθαρισμός Cache:    # Αυτόματο TTL 24 ωρών, ή χειροκίνητα:    router.response_cache.clear_old_entries()Περιβαλλοντικές Μεταβλητές:---------------------------- KIMI_API_KEY: API key για Moonshot AI- DEEPSEEK_API_KEY: API key για DeepSeek- ANTHROPIC_API_KEY: API key για Anthropic- OPENAI_API_KEY: API key για OpenAI- DAILY_AI_BUDGET: Ημερήσιο όριο δαπανών (default: $10)Παραδείγματα:------------->>> router = ModelRouter(cache_dir="./my_cache")>>> # Task με caching>>> result = await router.generate_with_fallback(...     prompt="Explain Python decorators",...     task_type=TaskType.DOCUMENTATION... )>>> # Δεύτερο ίδιο request - επιστρέφει από cache>>> result2 = await router.generate_with_fallback(...     prompt="Explain Python decorators", ...     task_type=TaskType.DOCUMENTATION... )  # Σχεδόν instantaneous, κόστος 0Dependencies:-------------- aiohttp: για async HTTP requests- python-dotenv: για environment variables (προαιρετικά)"""import osimport jsonimport hashlibimport timeimport asynciofrom enum import Enumfrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List, Unionfrom pathlib import Pathfrom datetime import datetime, timedeltaimport aiohttpimport logging# Setup logginglogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class TaskType(Enum):    """Τύποι εργασιών για routing"""    CODE_GENERATION = "code_generation"    # Παραγωγή κώδικα    CODE_REVIEW = "code_review"            # Αξιολόγηση κώδικα    DEBUGGING = "debugging"                # Debugging    ARCHITECTURE = "architecture"          # Σχεδιασμός αρχιτεκτονικής    DOCUMENTATION = "documentation"        # Τεκμηρίωση    ANALYSIS = "analysis"                  # Ανάλυση δεδομένων/κώδικα    CREATIVE = "creative"                  # Δημιουργικά tasks    CHAT = "chat"                          # Απλή συνομιλίαclass ModelTier(Enum):    """Επίπεδα μοντέλων ανά κόστος/δυνατότητες"""    PREMIUM = "premium"      # Υψηλότερο κόστος, καλύτερη ποιότητα    STANDARD = "standard"    # Ισορροπία κόστους/ποιότητας    FAST = "fast"            # Χαμηλό κόστος, γρήγορο    LOCAL = "local"          # Τοπικά μοντέλα (δεν υλοποιείται ακόμα)@dataclassclass ModelConfig:    """Ρύθμιση μοντέλου AI"""    name: str                           # Εμφανιζόμενο όνομα    provider: str                       # Πάροχος (moonshot, deepseek, κλπ)    cost_per_1k_tokens: float          # Κόστος ανά 1000 tokens    context_window: int                # Μέγιστο context σε tokens    strengths: List[TaskType]          # Δυνατά σημεία    tier: ModelTier                    # Επίπεδο    api_key_env: str                   # Environment variable για API key    max_retries: int = 3               # Μέγιστες προσπάθειες    timeout: int = 60                  # Timeout σε δευτερόλεπτα        def estimate_cost(self, input_tokens: int, output_tokens: int) -> float:        """Υπολογισμός εκτιμώμενου κόστους"""        return (input_tokens + output_tokens) * self.cost_per_1k_tokens / 1000        def get_api_key(self) -> Optional[str]:        """Ανάκτηση API key από environment"""        return os.getenv(self.api_key_env)class ModelRouter:    """    Κεντρικός router για επιλογή και χρήση AI μοντέλων.        Features:    - Smart routing βάσει task type και complexity    - Automatic fallback chain    - Response caching με TTL    - Cost tracking και budget enforcement    - Async/await support για όλες τις operations        Usage:        router = ModelRouter(cache_dir="./cache", daily_budget=20.0)                # Απλή χρήση        response = await router.generate_with_fallback(            prompt="Write a Python class",            task_type=TaskType.CODE_GENERATION        )                # Με συγκεκριμένο μοντέλο        response = await router.call_model(            model_id="deepseek-chat",            prompt="Explain recursion",            temperature=0.7        )    """        # Διαθέσιμα μοντέλα με τις ρυθμίσεις τους    MODELS: Dict[str, ModelConfig] = {        "kimi-k2.5": ModelConfig(            name="Kimi K2.5",            provider="moonshot",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.015,            context_window=256000,            strengths=[                TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,                 TaskType.ARCHITECTURE,                TaskType.CODE_REVIEW,                 TaskType.ANALYSIS            ],            tier=ModelTier.PREMIUM,            api_key_env="KIMI_API_KEY",            max_retries=3        ),        "deepseek-chat": ModelConfig(            name="DeepSeek V3",            provider="deepseek",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.002,            context_window=64000,            strengths=[                TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,                 TaskType.DEBUGGING,                TaskType.ANALYSIS,                TaskType.CHAT            ],            tier=ModelTier.STANDARD,            api_key_env="DEEPSEEK_API_KEY"        ),        "deepseek-reasoner": ModelConfig(            name="DeepSeek R1",            provider="deepseek",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.003,            context_window=64000,            strengths=[                TaskType.DEBUGGING,                 TaskType.ARCHITECTURE,                TaskType.ANALYSIS            ],            tier=ModelTier.PREMIUM,            api_key_env="DEEPSEEK_API_KEY"        ),        "claude-3-5-sonnet": ModelConfig(            name="Claude 3.5 Sonnet",            provider="anthropic",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.003,            context_window=200000,            strengths=[                TaskType.CODE_REVIEW,                 TaskType.CREATIVE,                TaskType.DOCUMENTATION            ],            tier=ModelTier.PREMIUM,            api_key_env="ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"        ),        "gpt-4o-mini": ModelConfig(            name="GPT-4o Mini",            provider="openai",            cost_per_1k_tokens=0.00015,            context_window=128000,            strengths=[                TaskType.CHAT,                 TaskType.DOCUMENTATION,                TaskType.ANALYSIS            ],            tier=ModelTier.FAST,            api_key_env="OPENAI_API_KEY"        )    }        # Default fallback chain ανάλογα με το task    DEFAULT_FALLBACK_CHAINS: Dict[TaskType, List[str]] = {        TaskType.CODE_GENERATION: ["kimi-k2.5", "deepseek-chat", "claude-3-5-sonnet"],        TaskType.DEBUGGING: ["deepseek-reasoner", "kimi-k2.5", "deepseek-chat"],        TaskType.ARCHITECTURE: ["kimi-k2.5", "deepseek-reasoner", "claude-3-5-sonnet"],        TaskType.CODE_REVIEW: ["claude-3-5-sonnet", "kimi-k2.5", "deepseek-chat"],        TaskType.DOCUMENTATION: ["claude-3-5-sonnet", "gpt-4o-mini", "kimi-k2.5"],        TaskType.ANALYSIS: ["deepseek-reasoner", "kimi-k2.5", "deepseek-chat"],        TaskType.CREATIVE: ["claude-3-5-sonnet", "kimi-k2.5"],        TaskType.CHAT: ["gpt-4o-mini", "deepseek-chat"]    }        def __init__(self,                  cache_dir: str = "./cache",                 daily_budget: Optional[float] = None,                 default_temperature: float = 0.7):        """        Αρχικοποίηση router.                Args:            cache_dir: Directory για caching αποκρίσεων            daily_budget: Ημερήσιο όριο δαπανών (default από env DAILY_AI_BUDGET)            default_temperature: Default temperature για generation        """        self.cache_dir = Path(cache_dir)        self.cache_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                self.daily_budget = daily_budget or float(            os.getenv("DAILY_AI_BUDGET", "10.0")        )        self.default_temperature = default_temperature                self.cost_tracker = CostTracker(daily_budget=self.daily_budget)        self.response_cache = ResponseCache(cache_dir)                logger.info(f"ModelRouter initialized with budget: ${self.daily_budget}/day")        def select_model(self,                     task_type: TaskType,                    complexity: str = "medium",                    budget_constraint: Optional[float] = None,                    preferred_provider: Optional[str] = None) -> str:        """        Επιλογή βέλτιστου μοντέλου για task.                Args:            task_type: Τύπος εργασίας            complexity: low/medium/high - επηρεάζει επιλογή            budget_constraint: Μέγιστο κόστος ανά 1k tokens            preferred_provider: Προτίμηση σε συγκεκριμένο provider                Returns:            model_id: ID του επιλεγμένου μοντέλου                    Example:            >>> router = ModelRouter()            >>> model = router.select_model(            ...     TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,            ...     complexity="high",            ...     budget_constraint=0.01            ... )            >>> print(model)  # 'deepseek-chat' ή 'kimi-k2.5' αν επιτρέπεται budget        """        candidates = []                for model_id, config in self.MODELS.items():            # Φιλτράρισμα βάσει task type            if task_type not in config.strengths:                continue                        # Φιλτράρισμα βάσει provider preference            if preferred_provider and config.provider != preferred_provider:                continue                        # Υπολογισμός score            score = self._calculate_score(config, complexity, task_type)            candidates.append((model_id, config, score))                # Ταξινόμηση βάσει score        candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[2], reverse=True)                # Εφαρμογή budget constraint        if budget_constraint:            candidates = [                (m, c, s) for m, c, s in candidates                 if c.cost_per_1k_tokens <= budget_constraint            ]                if not candidates:            logger.warning(f"No suitable model found for {task_type}, using default")            return "kimi-k2.5"                selected = candidates[0][0]        logger.info(f"Selected model {selected} for {task_type.value}")        return selected        def _calculate_score(self,                         config: ModelConfig,                         complexity: str,                        task_type: TaskType) -> float:        """        Υπολογισμός suitability score για μοντέλο.                Παράγοντες:        - Complexity match (high complexity -> bigger context)        - Task strength match        - Cost efficiency        - Context window adequacy        """        # Base complexity multipliers        complexity_weights = {            "low": 1.0,            "medium": 1.5,            "high": 2.5        }                base_score = complexity_weights.get(complexity, 1.0)                # Context window fitness (0.5 - 2.0)        # Υψηλότερο score για μεγαλύτερα context σε complex tasks        context_score = min(config.context_window / 50000, 2.0)        if complexity == "high":            context_score *= 1.5                # Cost efficiency (inverse, normalized)        # Προτιμούμε φθηνότερα μοντέλα για απλά tasks        cost_score = 1.0 / (config.cost_per_1k_tokens * 50 + 0.5)        if complexity == "high":            cost_score *= 0.8  # Λιγότερο σημαντικό για complex tasks                # Strength match bonus        strength_bonus = 1.5 if task_type in config.strengths else 1.0                final_score = base_score * context_score * cost_score * strength_bonus        return final_score        async def generate_with_fallback(self,                                   prompt: str,                                   task_type: TaskType,                                   complexity: str = "medium",                                   temperature: Optional[float] = None,                                   max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,                                   system_prompt: Optional[str] = None,                                   use_cache: bool = True,                                   max_retries: int = 3) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """        Generation με automatic fallback και caching.                Αυτή είναι η κύρια μέθοδος χρήσης. Προσπαθεί το καλύτερο μοντέλο,        και αν αποτύχει συνεχίζει με το επόμενο στη fallback chain.                Args:            prompt: Το κύριο prompt            task_type: Τύπος εργασίας για επιλογή μοντέλου            complexity: low/medium/high            temperature: Creativity (0.0-1.0)            max_tokens: Μέγιστο μήκος απόκρισης            system_prompt: System prompt αν υποστηρίζεται            use_cache: Να χρησιμοποιηθεί caching            max_retries: Προσπάθειες ανά μοντέλο                Returns:            Dict με:            - content: Το κείμενο απόκρισης            - model: Ποιο μοντέλο χρησιμοποιήθηκε            - cost: Κόστος σε $            - tokens: Dict με input/output tokens            - cached: Boolean αν ήταν cached            - latency: Χρόνος απόκρισης σε ms                    Raises:            Exception: Αν αποτύχουν όλα τα μοντέλα                Example:            >>> result = await router.generate_with_fallback(            ...     prompt="Write a Python decorator",            ...     task_type=TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,            ...     system_prompt="You are a Python expert"            ... )            >>> print(result["content"])            >>> print(f"Cost: ${result['cost']:.4f}")        """        # Έλεγχος cache        if use_cache:            cache_key = self._generate_cache_key(prompt, task_type, system_prompt)            cached = await self.response_cache.get(cache_key)            if cached:                logger.info("Cache hit, returning cached response")                return {                    "content": cached["content"],                    "model": "cache",                    "cost": 0.0,                    "tokens": {"input": 0, "output": 0},                    "cached": True,                    "latency": 0                }                # Έλεγχος budget        if self.cost_tracker.is_budget_exceeded():            raise Exception(f"Daily budget ${self.daily_budget} exceeded")                # Επιλογή fallback chain        fallback_chain = self.DEFAULT_FALLBACK_CHAINS.get(            task_type,             ["kimi-k2.5", "deepseek-chat"]        )                errors = []        start_time = time.time()                for model_id in fallback_chain:            try:                config = self.MODELS[model_id]                                # Έλεγχος API key                if not config.get_api_key():                    logger.warning(f"No API key for {model_id}, skipping")                    continue                                # Κλήση μοντέλου                result = await self._call_model_api(                    config=config,                    model_id=model_id,                    prompt=prompt,                    temperature=temperature or self.default_temperature,                    max_tokens=max_tokens,                    system_prompt=system_prompt                )                                # Επιτυχία - caching και logging                if use_cache:                    await self.response_cache.set(cache_key, {                        "content": result["content"],                        "timestamp": time.time()                    })                                latency = int((time.time() - start_time) * 1000)                                self.cost_tracker.log_usage(                    model_id=model_id,                    input_tokens=result["tokens"]["input"],                    output_tokens=result["tokens"]["output"],                    cost=result["cost"]                )                                logger.info(f"Success with {model_id}, cost: ${result['cost']:.4f}")                                return {                    "content": result["content"],                    "model": model_id,                    "cost": result["cost"],                    "tokens": result["tokens"],                    "cached": False,                    "latency": latency                }                            except Exception as e:                error_msg = f"{model_id}: {str(e)}"                logger.error(error_msg)                errors.append(error_msg)                continue                # Όλα απέτυχαν        raise Exception(f"All models failed: {'; '.join(errors)}")        async def call_model(self,                        model_id: str,                        prompt: str,                        temperature: float = 0.7,                        max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,                        system_prompt: Optional[str] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """        Απευθείας κλήση συγκεκριμένου μοντέλου.                Χρήσιμο όταν θέλουμε συγκεκριμένο μοντέλο χωρίς fallback.        """        if model_id not in self.MODELS:            raise ValueError(f"Unknown model: {model_id}")                config = self.MODELS[model_id]                if not config.get_api_key():            raise Exception(f"No API key for {model_id}")                return await self._call_model_api(            config, model_id, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt        )        async def _call_model_api(self,                             config: ModelConfig,                             model_id: str,                             prompt: str,                             temperature: float,                             max_tokens: Optional[int],                             system_prompt: Optional[str]) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """        Εσωτερική μέθοδος κλήσης API.                Υλοποίηση για κάθε provider ξεχωριστά.        """        provider = config.provider                if provider == "moonshot":            return await self._call_moonshot(                config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt            )        elif provider == "deepseek":            return await self._call_deepseek(                config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt            )        elif provider == "anthropic":            return await self._call_anthropic(                config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt            )        elif provider == "openai":            return await self._call_openai(                config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt            )        else:            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported provider: {provider}")        async def _call_moonshot(self, config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt):        """Κλήση Moonshot API (Kimi)"""        api_key = config.get_api_key()        headers = {            "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",            "Content-Type": "application/json"        }                messages = []        if system_prompt:            messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system_prompt})        messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})                payload = {            "model": "kimi-k2.5",            "messages": messages,            "temperature": temperature,            "max_tokens": max_tokens or 4096        }                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            async with session.post(                "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions",                headers=headers,                json=payload,                timeout=config.timeout            ) as resp:                if resp.status != 200:                    error = await resp.text()                    raise Exception(f"Moonshot API error: {error}")                                data = await resp.json()                content = data["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]                usage = data["usage"]                                cost = config.estimate_cost(                    usage["prompt_tokens"],                    usage["completion_tokens"]                )                                return {                    "content": content,                    "tokens": {                        "input": usage["prompt_tokens"],                        "output": usage["completion_tokens"]                    },                    "cost": cost                }        async def _call_deepseek(self, config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt):        """Κλήση DeepSeek API"""        api_key = config.get_api_key()        headers = {            "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",            "Content-Type": "application/json"        }                messages = []        if system_prompt:            messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system_prompt})        messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})                # Map model_id to actual DeepSeek model name        model_name = "deepseek-chat" if "chat" in config.name.lower() else "deepseek-reasoner"                payload = {            "model": model_name,            "messages": messages,            "temperature": temperature,            "max_tokens": max_tokens or 4096        }                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            async with session.post(                "https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions",                headers=headers,                json=payload,                timeout=config.timeout            ) as resp:                if resp.status != 200:                    error = await resp.text()                    raise Exception(f"DeepSeek API error: {error}")                                data = await resp.json()                content = data["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]                usage = data["usage"]                                cost = config.estimate_cost(                    usage["prompt_tokens"],                    usage["completion_tokens"]                )                                return {                    "content": content,                    "tokens": {                        "input": usage["prompt_tokens"],                        "output": usage["completion_tokens"]                    },                    "cost": cost                }        async def _call_anthropic(self, config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt):        """Κλήση Anthropic API (Claude)"""        api_key = config.get_api_key()        headers = {            "x-api-key": api_key,            "Content-Type": "application/json",            "anthropic-version": "2023-06-01"        }                payload = {            "model": "claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022",            "max_tokens": max_tokens or 4096,            "temperature": temperature,            "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]        }                if system_prompt:            payload["system"] = system_prompt                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            async with session.post(                "https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",                headers=headers,                json=payload,                timeout=config.timeout            ) as resp:                if resp.status != 200:                    error = await resp.text()                    raise Exception(f"Anthropic API error: {error}")                                data = await resp.json()                content = data["content"][0]["text"]                                cost = config.estimate_cost(                    data["usage"]["input_tokens"],                    data["usage"]["output_tokens"]                )                                return {                    "content": content,                    "tokens": {                        "input": data["usage"]["input_tokens"],                        "output": data["usage"]["output_tokens"]                    },                    "cost": cost                }        async def _call_openai(self, config, prompt, temperature, max_tokens, system_prompt):        """Κλήση OpenAI API"""        api_key = config.get_api_key()        headers = {            "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",            "Content-Type": "application/json"        }                messages = []        if system_prompt:            messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system_prompt})        messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})                payload = {            "model": "gpt-4o-mini",            "messages": messages,            "temperature": temperature,            "max_tokens": max_tokens or 4096        }                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            async with session.post(                "https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions",                headers=headers,                json=payload,                timeout=config.timeout            ) as resp:                if resp.status != 200:                    error = await resp.text()                    raise Exception(f"OpenAI API error: {error}")                                data = await resp.json()                content = data["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]                usage = data["usage"]                                cost = config.estimate_cost(                    usage["prompt_tokens"],                    usage["completion_tokens"]                )                                return {                    "content": content,                    "tokens": {                        "input": usage["prompt_tokens"],                        "output": usage["completion_tokens"]                    },                    "cost": cost                }        def _generate_cache_key(self,                            prompt: str,                            task_type: TaskType,                           system_prompt: Optional[str]) -> str:        """Δημιουργία deterministic cache key"""        content = f"{task_type.value}:{system_prompt or ''}:{prompt}"        return hashlib.sha256(content.encode()).hexdigest()[:32]        def get_cost_report(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Αναφορά κόστους και χρήσης"""        return self.cost_tracker.get_detailed_report()class ResponseCache:    """    Semantic caching για LLM αποκρίσεις.        Features:    - TTL-based expiration (default 24h)    - Persistent storage (JSON files)    - Async operations    - Automatic cleanup        Usage:        cache = ResponseCache("./cache")        await cache.set("key", {"content": "response"})        data = await cache.get("key")  # Returns None if expired    """        def __init__(self, cache_dir: Union[str, Path], ttl: int = 86400):        """        Args:            cache_dir: Directory για cache files            ttl: Time-to-live σε δευτερόλεπτα (default 24h)        """        self.cache_dir = Path(cache_dir)        self.cache_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)        self.ttl = ttl        async def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[Dict]:        """        Ανάκτηση από cache αν δεν έχει λήξει.                Args:            key: Cache key                    Returns:            Cached data ή None αν δεν υπάρχει/έχει λήξει        """        cache_file = self.cache_dir / f"{key}.json"                if not cache_file.exists():            return None                try:            data = json.loads(cache_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))                        # Έλεγχος λήξης            if time.time() - data.get("timestamp", 0) > self.ttl:                cache_file.unlink(missing_ok=True)                return None                        return data                    except (json.JSONDecodeError, IOError):            cache_file.unlink(missing_ok=True)            return None        async def set(self, key: str, data: Dict):        """        Αποθήκευση στο cache.                Args:            key: Cache key            data: Data να αποθηκευτούν (πρέπει να είναι JSON serializable)        """        cache_file = self.cache_dir / f"{key}.json"                entry = {            "timestamp": time.time(),            **data        }                try:            cache_file.write_text(                json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False),                encoding='utf-8'            )        except IOError as e:            logger.error(f"Cache write error: {e}")        async def clear_expired(self):        """Καθαρισμός ληγμένων entries"""        count = 0        for cache_file in self.cache_dir.glob("*.json"):            try:                data = json.loads(cache_file.read_text())                if time.time() - data.get("timestamp", 0) > self.ttl:                    cache_file.unlink()                    count += 1            except Exception:                continue        logger.info(f"Cleared {count} expired cache entries")        async def clear_all(self):        """Πλήρης καθαρισμός cache"""        for cache_file in self.cache_dir.glob("*.json"):            cache_file.unlink(missing_ok=True)        logger.info("Cache cleared completely")class CostTracker:    """    Παρακολούθηση κόστους AI API calls.        Features:    - Ημερήσιο budget tracking    - Analytics ανά μοντέλο    - Persistent logging    - Alerts για υπέρβαση budget        Usage:        tracker = CostTracker(daily_budget=20.0)        tracker.log_usage("kimi-k2.5", 1000, 500, 0.0225)                if tracker.is_budget_exceeded():            print("Budget exceeded!")                stats = tracker.get_detailed_report()    """        def __init__(self,                  daily_budget: float = 10.0,                 log_file: str = "ai_costs.jsonl"):        """        Args:            daily_budget: Ημερήσιο όριο σε $            log_file: Αρχείο για logging χρήσης        """        self.daily_budget = daily_budget        self.log_file = Path(log_file)        self._today_usage = 0.0        self._last_reset = datetime.now().date()                # Φόρτωση σημερινής χρήσης από log        self._load_today_usage()        def _load_today_usage(self):        """Φόρτωση σημερινής χρήσης από log file"""        if not self.log_file.exists():            return                today = datetime.now().date().isoformat()        total = 0.0                try:            with open(self.log_file, 'r') as f:                for line in f:                    try:                        entry = json.loads(line.strip())                        if entry.get("date") == today:                            total += entry.get("cost", 0)                    except json.JSONDecodeError:                        continue            self._today_usage = total        except IOError:            pass        def log_usage(self,                   model: str,                   input_tokens: int,                   output_tokens: int,                  cost: float):        """        Καταγραφή χρήσης.                Args:            model: ID μοντέλου            input_tokens: Αριθμός input tokens            output_tokens: Αριθμός output tokens              cost: Κόστος σε $        """        # Έλεγχος αν άλλαξε μέρα        current_date = datetime.now().date()        if current_date != self._last_reset:            self._today_usage = 0.0            self._last_reset = current_date                self._today_usage += cost                entry = {            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),            "date": current_date.isoformat(),            "model": model,            "input_tokens": input_tokens,            "output_tokens": output_tokens,            "cost": cost,            "total_today": self._today_usage        }                # Append to log        with open(self.log_file, 'a') as f:            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\n')                # Alert αν πλησιάζουμε όριο        if self._today_usage > self.daily_budget * 0.9:            logger.warning(                f"BUDGET ALERT: ${self._today_usage:.2f} / ${self.daily_budget:.2f}"            )        def is_budget_exceeded(self) -> bool:        """Έλεγχος αν έχει υπερβεί το ημερήσιο όριο"""        return self._today_usage >= self.daily_budget        def get_stats(self) -> Dict[str, float]:        """Βασικά στατιστικά"""        return {            "today": self._today_usage,            "budget": self.daily_budget,            "remaining": max(0, self.daily_budget - self._today_usage),            "percentage": (self._today_usage / self.daily_budget * 100) if self.daily_budget > 0 else 0        }        def get_detailed_report(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Αναλυτική αναφορά"""        if not self.log_file.exists():            return {"error": "No log file found"}                total_cost = 0.0        by_model = {}        by_day = {}                with open(self.log_file, 'r') as f:            for line in f:                try:                    entry = json.loads(line.strip())                    cost = entry.get("cost", 0)                    model = entry.get("model", "unknown")                    date = entry.get("date", "unknown")                                        total_cost += cost                    by_model[model] = by_model.get(model, 0) + cost                    by_day[date] = by_day.get(date, 0) + cost                                    except json.JSONDecodeError:                    continue                return {            "total_all_time": total_cost,            "today": self._today_usage,            "budget": self.daily_budget,            "by_model": by_model,            "by_day": by_day,            "projected_monthly": self._today_usage * 30        }# Παραδείγματα Χρήσης (για testing)async def example_usage():    """Παράδειγμα πλήρους χρήσης του router"""        print("=" * 60)    print("AI Router - Παράδειγμα Χρήσης")    print("=" * 60)        # Αρχικοποίηση    router = ModelRouter(        cache_dir="./example_cache",        daily_budget=5.0    )        # 1. Απλό generation με auto-selection    print("\n1. Code Generation (Auto-select):")    try:        result = await router.generate_with_fallback(            prompt="Write a Python function to calculate fibonacci numbers",            task_type=TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,            complexity="medium"        )        print(f"  Model: {result['model']}")        print(f"  Cost: ${result['cost']:.4f}")        print(f"  Latency: {result['latency']}ms")        print(f"  Preview: {result['content'][:100]}...")    except Exception as e:        print(f"  Error: {e}")        # 2. Με budget constraint    print("\n2. Budget-Constrained Selection:")    cheap_model = router.select_model(        TaskType.CHAT,        budget_constraint=0.001  # Φθηνότερο από 0.001/1k tokens    )    print(f"  Selected for low budget: {cheap_model}")        # 3. Cost report    print("\n3. Cost Report:")    report = router.get_cost_report()    print(f"  Today: ${report['today']:.4f}")    print(f"  Budget: ${report['budget']:.2f}")    print(f"  By Model: {report.get('by_model', {})}")        # 4. Caching demonstration    print("\n4. Caching (2nd identical request):")    start = time.time()    result2 = await router.generate_with_fallback(        prompt="Write a Python function to calculate fibonacci numbers",        task_type=TaskType.CODE_GENERATION    )    elapsed = (time.time() - start) * 1000    print(f"  Cached: {result2['cached']}")    print(f"  Time: {elapsed:.2f}ms (should be ~0 if cached)")    print(f"  Cost: ${result2['cost']:.4f} (should be 0 if cached)")if __name__ == "__main__":    # Run examples    asyncio.run(example_usage())
2. Notification System (notifications.py) - Πλήρως Ενημερωμένο
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""notifications.py - Multi-Channel Notification SystemΛειτουργίες:------------1. Αποστολή ειδοποιήσεων μέσω Telegram Bot2. Αποστολή ειδοποιήσεων μέσω Slack Webhooks3. Local logging όλων των notifications4. Διαφορετικά επίπεδα προτεραιότητας (INFO, SUCCESS, WARNING, ERROR, CRITICAL)5. Rich formatting με emojis και metadata6. Async/await support για μη-blocking αποστολήΥποστηριζόμενα Channels:------------------------- Telegram: Rich messages με Markdown, silent mode για low priority- Slack: Attachments με colors, timestamps, footers- File Log: Persistent JSON logging για audit trailΕπίπεδα Ειδοποίησης:-------------------- INFO: Γενικές πληροφορίες (silent σε Telegram)- SUCCESS: Επιτυχής ολοκλήρωση- WARNING: Προειδοποίηση, χρειάζεται προσοχή- ERROR: Σφάλμα, αποτυχία operation- CRITICAL: Κρίσιμο σφάλμα, απαιτείται άμεση παρέμβασηΟδηγίες Χρήσης:---------------1. Βασική Αρχικοποίηση:    notifier = NotificationManager()    # Αυτόματα φορτώνει tokens από environment2. Αποστολή Απλής Ειδοποίησης:    await notifier.notify(Notification(        title="Task Complete",        message="The analysis finished successfully",        level=NotificationLevel.SUCCESS    ))3. Project-Specific Notifications:    await notifier.notify_project_start("proj_001", "Data processing")    await notifier.notify_checkpoint("proj_001", "Review required")    await notifier.notify_completion("proj_001", "All tasks done")    await notifier.notify_error("proj_001", "Connection failed", critical=True)4. Έλεγχος Configuration:    if not notifier.channels:        print("No notification channels configured!")Περιβαλλοντικές Μεταβλητές:---------------------------- TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN: Token από @BotFather- TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID: Chat ID για αποστολή (μπορεί να είναι group)- SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL: Incoming Webhook URL από Slack AppsTelegram Setup:---------------1. Πήγαινε στο @BotFather στο Telegram2. Δημιούργησε νέο bot: /newbot3. Πάρε το token (μοιάζει με 123456:ABC-DEF1234ghIkl-zyx57W2v1u123ew11)4. Για chat ID:   - Στείλε μήνυμα στο bot   - Πήγαινε στο https://api.telegram.org/bot<token>/getUpdates   - Βρες το "chat":{"id":123456789}Slack Setup:------------1. Πήγαινε στο https://api.slack.com/apps2. Create New App → From scratch3. Ενεργοποίηση Incoming Webhooks4. Add New Webhook to Workspace5. Επίλεξε channel και αντιγραφή URLΠαραδείγματα:------------->>> notifier = NotificationManager()>>> >>> # Ειδοποίηση έναρξης>>> await notifier.notify_project_start(...     project_id="web_scraper_v2",...     description="E-commerce price monitoring"... )>>> >>> # Ειδοποίηση σφάλματος>>> try:...     risky_operation()... except Exception as e:...     await notifier.notify_error(...         project_id="web_scraper_v2",...         error=str(e),...         critical=True  # Θα στείλει και ήχο...     )Dependencies:-------------- aiohttp: για async HTTP requests- python-dotenv: προαιρετικά για env vars"""import osimport jsonimport asyncioimport aiohttpfrom enum import Enum, autofrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any, Unionfrom datetime import datetimefrom pathlib import Pathimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class NotificationLevel(Enum):    """    Επίπεδα σοβαρότητας ειδοποιήσεων.        Καθορίζουν:    - Visual styling (colors, emojis)    - Sound notifications (για critical)    - Silent mode (για info σε Telegram)    """    INFO = ("info", "ℹ️", "#36a64f", False)      # (name, emoji, color, sound)    SUCCESS = ("success", "✅", "#28a745", False)    WARNING = ("warning", "⚠️", "#ffc107", True)    ERROR = ("error", "❌", "#dc3545", True)    CRITICAL = ("critical", "🚨", "#721c24", True)        def __init__(self, label, emoji, color, alert):        self.label = label        self.emoji = emoji        self.color = color  # Hex color για Slack        self.alert = alert  # True = play sound/notification@dataclassclass Notification:    """    Data class για ειδοποίηση.        Attributes:        title: Τίτλος ειδοποίησης        message: Κύριο μήνυμα (μπορεί να περιέχει newlines)        level: Επίπεδο σοβαρότητας        timestamp: Χρόνος δημιουργίας        project_id: Συσχέτιση με project (προαιρετικό)        metadata: Επιπλέον δεδομένα (dict, προαιρετικό)        actions: Λίστα από actionable buttons (για μελλοντική χρήση)    """    title: str    message: str    level: NotificationLevel    timestamp: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)    project_id: Optional[str] = None    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None    actions: List[Dict[str, str]] = field(default_factory=list)class NotificationChannel:    """Abstract base class για notification channels"""        async def send(self, notification: Notification):        raise NotImplementedError        def is_configured(self) -> bool:        raise NotImplementedErrorclass NotificationManager:    """    Κεντρικός manager για multi-channel notifications.        Αυτόματα ανακαλύπτει και ρυθμίζει διαθέσιμα channels από environment.    Παρέχει high-level methods για common notification patterns.        Usage:        manager = NotificationManager()                # Έλεγχος διαθέσιμων channels        print(f"Active channels: {len(manager.channels)}")                # Αποστολή σε όλα τα channels        await manager.notify(Notification(...))                # Project lifecycle notifications        await manager.notify_project_start("proj1", "Description")        await manager.notify_checkpoint("proj1", "Needs review")        await manager.notify_completion("proj1", "Results summary")        await manager.notify_error("proj1", "Error details", critical=True)    """        def __init__(self):        self.channels: List[NotificationChannel] = []                # Auto-configure channels από environment        self._setup_telegram()        self._setup_slack()        self._setup_log()                logger.info(f"NotificationManager initialized with {len(self.channels)} channels")        def _setup_telegram(self):        """Ρύθμιση Telegram channel αν υπάρχουν credentials"""        token = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN")        chat_id = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID")                if token and chat_id:            self.channels.append(TelegramChannel(token, chat_id))            logger.info("Telegram channel configured")        else:            logger.debug("Telegram not configured (missing env vars)")        def _setup_slack(self):        """Ρύθμιση Slack channel αν υπάρχει webhook"""        webhook = os.getenv("SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL")                if webhook:            self.channels.append(SlackChannel(webhook))            logger.info("Slack channel configured")        else:            logger.debug("Slack not configured (missing env var)")        def _setup_log(self):        """Πάντα προσθέτουμε local logging"""        self.channels.append(LogChannel())        async def notify(self, notification: Notification):        """        Αποστολή ειδοποίησης σε όλα τα configured channels.                Τρέχει parallel σε όλα τα channels με gather.        Αποτυχίες σε ένα channel δεν επηρεάζουν τα άλλα.                Args:            notification: Notification object προς αποστολή        """        if not self.channels:            logger.warning("No notification channels configured!")            return                tasks = [            self._send_to_channel(channel, notification)             for channel in self.channels        ]                results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)                # Log αποτυχίες αλλά μην τα propagare        for i, result in enumerate(results):            if isinstance(result, Exception):                logger.error(f"Channel {i} failed: {result}")        async def _send_to_channel(self,                                channel: NotificationChannel,                                notification: Notification):        """Βοηθητικό για error handling ανά channel"""        try:            await channel.send(notification)        except Exception as e:            logger.error(f"Notification failed for {channel.__class__.__name__}: {e}")            raise        # High-level convenience methods        async def notify_project_start(self, project_id: str, description: str):        """        Ειδοποίηση έναρξης project.
