Args:            project_id: Μοναδικό ID project            description: Περιγραφή του project        """        await self.notify(Notification(            title="🚀 Project Started",            message=f"**{project_id}**\n\n{description}",            level=NotificationLevel.INFO,            project_id=project_id        ))        async def notify_progress(self,                              project_id: str,                              task: str,                              percent: int):        """        Ειδοποίηση προόδου (για μακροχρόνια tasks).                Args:            project_id: ID project            task: Τρέχον task            percent: Ποσοστό ολοκλήρωσης 0-100        """        bar = "█" * (percent // 10) + "░" * (10 - percent // 10)        await self.notify(Notification(            title=f"📊 Progress Update: {percent}%",            message=f"Task: {task}\n[{bar}] {percent}%",            level=NotificationLevel.INFO,            project_id=project_id,            metadata={"percent": percent, "task": task}        ))        async def notify_checkpoint(self,                                project_id: str,                                message: str,                               input_prompt: Optional[str] = None):        """        Ειδοποίηση checkpoint - αναμονή για user input.                Στέλνει WARNING level για να τραβήξει προσοχή.                Args:            project_id: ID project            message: Περιγραφή του checkpoint            input_prompt: Τι περιμένουμε από τον χρήστη        """        full_message = message        if input_prompt:            full_message += f"\n\n**Action Required:**\n{input_prompt}"                await self.notify(Notification(            title="⏸️ Checkpoint Reached",            message=full_message,            level=NotificationLevel.WARNING,            project_id=project_id        ))        async def notify_completion(self,                                project_id: str,                                results: str,                               stats: Optional[Dict] = None):        """        Ειδοποίηση επιτυχούς ολοκλήρωσης.                Args:            project_id: ID project            results: Περίληψη αποτελεσμάτων            stats: Προαιρετικά στατιστικά (duration, cost, κλπ)        """        message = results        if stats:            stats_str = "\n".join(f"• {k}: {v}" for k, v in stats.items())            message += f"\n\n**Statistics:**\n{stats_str}"                await self.notify(Notification(            title="✅ Project Completed",            message=message,            level=NotificationLevel.SUCCESS,            project_id=project_id,            metadata=stats        ))        async def notify_error(self,                           project_id: str,                           error: str,                          critical: bool = False,                          context: Optional[str] = None):        """        Ειδοποίηση σφάλματος.                Args:            project_id: ID project            error: Μήνυμα σφάλματος            critical: Αν True, χρησιμοποιεί CRITICAL level (ήχος)            context: Πρόσθετο context (stack trace, κλπ)        """        message = error        if context:            message += f"\n\n```\n{context[:500]}\n```"  # Truncate long context                await self.notify(Notification(            title="🚨 Critical Error" if critical else "❌ Error Occurred",            message=message,            level=NotificationLevel.CRITICAL if critical else NotificationLevel.ERROR,            project_id=project_id        ))        async def notify_cost_alert(self,                                current: float,                                budget: float,                               project_id: Optional[str] = None):        """        Ειδοποίηση υπέρβασης budget.                Args:            current: Τρέχον κόστος            budget: Όριο budget            project_id: Προαιρετικά ID project        """        percent = (current / budget * 100) if budget > 0 else 0        await self.notify(Notification(            title="💰 Budget Alert",            message=f"Current: ${current:.2f} / ${budget:.2f} ({percent:.1f}%)",            level=NotificationLevel.WARNING if percent < 100 else NotificationLevel.CRITICAL,            project_id=project_id,            metadata={"current": current, "budget": budget, "percent": percent}        ))class TelegramChannel(NotificationChannel):    """    Telegram Bot API implementation.        Features:    - Markdown formatting    - Silent mode για INFO level    - Message length handling (max 4096 chars)    - Error handling για invalid chat IDs        Setup:        1. Δημιούργησε bot μέσω @BotFather        2. Πάρε token        3. Στείλε μήνυμα στο bot        4. Βρες chat ID μέσω getUpdates    """        MAX_LENGTH = 4096  # Telegram limit        def __init__(self, token: str, chat_id: str):        self.token = token        self.chat_id = chat_id        self.base_url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{token}"        def is_configured(self) -> bool:        return bool(self.token and self.chat_id)        async def send(self, notification: Notification):        """        Αποστολή μέσω Telegram Bot API.                Χειρίζεται:        - Markdown escaping        - Message truncation        - Silent notifications για low priority        """        emoji = notification.level.emoji        text = f"{emoji} *{self._escape_markdown(notification.title)}*\n\n"        text += self._escape_markdown(notification.message)                if notification.project_id:            text += f"\n\n`Project: {notification.project_id}`"                # Truncate αν χρειάζεται        if len(text) > self.MAX_LENGTH:            text = text[:self.MAX_LENGTH-20] + "\n\n...(truncated)"                payload = {            "chat_id": self.chat_id,            "text": text,            "parse_mode": "Markdown",            "disable_notification": not notification.level.alert        }                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            url = f"{self.base_url}/sendMessage"            try:                async with session.post(url, json=payload, timeout=30) as resp:                    if resp.status == 403:                        logger.error("Telegram 403: Bot not authorized or wrong chat ID")                    elif resp.status == 400:                        error = await resp.text()                        logger.error(f"Telegram 400: {error}")                    elif resp.status != 200:                        error = await resp.text()                        raise Exception(f"Telegram API error {resp.status}: {error}")                                    except aiohttp.ClientError as e:                raise Exception(f"Telegram connection error: {e}")        def _escape_markdown(self, text: str) -> str:        """        Escape MarkdownV1 special characters.                Τα _ * [ ] ( ) ~ ` > # + - = | { } . ! πρέπει να escape-αρονται        με \ μπροστά.        """        chars = '_*[]()~`>#+-=|{}.!'        for char in chars:            text = text.replace(char, f'\\{char}')        return textclass SlackChannel(NotificationChannel):    """    Slack Incoming Webhooks implementation.        Features:    - Rich attachments με colors    - Timestamps και footers    - Markdown-like formatting (Slack mrkdwn)        Setup:        1. Δημιούργησε App στο api.slack.com        2. Ενεργοποίηση Incoming Webhooks        3. Authorize σε channel        4. Αντιγραφή Webhook URL    """        def __init__(self, webhook_url: str):        self.webhook_url = webhook_url        def is_configured(self) -> bool:        return bool(self.webhook_url)        async def send(self, notification: Notification):        """        Αποστολή μέσω Slack Webhook.                Χρησιμοποιεί attachments για rich formatting.        """        # Build fields από metadata        fields = []        if notification.metadata:            for key, value in notification.metadata.items():                fields.append({                    "title": key.replace("_", " ").title(),                    "value": str(value),                    "short": len(str(value)) < 50                })                attachment = {            "color": notification.level.color,            "title": f"{notification.level.emoji} {notification.title}",            "text": notification.message,            "footer": "Manus-Win11 Agent",            "ts": int(notification.timestamp.timestamp()),            "fields": fields if fields else None        }                # Remove None values        attachment = {k: v for k, v in attachment.items() if v is not None}                payload = {"attachments": [attachment]}                async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:            try:                async with session.post(                    self.webhook_url,                     json=payload,                    timeout=30                ) as resp:                    if resp.status == 410:                        logger.error("Slack webhook disabled or revoked")                    elif resp.status != 200:                        error = await resp.text()                        raise Exception(f"Slack error {resp.status}: {error}")                                    except aiohttp.ClientError as e:                raise Exception(f"Slack connection error: {e}")class LogChannel(NotificationChannel):    """    Local file logging για notifications.        Χρήσιμο για:    - Audit trail    - Debugging    - Backup όταν άλλα channels αποτυγχάνουν        Format: JSON Lines (κάθε γραμμή ένα JSON object)    Rotation: Διατήρηση τελευταίων 1000 entries    """        def __init__(self, log_file: str = "notifications.jsonl", max_entries: int = 1000):        self.log_file = Path(log_file)        self.max_entries = max_entries        def is_configured(self) -> bool:        return True  # Πάντα configured        async def send(self, notification: Notification):        """        Append notification to log file.                Διατηρεί μόνο τα τελευταία max_entries για να μην μεγαλώνει        απεριόριστα το αρχείο.        """        entry = {            "timestamp": notification.timestamp.isoformat(),            "level": notification.level.label,            "title": notification.title,            "message": notification.message,            "project_id": notification.project_id,            "metadata": notification.metadata        }                # Read existing entries        entries = []        if self.log_file.exists():            try:                with open(self.log_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:                    entries = [line for line in f if line.strip()]            except IOError:                pass                # Add new entry        entries.append(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False))                # Keep only last max_entries        entries = entries[-self.max_entries:]                # Write back        try:            with open(self.log_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:                f.write('\n'.join(entries) + '\n')        except IOError as e:            logger.error(f"Failed to write notification log: {e}")# Παραδείγματα Χρήσηςasync def example_usage():    """Παράδειγμα χρήσης του notification system"""        print("=" * 60)    print("Notification System - Παράδειγμα Χρήσης")    print("=" * 60)        # Αρχικοποίηση (θα φορτώσει από environment)    notifier = NotificationManager()    print(f"\nConfigured channels: {len(notifier.channels)}")        # 1. Project lifecycle    print("\n1. Project Start:")    await notifier.notify_project_start(        project_id="example_project",        description="Testing notification system"    )        # 2. Progress updates    print("\n2. Progress Updates:")    for i in range(0, 101, 25):        await notifier.notify_progress(            project_id="example_project",            task="Data processing",            percent=i        )        await asyncio.sleep(0.1)  # Simulate work        # 3. Checkpoint    print("\n3. Checkpoint:")    await notifier.notify_checkpoint(        project_id="example_project",        message="Review the generated code before proceeding",        input_prompt="Reply with 'approve' or 'modify: <suggestions>'"    )        # 4. Completion    print("\n4. Completion:")    await notifier.notify_completion(        project_id="example_project",        results="Successfully processed 1000 records",        stats={            "duration": "5m 30s",            "cost": "$0.45",            "records_processed": 1000        }    )        # 5. Error handling    print("\n5. Error Example:")    try:        1 / 0    except Exception as e:        await notifier.notify_error(            project_id="example_project",            error=str(e),            critical=False,            context="Division by zero in calculation module"        )        print("\n✅ All notifications sent!")    print("Check notifications.jsonl for log output")if __name__ == "__main__":    # Setup logging για να βλέπουμε debug messages    logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)        # Run example    asyncio.run(example_usage())
3. State Manager (state_manager.py) - Πλήρως Ενημερωμένο
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""state_manager.py - Persistent Project State & Resume CapabilityΛειτουργίες:------------1. Persistent αποθήκευση κατάστασης project (SQLite)2. Checkpoint system για pause/resume3. Automatic recovery από failures4. History tracking (completed tasks, errors)5. Context management για μεταβλητές μεταξύ tasks6. Project archival και cleanupΧαρακτηριστικά:---------------- Atomic updates: Κάθε αλλαγή είναι transaction- Serialization: Pickle για complex objects, JSON για metadata- Querying: Φιλτράρισμα projects ανά status, date, κλπ- Concurrency: SQLite handles locking αυτόματαΒασικές Έννοιες:----------------ProjectState: Η πλήρης κατάσταση ενός project    - status: PENDING/RUNNING/PAUSED/COMPLETED/FAILED    - completed_tasks: Λίστα ολοκληρωμένων tasks    - current_task: Τρέχον task (αν running)    - context: Dictionary με shared data    - checkpoints: Λίστα από checkpointsCheckpoint: Σημείο παύσης για user input    - requires_input: True αν περιμένει χρήστη    - resolved: True αν ο χρήστης απάντησε    - user_response: Η απάντηση του χρήστηΟδηγίες Χρήσης:---------------1. Δημιουργία Project:    sm = StateManager()    state = ProjectState(        project_id="my_project",        status=ProjectStatus.PENDING,        created_at=datetime.now()    )    sm.save_state(state)2. Εκτέλεση με Resume Capability:    async with ResumableTask(sm, "my_project", "task_name") as task:        if task is None:  # Already completed            return                # Do work...        result = await process_data()                # Optional checkpoint        if needs_review:            user_input = await task.checkpoint(                "Review results",                "Approve? (yes/no)"            )    3. Recovery από Crash:    # Μετά από crash, απλά φορτώνουμε το state    state = sm.load_state("my_project")    if state.status == ProjectStatus.RUNNING:        # Resume from last completed task        print(f"Resuming from task: {state.current_task}")4. Έλεγχος Pending Checkpoints:    pending = sm.get_pending_checkpoints("my_project")    for cp in pending:        print(f"Waiting for input: {cp.input_prompt}")Database Schema:----------------projects:    - project_id (TEXT PRIMARY KEY)    - state (BLOB - pickled ProjectState)    - updated_at (TIMESTAMP)checkpoints:    - id (TEXT PRIMARY KEY)    - project_id (TEXT, FOREIGN KEY)    - timestamp (TIMESTAMP)    - data (BLOB - pickled Checkpoint)Παραδείγματα:------------->>> # Δημιουργία και εκτέλεση>>> sm = StateManager("projects.db")>>> >>> # Simulate task execution>>> async def run_tasks():...     async with ResumableTask(sm, "proj1", "download") as t:...         print("Downloading...")...     ...     async with ResumableTask(sm, "proj1", "process") as t:...         if t:...             user_resp = await t.checkpoint("Review", "OK?")...             print(f"User said: {user_resp}")>>> >>> asyncio.run(run_tasks())>>> >>> # Έλεγχος status>>> state = sm.load_state("proj1")>>> print(state.completed_tasks)  # ['download']>>> print(state.status)  # PAUSED (waiting for checkpoint)Dependencies:-------------- sqlite3: Built-in, no install needed- pickle: Built-in- dataclasses: Built-in (Python 3.7+)"""import pickleimport sqlite3import jsonimport asynciofrom enum import Enum, autofrom dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdictfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List, Union, Callablefrom pathlib import Pathfrom datetime import datetime, timedeltafrom contextlib import asynccontextmanagerimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class ProjectStatus(Enum):    """    Καταστάσεις ζωής ενός project.        Transitions:        PENDING -> RUNNING (on start)        RUNNING -> PAUSED (on checkpoint)        PAUSED -> RUNNING (on user input)        RUNNING -> COMPLETED (on success)        RUNNING -> FAILED (on error)        PAUSED -> FAILED (on timeout/cancel)    """    PENDING = "pending"      # Δημιουργήθηκε, δεν ξεκίνησε ακόμα    RUNNING = "running"      # Εκτελείται αυτή τη στιγμή    PAUSED = "paused"        # Σε checkpoint, περιμένει user input    COMPLETED = "completed"  # Ολοκληρώθηκε επιτυχώς    FAILED = "failed"        # Απέτυχε, μπορεί να χρειάζεται retry@dataclassclass Checkpoint:    """    Αναπαράσταση ενός checkpoint (σημείου παύσης).        Ένα checkpoint μπορεί να είναι:    - Simple: Απλά σημειώνει πρόοδο (requires_input=False)    - Interactive: Περιμένει απάντηση χρήστη (requires_input=True)        Attributes:        id: Μοναδικό ID (προτείνεται: project_timestamp)        timestamp: Πότε δημιουργήθηκε        description: Τι περιγράφει το checkpoint        requires_input: Αν χρειάζεται αλληλεπίδραση        input_prompt: Τι ζητάμε από τον χρήστη        resolved: Αν έχει επιλυθεί        user_response: Η απάντηση που δόθηκε    """    id: str    timestamp: datetime    description: str    requires_input: bool = False    input_prompt: Optional[str] = None    resolved: bool = False    user_response: Optional[str] = None        def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Convert to dictionary για serialization"""        return {            "id": self.id,            "timestamp": self.timestamp.isoformat(),            "description": self.description,            "requires_input": self.requires_input,            "input_prompt": self.input_prompt,            "resolved": self.resolved,            "user_response": self.user_response        }@dataclassclass ProjectState:    """    Πλήρης κατάσταση ενός project.        Αυτό αποθηκεύεται στο database και φορτώνεται σε κάθε resume.        Attributes:        project_id: Μοναδικό identifier        status: Τρέχουσα κατάσταση        created_at: Χρόνος δημιουργίας        updated_at: Χρόνος τελευταίας ενημέρωσης        current_task: Ποιο task τρέχει τώρα (αν running)        completed_tasks: Λίστα ολοκληρωμένων task names        context: Dictionary για shared data (π.χ. file paths, results)        checkpoints: Λίστα όλων των checkpoints        error_log: Λίστα σφαλμάτων        metadata: Extra info (version, tags, κλπ)    """    project_id: str    status: ProjectStatus    created_at: datetime    updated_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)    current_task: Optional[str] = None    completed_tasks: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)    context: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)    checkpoints: List[Checkpoint] = field(default_factory=list)    error_log: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)        def __post_init__(self):        """Ensure all lists are initialized"""        if self.completed_tasks is None:            self.completed_tasks = []        if self.context is None:            self.context = {}        if self.checkpoints is None:            self.checkpoints = []        if self.error_log is None:            self.error_log = []        if self.metadata is None:            self.metadata = {}        def is_task_completed(self, task_name: str) -> bool:        """Έλεγχος αν ένα task έχει ολοκληρωθεί"""        return task_name in self.completed_tasks        def get_pending_checkpoints(self) -> List[Checkpoint]:        """Επιστροφή unresolved checkpoints"""        return [cp for cp in self.checkpoints if not cp.resolved]        def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Convert to dictionary"""        return {            "project_id": self.project_id,            "status": self.status.value,            "created_at": self.created_at.isoformat(),            "updated_at": self.updated_at.isoformat(),            "current_task": self.current_task,            "completed_tasks": self.completed_tasks,            "context": self.context,            "checkpoints": [cp.to_dict() for cp in self.checkpoints],            "error_log": self.error_log,            "metadata": self.metadata        }class StateManager:    """    Κεντρικός manager για persistent state.        Χρησιμοποιεί SQLite για atomic updates και durability.    Τα states αποθηκεύονται ως pickle blobs (για να κρατήσουμε    όλους τους τύπους δεδομένων).        Usage:        sm = StateManager("my_projects.db")                # Save        state = ProjectState(...)        sm.save_state(state)                # Load        state = sm.load_state("project_id")                # Query        active = sm.list_projects(status=ProjectStatus.RUNNING)                # Checkpoints        cp = sm.create_checkpoint("proj1", "Review needed", True, "Approve?")        sm.resolve_checkpoint("proj1", cp.id, "yes")    """        def __init__(self, db_path: str = "projects.db"):        """        Αρχικοποίηση StateManager.                Args:            db_path: Path to SQLite database file        """        self.db_path = db_path        self._init_db()        logger.info(f"StateManager initialized with database: {db_path}")        def _init_db(self):        """Δημιουργία tables αν δεν υπάρχουν"""        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            # Main projects table            conn.execute("""                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (                    project_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,                    state BLOB NOT NULL,                    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP                )            """)                        # Checkpoints table (normalized για εύκολο querying)            conn.execute("""                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS checkpoints (                    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,                    project_id TEXT NOT NULL,                    timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,                    data BLOB NOT NULL,                    FOREIGN KEY (project_id) REFERENCES projects(project_id)                        ON DELETE CASCADE                )            """)                        # Index για γρήγορο lookup            conn.execute("""                CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_checkpoints_project                 ON checkpoints(project_id)            """)                        conn.commit()        def save_state(self, state: ProjectState):        """        Αποθήκευση state στο database.                Αυτόματα ενημερώνει το updated_at timestamp.        Χρησιμοποιεί REPLACE για insert ή update.                Args:            state: ProjectState προς αποθήκευση        """        state.updated_at = datetime.now()                with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            conn.execute(                """                INSERT OR REPLACE INTO projects (project_id, state, updated_at)                 VALUES (?, ?, ?)                """,                (state.project_id, pickle.dumps(state), state.updated_at)            )            conn.commit()                    logger.debug(f"Saved state for project: {state.project_id}")        def load_state(self, project_id: str) -> Optional[ProjectState]:        """        Φόρτωση state από database.                Args:            project_id: ID του project                    Returns:            ProjectState ή None αν δεν υπάρχει        """        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            cursor = conn.execute(                "SELECT state FROM projects WHERE project_id = ?",                 (project_id,)            )            row = cursor.fetchone()                        if row:                return pickle.loads(row[0])            return None        def delete_state(self, project_id: str) -> bool:        """        Διαγραφή project και όλων των checkpoints του.                Args:            project_id: ID προς διαγραφή                    Returns:            True αν βρέθηκε και διαγράφηκε        """        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            cursor = conn.execute(                "DELETE FROM projects WHERE project_id = ?",                (project_id,)            )            conn.commit()            return cursor.rowcount > 0        def list_projects(self,                      status: Optional[ProjectStatus] = None,                     older_than_days: Optional[int] = None) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:        """        Λίστα projects με optional filtering.                Args:            status: Φιλτράρισμα ανά status            older_than_days: Φιλτράρισμα παλιών projects                    Returns:            Λίστα dictionaries με project_id και updated_at        """        query = "SELECT project_id, updated_at FROM projects WHERE 1=1"        params = []                if status:            # Note: This requires loading each state to check status            # Για μεγάλα datasets θα ήταν καλύτερο να έχουμε status column            pass                with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            cursor = conn.execute(query, params)            rows = cursor.fetchall()                projects = []        for project_id, updated_at in rows:            # Φιλτράρισμα ανά status αν χρειάζεται            if status:                state = self.load_state(project_id)                if not state or state.status != status:                    continue                        # Φιλτράρισμα ανά date            if older_than_days:                updated = datetime.fromisoformat(updated_at)                if datetime.now() - updated < timedelta(days=older_than_days):                    continue                        projects.append({                "project_id": project_id,                "updated_at": updated_at            })                return projects        def create_checkpoint(self,                         project_id: str,                         description: str,                         requires_input: bool = False,                         input_prompt: Optional[str] = None) -> Checkpoint:        """        Δημιουργία νέου checkpoint.                Αυτόματα ενημερώνει το project state αν χρειάζεται input.                Args:            project_id: ID project            description: Τι περιγράφει το checkpoint            requires_input: Αν περιμένει user interaction            input_prompt: Τι να ρωτήσουμε τον χρήστη                    Returns:            Checkpoint object        """        checkpoint = Checkpoint(            id=f"{project_id}_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S_%f')}",            timestamp=datetime.now(),            description=description,            requires_input=requires_input,            input_prompt=input_prompt        )                # Update project state        state = self.load_state(project_id)        if state:            state.checkpoints.append(checkpoint)            if requires_input:                state.status = ProjectStatus.PAUSED            self.save_state(state)                        # Also save to checkpoints table για εύκολο querying            with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:                conn.execute(                    """                    INSERT INTO checkpoints (id, project_id, data)                     VALUES (?, ?, ?)                    """,                    (checkpoint.id, project_id, pickle.dumps(checkpoint))                )                conn.commit()                logger.info(f"Created checkpoint {checkpoint.id} for {project_id}")        return checkpoint        def resolve_checkpoint(self,                          project_id: str,                          checkpoint_id: str,                          user_response: str) -> bool:        """        Επίλυση pending checkpoint με user input.                Args:            project_id: ID project            checkpoint_id: ID checkpoint            user_response: Τι απάντησε ο χρήστης                    Returns:            True αν βρέθηκε και επιλύθηκε        """        state = self.load_state(project_id)        if not state:            return False                # Find and update checkpoint        for cp in state.checkpoints:            if cp.id == checkpoint_id:                cp.resolved = True                cp.user_response = user_response                                # Update status back to running                state.status = ProjectStatus.RUNNING                self.save_state(state)                                logger.info(f"Resolved checkpoint {checkpoint_id}")                return True                return False        def get_pending_checkpoints(self, project_id: str) -> List[Checkpoint]:        """        Λήψη όλων των unresolved checkpoints για project.                Args:            project_id: ID project                    Returns:            Λίστα από Checkpoints        """        state = self.load_state(project_id)        if not state:            return []                return [cp for cp in state.checkpoints if not cp.resolved]        def add_error(self, project_id: str, error_message: str):        """        Καταγραφή σφάλματος στο project.                Args:            project_id: ID project            error_message: Μήνυμα σφάλματος        """        state = self.load_state(project_id)        if state:            timestamp = datetime.now().isoformat()            state.error_log.append(f"[{timestamp}] {error_message}")            state.status = ProjectStatus.FAILED            self.save_state(state)        def archive_completed(self, days_old: int = 30) -> int:        """        Archival παλιών completed projects.                Args:            days_old: Πόσες μέρες παλιά να διαγραφούν                    Returns:            Αριθμός διαγραμμένων projects        """        cutoff = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=days_old)        count = 0                with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:            # Get old completed projects            cursor = conn.execute(                "SELECT project_id, state FROM projects"            )                        for project_id, state_blob in cursor:                state = pickle.loads(state_blob)                if (state.status == ProjectStatus.COMPLETED and                     state.updated_at < cutoff):                    conn.execute(                        "DELETE FROM projects WHERE project_id = ?",                        (project_id,)                    )                    count += 1                        conn.commit()                logger.info(f"Archived {count} old projects")        return count        def export_project(self, project_id: str, export_path: str):        """        Export project state σε JSON file.                Χρήσιμο για backup ή analysis.                Args:            project_id: ID project            export_path: Που να αποθηκευτεί το JSON        """        state = self.load_state(project_id)        if not state:            raise ValueError(f"Project {project_id} not found")                export_data = {            "exported_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),            "state": state.to_dict()        }                Path(export_path).write_text(            json.dumps(export_data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False),            encoding='utf-8'        )class ResumableTask:    """    Context manager για atomic task execution με auto-resume.        Features:    - Automatic skip αν task ήδη completed    - Automatic state update σε success/failure    - Checkpoint creation με user input    - Error logging        Usage:        async with ResumableTask(sm, "proj1", "download_data") as task:            if task is None:                return  # Already done                        # Do work...            data = await download()                        # Optional checkpoint            if needs_verification:                approval = await task.checkpoint(                    "Verify downloaded data",                    "Is the data correct? (yes/no)"                )                if approval != "yes":                    raise ValueError("Data rejected")        Args:        state_manager: StateManager instance        project_id: ID του project        task_name: Μοναδικό όνομα task        notifier: Optional NotificationManager για alerts    """        def __init__(self,                 state_manager: StateManager,                 project_id: str,                 task_name: str,                 notifier=None):        self.state_manager = state_manager        self.project_id = project_id        self.task_name = task_name        self.notifier = notifier        self.state = None        self._entered = False        async def __aenter__(self):        """Entry point του context manager"""        self.state = self.state_manager.load_state(self.project_id)                # Create if not exists        if not self.state:            self.state = ProjectState(                project_id=self.project_id,                status=ProjectStatus.RUNNING,                created_at=datetime.now()            )                # Check if already completed        if self.task_name in self.state.completed_tasks:            logger.info(f"Task {self.task_name} already completed, skipping")            return None                # Mark as running        self.state.current_task = self.task_name        self.state.status = ProjectStatus.RUNNING        self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                self._entered = True        logger.info(f"Starting task: {self.task_name}")        return self        async def __aexit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):        """Exit point - καθαρισμός και logging"""        if not self._entered:            return False                if exc_type is None:            # Success            self.state.completed_tasks.append(self.task_name)            self.state.current_task = None            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)            logger.info(f"Completed task: {self.task_name}")                    else:            # Failure            error_msg = f"{exc_type.__name__}: {str(exc_val)}"            self.state.error_log.append(                f"[{datetime.now().isoformat()}] {self.task_name}: {error_msg}"            )            self.state.status = ProjectStatus.FAILED            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                        if self.notifier:                await self.notifier.notify_error(                    self.project_id,                    error_msg,                    critical=True                )                        logger.error(f"Task {self.task_name} failed: {error_msg}")                return False  # Don't suppress exceptions        async def checkpoint(self,                        description: str,                        input_prompt: Optional[str] = None,                        timeout: Optional[int] = None) -> Optional[str]:        """        Δημιουργία checkpoint και αναμονή για user input.                Args:            description: Τι περιγράφει το checkpoint            input_prompt: Τι ζητάμε από τον χρήστη            timeout: Μέγιστος χρόνος αναμονής (δευτερόλεπτα)                    Returns:            User response string ή None αν timeout        """        if not input_prompt:            # Simple checkpoint, no waiting            self.state_manager.create_checkpoint(                self.project_id, description, False            )            return None                # Interactive checkpoint        cp = self.state_manager.create_checkpoint(            self.project_id, description, True, input_prompt        )                if self.notifier:            await self.notifier.notify_checkpoint(                self.project_id,                description,                input_prompt            )                logger.info(f"Waiting for user input on checkpoint {cp.id}")                # Poll for resolution        start_time = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()        while True:            # Check if resolved            pending = self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(self.project_id)            for p in pending:                if p.id == cp.id and p.resolved:                    logger.info(f"Checkpoint {cp.id} resolved")                    return p.user_response                        # Check timeout            if timeout and (asyncio.get_event_loop().time() - start_time) > timeout:                logger.warning(f"Checkpoint {cp.id} timeout")                return None                        await asyncio.sleep(1)        async def pause_for_approval(self,                                   message: str,                                  options: List[str] = None) -> str:        """        Παύση μέχρι να λάβουμε συγκεκριμένη απάντηση.                Convenience method για common pattern.                Args:            message: Μήνυμα προς τον χρήστη            options: Αποδεκτές απαντήσεις (π.χ. ["yes", "no", "retry"])                    Returns:            Η επιλογή του χρήστη        """        options_str = f"Options: {', '.join(options)}" if options else ""        prompt = f"{message}\n{options_str}".strip()                while True:            response = await self.checkpoint(message, prompt)                        if options and response not in options:                await self.notifier.notify_error(                    self.project_id,                    f"Invalid response '{response}'. Expected: {options}",                    critical=False                )                continue                        return response# Παραδείγματα Χρήσηςasync def example_usage():    """Παράδειγμα πλήρους ροής με StateManager"""        print("=" * 60)    print("State Manager - Παράδειγμα Χρήσης")    print("=" * 60)        # Αρχικοποίηση    sm = StateManager("example.db")        # 1. Δημιουργία project    print("\n1. Creating project...")    project_id = "data_pipeline_v1"    state = ProjectState(        project_id=project_id,        status=ProjectStatus.PENDING,        created_at=datetime.now(),        metadata={"version": "1.0", "type": "etl"}    )    sm.save_state(state)    print(f"   Created: {project_id}")        # 2. Εκτέλεση tasks με resume capability    print("\n2. Executing tasks (with resume)...")        # Task 1: Extract    async with ResumableTask(sm, project_id, "extract_data") as task:        if task:            print("   Running: extract_data")            # Simulate work            await asyncio.sleep(0.5)            task.state.context["extracted_files"] = ["data1.csv", "data2.csv"]        # Task 2: Transform (με checkpoint)    async with ResumableTask(sm, project_id, "transform_data") as task:        if task:            print("   Running: transform_data")            await asyncio.sleep(0.5)                        # Checkpoint για review            print("   Creating checkpoint for review...")            # Σε πραγματική χρήση, αυτό θα περίμενε πραγματικό user input            # Εδώ το προσομοιώνουμε            cp = sm.create_checkpoint(                project_id,                "Review transformed data",                requires_input=True,                input_prompt="Data looks good? (yes/no)"            )            print(f"   Checkpoint created: {cp.id}")                        # Simulate user resolution            await asyncio.sleep(1)            sm.resolve_checkpoint(project_id, cp.id, "yes")            print("   Checkpoint resolved by user")        # Task 3: Load    async with ResumableTask(sm, project_id, "load_data") as task:        if task:            print("   Running: load_data")            await asyncio.sleep(0.5)        # 3. Έλεγχος τελικής κατάστασης    print("\n3. Final state:")    final_state = sm.load_state(project_id)    print(f"   Status: {final_state.status.value}")    print(f"   Completed tasks: {final_state.completed_tasks}")    print(f"   Context: {final_state.context}")        # 4. Προσομοίωση resume (επανεκκίνηση από το 0)    print("\n4. Simulating restart (tasks should be skipped)...")        async with ResumableTask(sm, project_id, "extract_data") as task:        if task is None:            print("   extract_data: SKIPPED (already done)")        # 5. Export    print("\n5. Exporting project state...")    sm.export_project(project_id, "project_export.json")    print("   Exported to: project_export.json")        # Cleanup    print("\n6. Cleanup...")    sm.delete_state(project_id)    Path("example.db").unlink(missing_ok=True)    Path("project_export.json").unlink(missing_ok=True)    print("   Done!")if __name__ == "__main__":    logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)    asyncio.run(example_usage())
4. Agent Core (agent_core.py) - Πλήρως Ενημερωμένο
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""agent_core.py - Manus-Win11 Agent CoreΛειτουργίες:------------1. Ενσωμάτωση όλων των subsystems (AI Router, Notifications, State)2. Task planning και execution3. Tool registration και calling4. Error handling με recovery5. Cost optimization και budget management6. Human-in-the-loop checkpointsΑρχιτεκτονική:--------------AgentCore├── ModelRouter (AI selection & caching)├── NotificationManager (alerts & updates)├── StateManager (persistence & resume)└── Tools (registered capabilities)Task Execution Flow:--------------------1. Plan Creation: Λίστα από tasks με dependencies2. Execution: Κάθε task τρέχει με ResumableTask3. AI Generation: Επιλογή μοντέλου + generation4. Tool Calling: Αν χρειάζεται εκτέλεση εργαλείου5. Checkpoint: Παύση για user input αν χρειάζεται6. State Update: Αποθήκευση προόδου7. Notification: Ενημέρωση χρήστηΟδηγίες Χρήσης:---------------1. Βασική Αρχικοποίηση:    agent = AgentCore(        project_id="my_project",        description="Automate data analysis"    )2. Ορισμός Task Plan:    plan = [        {            "name": "analyze_requirements",            "type": TaskType.ANALYSIS,            "description": "Analyze the data structure",            "prompt": "Given this dataset..., what are the key columns?"        },        {            "name": "generate_code",            "type": TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,            "description": "Create processing script",            "depends_on": ["analyze_requirements"],            "checkpoint": True,            "checkpoint_desc": "Review generated code",            "input_prompt": "Does the code look correct? (yes/regenerate)"        }    ]3. Εκτέλεση:    await agent.execute_plan(plan)4. Resume μετά από crash:    # Αυτόματο, απλά ξανατρέχεις:    await agent.execute_plan(plan)  # Θα συνεχίσει από εκεί που έμεινε5. Tool Registration:    def my_tool(code: str):        # Execute code...        return result        agent.register_tool("code_executor", my_tool)Task Configuration:-------------------Κάθε task στο plan είναι dictionary με:- name: Μοναδικό όνομα (string)- type: TaskType (ANALYSIS, CODE_GENERATION, κλπ)- description: Περιγραφή για logs- prompt: Το prompt για το AI (string ή template)- depends_on: Λίστα από task names που πρέπει να ολοκληρωθούν πρώτα- checkpoint: Boolean, αν θα κάνει pause για user input- checkpoint_desc: Τι περιγράφει το checkpoint- input_prompt: Τι να ρωτήσουμε τον χρήστη- tool: Όνομα εργαλείου για post-processing- max_tokens: Όριο tokens για απόκριση- temperature: Creativity 0.0-1.0- use_cache: Boolean, αν θα χρησιμοποιηθεί caching (default True)Περιβαλλοντικές Μεταβλητές:---------------------------- Κληρονομούνται από subsystems (δες ai_router.py, notifications.py)- AGENT_DEFAULT_TEMPERATURE: Default temperature (default 0.7)- AGENT_MAX_RETRIES: Max retries per task (default 3)- AGENT_CHECKPOINT_TIMEOUT: Timeout για checkpoints σε δευτερόλεπτα (default 3600)Παραδείγματα:------------->>> # Simple analysis task>>> agent = AgentCore("analysis_001", "Customer data analysis")>>> await agent.execute_plan([...     {...         "name": "analyze",...         "type": TaskType.ANALYSIS,...         "description": "Analyze customer churn",...         "prompt": "Analyze this customer data for churn patterns..."...     }... ])>>> # With checkpoint>>> await agent.execute_plan([...     {...         "name": "generate",...         "type": TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,...         "description": "Generate API client",...         "prompt": "Create a Python client for REST API...",...         "checkpoint": True,...         "input_prompt": "Review the code. Approve? (yes/modify/cancel)"...     }... ])>>> # Agent pauses here, sends notification, waits for user responseDependencies:-------------- ai_router: ModelRouter, TaskType- notifications: NotificationManager- state_manager: StateManager, ResumableTask, ProjectStatus- aiohttp: για async operations- python-dotenv: προαιρετικά για env vars"""import osimport asyncioimport jsonimport loggingfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Callable, Unionfrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom datetime import datetimefrom pathlib import Path# Import subsystemsfrom ai_router import ModelRouter, TaskType, ModelTierfrom notifications import NotificationManager, Notification, NotificationLevelfrom state_manager import StateManager, ResumableTask, ProjectState, ProjectStatuslogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass AgentConfig:    """    Configuration για AgentCore.        Attributes:        project_id: Μοναδικό ID project        description: Περιγραφή για notifications        daily_budget: Ημερήσιο AI budget        auto_resume: Αυτόματο resume από checkpoints        notification_channels: Λίστα channels (['telegram', 'slack'])        default_temperature: Default temperature για generation        max_retries: Max retries ανά task        checkpoint_timeout: Timeout για checkpoints (sec)        cache_dir: Directory για AI response cache    """    project_id: str    description: str    daily_budget: float = 10.0    auto_resume: bool = True    notification_channels: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)    default_temperature: float = 0.7    max_retries: int = 3    checkpoint_timeout: int = 3600  # 1 hour    cache_dir: str = "./cache"class AgentCore:    """    Κεντρικός agent για αυτόνομη εκτέλεση tasks.        Ενσωματώνει:    - AI model selection και generation    - State persistence και resume    - Notifications    - Tool execution    - Cost tracking        Usage:        config = AgentConfig(            project_id="etl_pipeline",            description="Extract and transform data"        )                agent = AgentCore(config)                # Register custom tools        agent.register_tool("save_file", save_file_function)                # Execute plan        await agent.execute_plan([            {"name": "step1", "type": TaskType.ANALYSIS, ...},            {"name": "step2", "type": TaskType.CODE_GENERATION, ...}        ])    """        def __init__(self, config: AgentConfig):        """        Αρχικοποίηση AgentCore και όλων των subsystems.                Args:            config: AgentConfig με ρυθμίσεις        """        self.config = config                # Initialize subsystems        self.router = ModelRouter(            cache_dir=config.cache_dir,            daily_budget=config.daily_budget        )                self.notifier = NotificationManager()        self.state_manager = StateManager()                # Tool registry        self.tools: Dict[str, Callable] = {}                # Load or create project state        self.state = self.state_manager.load_state(config.project_id)        if not self.state:            self.state = ProjectState(                project_id=config.project_id,                status=ProjectStatus.PENDING,                created_at=datetime.now(),                metadata={                    "description": config.description,                    "config": {                        "daily_budget": config.daily_budget,                        "auto_resume": config.auto_resume                    }                }            )            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                logger.info(f"AgentCore initialized for project: {config.project_id}")        def register_tool(self, name: str, handler: Callable):        """        Καταχώρηση εργαλείου για χρήση από tasks.                Τα εργαλεία είναι συναρτήσεις που καλούνται μετά το AI generation        για να εκτελέσουν το παραγόμενο αποτέλεσμα (π.χ. αποθήκευση αρχείου).                Args:            name: Μοναδικό όνομα εργαλείου            handler: Συνάρτηση (args: str) -> Any                Example:            def save_python_code(code: str):                Path("script.py").write_text(code)                return {"saved": True, "path": "script.py"}                        agent.register_tool("save_python", save_python_code)        """        self.tools[name] = handler        logger.info(f"Registered tool: {name}")        async def execute_plan(self, plan: List[Dict[str, Any]]):        """        Εκτέλεση task plan με auto-resume και error recovery.                Αυτή είναι η κύρια μέθοδος χρήσης. Διαχειρίζεται:        - Dependency resolution        - Task execution με state persistence        - AI generation με model selection        - Checkpoints και user input        - Error handling και retries        - Notifications                Args:            plan: Λίστα από task dictionaries (βλέπε Task Configuration πάνω)                Raises:            Exception: Αν αποτύχει κρίσιμο task και δεν υπάρχει recovery                Example:            plan = [                {                    "name": "requirements",                    "type": TaskType.ANALYSIS,                    "description": "Analyze requirements",                    "prompt": "What are the key features needed?"                },                {                    "name": "implementation",                    "type": TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,                    "description": "Generate code",                    "prompt": "Generate Python code for...",                    "depends_on": ["requirements"],                    "checkpoint": True,                    "input_prompt": "Review the code?"                }            ]                        await agent.execute_plan(plan)        """        # Notify start        await self.notifier.notify_project_start(            self.config.project_id,            self.config.description        )                try:            # Build dependency graph            task_map = {t["name"]: t for t in plan}            executed = set(self.state.completed_tasks)                        for task in plan:                task_name = task["name"]                                # Skip if already completed                if task_name in executed:                    logger.info(f"Skipping completed task: {task_name}")                    continue                                # Check dependencies                deps = task.get("depends_on", [])                if not all(d in executed for d in deps):                    logger.warning(f"Dependencies not met for {task_name}")                    continue                                # Execute task                success = await self._execute_task(task)                                if success:                    executed.add(task_name)                else:                    raise Exception(f"Task {task_name} failed after retries")                        # Mark complete            self.state.status = ProjectStatus.COMPLETED            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                        await self.notifier.notify_completion(                self.config.project_id,                f"Completed {len(executed)} tasks successfully",                stats={                    "total_cost": self.router.cost_tracker.get_stats()["today"],                    "tasks_completed": len(executed)                }            )                    except Exception as e:            self.state.status = ProjectStatus.FAILED            self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                        await self.notifier.notify_error(                self.config.project_id,                str(e),                critical=True            )            raise        async def _execute_task(self, task: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:        """        Εκτέλεση single task με retries και checkpoint handling.                Args:            task: Task configuration dictionary                Returns:            True αν επιτυχία, False αν αποτυχία        """        task_name = task["name"]        max_retries = task.get("max_retries", self.config.max_retries)                for attempt in range(max_retries):            try:                async with ResumableTask(                    self.state_manager,                    self.config.project_id,                    task_name,                    self.notifier                ) as rt:                                        if rt is None:  # Already completed                        return True                                        # Update context με task-specific data                    context = {                        **self.state.context,                        "task_name": task_name,                        "attempt": attempt + 1                    }                                        # AI Generation                    ai_result = await self._generate_for_task(task, context)                                        # Tool execution αν υπάρχει                    if "tool" in task and task["tool"] in self.tools:                        tool_result = await self._execute_tool(                            task["tool"],                             ai_result["content"]                        )                        # Store result in context                        self.state.context[f"{task_name}_result"] = tool_result                                        # Checkpoint handling                    if task.get("checkpoint"):                        user_input = await rt.checkpoint(                            task.get("checkpoint_desc", "Checkpoint reached"),                            task.get("input_prompt")                        )                                                # Handle user response                        if user_input and user_input.lower() in ["no", "cancel", "abort"]:                            raise Exception(f"Task {task_name} cancelled by user")                                                # Store user input in context                        self.state.context[f"{task_name}_user_input"] = user_input                                        return True                                except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"Task {task_name} attempt {attempt + 1} failed: {e}")                if attempt == max_retries - 1:                    return False                await asyncio.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # Exponential backoff                return False        async def _generate_for_task(self,                                   task: Dict[str, Any],                                  context: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """        AI generation για task με model selection.                Args:            task: Task config            context: Current context variables                Returns:            Result από ModelRouter.generate_with_fallback        """        task_type = TaskType(task.get("type", "analysis"))                # Build prompt από template        prompt_template = task.get("prompt", "")        prompt = self._render_template(prompt_template, context)                # System prompt αν υπάρχει        system_prompt = task.get("system_prompt")                # Generation parameters        temperature = task.get("temperature", self.config.default_temperature)        max_tokens = task.get("max_tokens")        use_cache = task.get("use_cache", True)                # Execute generation        result = await self.router.generate_with_fallback(            prompt=prompt,            task_type=task_type,            temperature=temperature,            max_tokens=max_tokens,            system_prompt=system_prompt,            use_cache=use_cache,            max_retries=2  # Internal retries        )                # Store in context        self.state.context[f"{task['name']}_ai_response"] = result["content"]        self.state_manager.save_state(self.state)                return result        def _render_template(self, template: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:        """        Απλό templating για prompts.                Υποστηρίζει: {variable} syntax                Args:            template: String με {placeholders}            context: Dictionary με values                Returns:            Rendered string        """        try:            return template.format(**context)        except KeyError as e:            logger.warning(f"Missing template variable: {e}")            return template        async def _execute_tool(self, tool_name: str, input_data: str) -> Any:        """        Κλήση registered tool.                Args:            tool_name: Όνομα εργαλείου            input_data: Input (συνήθως το AI output)                Returns:            Tool result        """        if tool_name not in self.tools:            raise ValueError(f"Tool not found: {tool_name}")                handler = self.tools[tool_name]                # Support both sync and async tools        if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(handler):            return await handler(input_data)        else:            return handler(input_data)        def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """        Λήψη τρέχουσας κατάστασης agent.                Returns:            Dictionary με status info        """        cost_stats = self.router.cost_tracker.get_stats()                return {            "project_id": self.config.project_id,            "status": self.state.status.value,            "description": self.config.description,            "progress": {                "completed": len(self.state.completed_tasks),                "total": len(self.state.metadata.get("plan", [])),                "current_task": self.state.current_task            },            "pending_checkpoints": len(                self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(self.config.project_id)            ),            "cost": {                "today": cost_stats["today"],                "budget": cost_stats["budget"],                "remaining": cost_stats["remaining"]            },            "tools_registered": list(self.tools.keys()),            "last_updated": self.state.updated_at.isoformat()        }        async def wait_for_checkpoint(self, checkpoint_id: str,                                    timeout: Optional[int] = None) -> Optional[str]:        """        Ενεργή αναμονή για συγκεκριμένο checkpoint.                Χρήσιμο για external scripts που ελέγχουν checkpoints.                Args:            checkpoint_id: ID του checkpoint            timeout: Μέγιστος χρόνος αναμονής                Returns:            User response ή None αν timeout        """        timeout = timeout or self.config.checkpoint_timeout        start = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()                while True:            pending = self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(self.config.project_id)            for cp in pending:                if cp.id == checkpoint_id and cp.resolved:                    return cp.user_response                        if asyncio.get_event_loop().time() - start > timeout:                return None                        await asyncio.sleep(1)        def export_state(self, filepath: str):        """        Export πλήρους state για debugging.                Args:            filepath: Που να αποθηκευτεί το JSON        """        export_data = {            "exported_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),            "config": {                "project_id": self.config.project_id,                "description": self.config.description,                "daily_budget": self.config.daily_budget            },            "state": self.state.to_dict(),            "cost_report": self.router.get_cost_report()        }                Path(filepath).write_text(            json.dumps(export_data, indent=2, default=str),            encoding='utf-8'        )                logger.info(f"State exported to: {filepath}")# Παραδείγματα Χρήσηςasync def example_usage():    """Πλήρες παράδειγμα χρήσης AgentCore"""        print("=" * 70)    print("AgentCore - Παράδειγμα Χρήσης")    print("=" * 70)        # Configuration    config = AgentConfig(        project_id="example_data_pipeline",        description="Extract and analyze sales data",        daily_budget=5.0,        auto_resume=True,        cache_dir="./agent_cache"    )        # Initialize agent    agent = AgentCore(config)        # Register a simple tool    def save_analysis_report(content: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Tool για αποθήκευση report"""        filename = f"report_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.txt"        Path(filename).write_text(content, encoding='utf-8')        return {"saved": True, "filename": filename}        agent.register_tool("save_report", save_analysis_report)        # Define task plan    plan = [        {            "name": "analyze_requirements",            "type": TaskType.ANALYSIS,            "description": "Understand data structure",            "prompt": "Given a CSV with columns: date, product, sales, quantity. "                     "What analysis would be most valuable?",            "use_cache": True        },        {            "name": "generate_analysis_code",            "type": TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,            "description": "Create Python analysis script",            "prompt": "Generate Python code to analyze sales data. "                     "Include: total sales by product, monthly trends.",            "checkpoint": True,            "checkpoint_desc": "Review generated analysis code",            "input_prompt": "Does the code look correct? (yes/regenerate/cancel)",            "tool": "save_report"  # Save the generated code        }    ]        print(f"\nProject: {config.project_id}")    print(f"Description: {config.description}")    print(f"Plan: {len(plan)} tasks")        # Show initial status    print(f"\nInitial Status:")    status = agent.get_status()    print(f"  Status: {status['status']}")    print(f"  Budget: ${status['cost']['budget']}")        # Execute (σε πραγματική χρήση, θα περίμενε πραγματικό user input)    print(f"\nExecuting plan...")    print("(Σε πραγματική χρήση, θα σταματούσε στο checkpoint για input)")        # Για το παράδειγμα, θα τρέξουμε μόνο το πρώτο task    try:        await agent.execute_plan([plan[0]])        print("✓ First task completed")    except Exception as e:        print(f"✗ Error: {e}")        # Show final status    print(f"\nFinal Status:")    status = agent.get_status()    print(f"  Status: {status['status']}")    print(f"  Completed tasks: {status['progress']['completed']}")    print(f"  Cost so far: ${status['cost']['today']:.4f}")        # Export state    agent.export_state("agent_state.json")    print(f"\nState exported to: agent_state.json")        # Cleanup    Path("agent_state.json").unlink(missing_ok=True)    for f in Path(".").glob("report_*.txt"):        f.unlink()        print("\n✅ Example completed!")if __name__ == "__main__":    logging.basicConfig(        level=logging.INFO,        format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'    )        # Run example    asyncio.run(example_usage())
5. CLI Interface (cli.py) - Πλήρως Ενημερωμένο
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""cli.py - Command Line Interface για Manus-Win11 AgentΛειτουργίες:------------1. Διαχείριση projects (create, list, delete)2. Εκτέλεση task plans από JSON files3. Monitoring (status, logs, cost reports)4. Checkpoint resolution (user input)5. Configuration management6. Export/Import projectsΕντολές:--------create      Δημιουργία νέου projectlist        Λίστα όλων των projects  status      Έλεγχος κατάστασης projectrun         Εκτέλεση task plan από JSONresume      Συνέχιση paused projectcheckpoint  Επίλυση pending checkpointdelete      Διαγραφή projectexport      Export project statecosts       Αναφορά κόστουςmonitor     Real-time monitoring (live dashboard)Οδηγίες Χρήσης:---------------1. Δημιουργία Project:    python cli.py create my_project "Data analysis pipeline" --budget 202. Ορισμός Task Plan (plan.json):    {      "tasks": [        {          "name": "analyze",          "type": "analysis",          "description": "Analyze data",          "prompt": "What patterns do you see in this data?"        }      ]    }3. Εκτέλεση:    python cli.py run my_project plan.json4. Έλεγχος Status:    python cli.py status my_project5. Επίλυση Checkpoint:    python cli.py checkpoint my_project chk_001 "yes"6. Monitoring:    python cli.py monitor my_project  # Παρακολούθηση σε πραγματικό χρόνοConfiguration File:-------------------Το CLI ψάχνει για ~/.manus/config.json:{    "default_budget": 10.0,    "notification_channels": ["telegram"],    "cache_dir": "~/.manus/cache",    "db_path": "~/.manus/projects.db"}Environment Variables:----------------------- MANUS_CONFIG: Path to config file- MANUS_DB: Path to database- Ολα τα vars από ai_router και notificationsΠαραδείγματα:-------------# Δημιουργία και εκτέλεση$ python cli.py create web_scraper "E-commerce price monitor"Created project: web_scraper$ python cli.py run web_scraper plans/scraper.jsonStarting execution...Task 1/3: setup_environment ✓Task 2/3: generate_scraper_code ✓Checkpoint reached: Review generated codeUse: python cli.py checkpoint web_scraper web_scraper_20240115_120000 "yes"$ python cli.py checkpoint web_scraper web_scraper_20240115_120000 "yes"Checkpoint resolved, continuing...Task 3/3: test_scraper config_paths = [        os.getenv("MANUS_CONFIG"),        Path.home() / ".manus" / "config.json",        Path("config.json")    ]        for path in config_paths:        if path and Path(path).exists():            return json.loads(Path(path).read_text())        return {        "default_budget": 10.0,        "cache_dir": "./cache",        "db_path": "./projects.db"    }def get_db_path() -> str:    """Λήψη database path από env ή config"""    return os.getenv("MANUS_DB") or get_config().get("db_path", "./projects.db")def format_status(status: str) -> str:    """Colorize status για terminal"""    colors = {        "pending": "yellow",        "running": "blue",        "paused": "orange3",        "completed": "green",        "failed": "red"    }    color = colors.get(status, "white")    return f"[{color}]{status}[/{color}]"# CLI Group@click.group()@click.option('--verbose', '-v', is_flag=True, help="Verbose output")@click.pass_contextdef cli(ctx, verbose):    """Manus-Win11 Agent Framework CLI"""    ctx.ensure_object(dict)    ctx.obj['VERBOSE'] = verbose    ctx.obj['CONFIG'] = get_config()        if verbose:        console.print("[dim]Verbose mode enabled[/dim]")@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.argument("description")@click.option("--budget", "-b", default=10.0, help="Daily AI budget ($)")@click.option("--template", "-t", type=click.Choice(["empty", "web_scraper", "data_analysis"]),               default="empty", help="Project template")@click.pass_contextdef create(ctx, project_id: str, description: str, budget: float, template: str):    """Δημιουργία νέου project"""        config = AgentConfig(        project_id=project_id,        description=description,        daily_budget=budget,        cache_dir=ctx.obj['CONFIG'].get('cache_dir', './cache')    )        # Check if exists    sm = StateManager(get_db_path())    if sm.load_state(project_id):        console.print(f"[red]Error: Project {project_id} already exists[/red]")        sys.exit(1)        # Create    agent = AgentCore(config)        # Create template plan if requested    if template != "empty":        templates = {            "web_scraper": [                {"name": "analyze_site", "type": "analysis", "description": "Analyze target website"},                {"name": "generate_scraper", "type": "code_generation", "description": "Generate scraper code"},                {"name": "test_scraper", "type": "code_generation", "description": "Create tests"}            ],            "data_analysis": [              {"name": "visualize", "type": "code_generation", "description": "Create visualizations"}            ]        }                plan_file = f"{project_id}_plan.json"        with open(plan_file, 'w') as f:            json.dump({"tasks": templates[template]}, f, indent=2)        console.print(f"[dim]Created template plan: {plan_file}[/dim]")        console.print(Panel(        f"[green]Created project: {project_id}[/green]\n"        f"Description: {description}\n"        f"Budget: ${budget}/day\n"        f"Status: {format_status('pending')}",        title="Project Created"    ))@cli.command()@click.option("--status", "-s", type=click.Choice(["pending", "running", "paused", "completed", "failed"]),              help="Filter by status")@click.option("--all", "-a", is_flag=True, help="Show all including completed")@click.pass_contextdef list(ctx, status: Optional[str], all: bool):    """Λίστα όλων των projects"""        sm = StateManager(get_db_path())        # Filter logic    status_filter = ProjectStatus(status) if status else None        if not all and not status:        # By default, hide completed        projects = []        for p in sm.list_projects():            state = sm.load_state(p["project_id"])            if state and state.status != ProjectStatus.COMPLETED:                projects.append(p)    else:        projects = sm.list_projects(status=status_filter)        if not projects:        console.print("[yellow]No projects found[/yellow]")        return        table = Table(title="Projects")    table.add_column("ID", style="cyan")    table.add_column("Status", style="magenta")    table.add_column("Description", style="green")    table.add_column("Updated", style="dim")        for proj in projects:        state = sm.load_state(proj["project_id"])        desc = state.metadata.get("description", "N/A") if state else "N/A"                table.add_row(            proj["project_id"],            format_status(state.status.value) if state else "[dim]unknown[/dim]",            desc[:50] + "..." if len(desc) > 50 else desc,            str(proj["updated_at"])[:19]        )        console.print(table)@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.pass_contextdef status(ctx, project_id: str):    """Έλεγχος λεπτομερούς κατάστασης project"""        sm = StateManager(get_db_path())    state = sm.load_state(project_id)        if not state:        console.print(f"[red]Project {project_id} not found[/red]")        sys.exit(1)        # Get full status from AgentCore    config = AgentConfig(        project_id=project_id,        description="",        cache_dir=ctx.obj['CONFIG'].get('cache_dir', './cache')    )    agent = AgentCore(config)    status_info = agent.get_status()        # Main info panel    main_info = (        f"Status: {format_status(status_info['status'])}\n"        f"Description: {status_info['description']}\n"        f"Created: {state.created_at.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}\n"        f"Updated: {state.updated_at.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}"    )        # Progress    progress_info = (        f"Completed: {status_info['progress']['completed']} tasks\n"        f"Current: {status_info['progress']['current_task'] or 'None'}\n"        f"Pending Checkpoints: {status_info['pending_checkpoints']}"    )
