)        console.print(Panel(main_info, title="Project Info"))    console.print(Panel(progress_info, title="Progress"))    console.print(Panel(cost_info, title="Cost"))        # Pending checkpoints    pending = sm.get_pending_checkpoints(project_id)    if pending:        console.print("\n[yellow]Pending Checkpoints:[/yellow]")        for cp in pending:            console.print(f"  • {cp.id}: {cp.description}")            if cp.input_prompt:                console.print(f"    Prompt: {cp.input_prompt}")@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.argument("plan_file", type=click.Path(exists=True))@click.option("--dry-run", is_flag=True, help="Validate plan without executing")@click.pass_contextdef run(ctx, project_id: str, plan_file: str, dry_run: bool):    """Εκτέλεση task plan από JSON file"""        # Load plan    with open(plan_file) as f:        plan_data = json.load(f)        tasks = plan_data.get("tasks", [])        if not tasks:        console.print("[red]No tasks found in plan file[/red]")        sys.exit(1)        # Validate tasks    required_fields = ["name", "type", "description"]    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):        for field in required_fields:            if field not in task:                console.print(f"[red]Task {i} missing field: {field}[/red]")                sys.exit(1)                # Convert type string to TaskType        try:            task["type"] = TaskType(task["type"])        except ValueError:            console.print(f"[red]Invalid task type: {task['type']}[/red]")            sys.exit(1)        if dry_run:        console.print(f"[green]Plan validated: {len(tasks)} tasks[/green]")        for t in tasks:            console.print(f"  • {t['name']} ({t['type'].value})")        return        # Execute    sm = StateManager(get_db_path())    state = sm.load_state(project_id)        if not state:        console.print(f"[red]Project {project_id} not found. Create it first.[/red]")        sys.exit(1)        config = AgentConfig(        project_id=project_id,        description=state.metadata.get("description", ""),        daily_budget=state.metadata.get("config", {}).get("daily_budget", 10.0),        cache_dir=ctx.obj['CONFIG'].get('cache_dir', './cache')    )        agent = AgentCore(config)        console.print(f"[blue]Executing {len(tasks)} tasks...[/blue]")        try:        asyncio.run(agent.execute_plan(tasks))        console.print("[green]✓ Execution completed successfully[/green]")    except Exception as e:        console.print(f"[red]✗ Execution failed: {e}[/red]")        if ctx.obj['VERBOSE']:            import traceback            console.print(traceback.format_exc())        sys.exit(1)@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.argument("checkpoint_id")@click.argument("response")@click.pass_contextdef checkpoint(ctx, project_id: str, checkpoint_id: str, response: str):    """Επίλυση pending checkpoint με user response"""        sm = StateManager(get_db_path())        if not sm.load_state(project_id):        console.print(f"[red]Project {project_id} not found[/red]")        sys.exit(1)        success = sm.resolve_checkpoint(project_id, checkpoint_id, response)        if success:        console.print(f"[green]✓ Checkpoint {checkpoint_id} resolved[/green]")        console.print(f"[dim]Response recorded: {response}[/dim]")                # Check if project can resume        state = sm.load_state(project_id)        if state.status == ProjectStatus.RUNNING:            console.print("[blue]Project is ready to resume[/blue]")    else:        console.print(f"[red]✗ Failed to resolve checkpoint (not found or already resolved)[/red]")        sys.exit(1)@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.confirmation_option(prompt="Are you sure you want to delete this project?")@click.pass_contextdef delete(ctx, project_id: str):    """Διαγραφή project και όλων των δεδομένων του"""        sm = StateManager(get_db_path())        if sm.delete_state(project_id):        console.print(f"[green]✓ Project {project_id} deleted[/green]")    else:        console.print(f"[yellow]Project {project_id} not found[/yellow]")@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.argument("output_file", type=click.Path())@click.pass_contextdef export(ctx, project_id: str, output_file: str):    """Export project state σε JSON file"""        sm = StateManager(get_db_path())    state = sm.load_state(project_id)        if not state:        console.print(f"[red]Project {project_id} not found[/red]")        sys.exit(1)        export_data = {        "exported_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),        "project": state.to_dict()    }        with open(output_file, 'w') as f:        json.dump(export_data, f, indent=2, default=str)        console.print(f"[green]✓ Exported to {output_file}[/green]")@cli.command()@click.option("--project", "-p", help="Show costs for specific project")@click.option("--days", "-d", default=7, help="Days to include in report")@click.pass_contextdef costs(ctx, project: Optional[str], days: int):    """Αναφορά κόστους AI API usage"""        from ai_router import CostTracker        tracker = CostTracker()    report = tracker.get_detailed_report()        if "error" in report:        console.print(f"[yellow]{report['error']}[/yellow]")        return        # Summary    summary = (        f"Total All Time: ${report['total_all_time']:.4f}\n"        f"Today: ${report['today']:.4f}\n"        f"Projected Monthly: ${report['projected_monthly']:.2f}"    )    console.print(Panel(summary, title="Cost Summary"))        # By model    if report.get('by_model'):        console.print("\n[bold]By Model:[/bold]")        table = Table()        table.add_column("Model", style="cyan")        table.add_column("Cost", justify="right")                for model, cost in sorted(report['by_model'].items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):            table.add_row(model, f"${cost:.4f}")                console.print(table)@cli.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.option("--interval", "-i", default=5.0, help="Refresh interval in seconds")@click.pass_contextdef monitor(ctx, project_id: str, interval: float):    """Real-time monitoring dashboard για project"""        sm = StateManager(get_db_path())        if not sm.load_state(project_id):        console.print(f"[red]Project {project_id} not found[/red]")        sys.exit(1)        config = AgentConfig(        project_id=project_id,        description="",        cache_dir=ctx.obj['CONFIG'].get('cache_dir', './cache')    )        console.print(f"[blue]Monitoring {project_id} (refresh every {interval}s)[/blue]")    console.print("[dim]Press Ctrl+C to exit[/dim]\n")        try:        with Live(auto_refresh=False) as live:            while True:                agent = AgentCore(config)                status = agent.get_status()                                # Build display                layout = Layout()                                header = f"[bold]{project_id}[/bold] - {format_status(status['status'])}"                                content = (                    f"Progress: {status['progress']['completed']} tasks\n"                    f"Current: {status['progress']['current_task'] or 'Idle'}\n"                    f"Pending Checkpoints: {status['pending_checkpoints']}\n"                    f"Cost Today: ${status['cost']['today']:.4f} / ${status['cost']['budget']:.2f}"                )                                layout.update(Panel(content, title=header))                live.update(layout)                live.refresh()                                asyncio.run(asyncio.sleep(interval))                    except KeyboardInterrupt:        console.print("\n[dim]Monitoring stopped[/dim]")# Entry pointdef main():    """Entry point για CLI"""    try:        cli()    except Exception as e:        console.print(f"[red]Fatal error: {e}[/red]")        sys.exit(1)if __name__ == "__main__":    main()
6. README.md - Πλήρης Οδηγός Εγκατάστασης & Χρήσης
# Manus-Win11 Agent FrameworkΠροηγμένο AI Agent Framework για Windows 11 με intelligent model routing, persistent state management, και human-in-the-loop capabilities.## 🚀 Χαρακτηριστικά- **Intelligent AI Routing**: Αυτόματη επιλογή βέλτιστου μοντέλου (Kimi, DeepSeek, Claude, GPT)- **Cost Optimization**: Caching, budget tracking, και smart model selection- **Persistent State**: SQLite-based storage με pause/resume capability- **Multi-Channel Notifications**: Telegram & Slack integration- **Human-in-the-Loop**: Checkpoints για user approval σε κρίσιμα σημεία- **CLI Interface**: Πλήρες command line interface για διαχείριση## 📋 Απαιτήσεις- Python 3.8+- Windows 11 (ή Linux/macOS με compatible paths)- API Keys για τουλάχιστον ένα AI provider## ⚙️ Εγκατάσταση### 1. Clone & Setup```bashgit clone <repository>cd manus-win11python -m venv venvvenv\Scripts\activate  # Windows# ή source venv/bin/activate  # Linux/Macpip install -r requirements.txt
2. Configuration
Δημιούργησε .env file:
# AI API Keys (τουλάχιστον ένα απαιτείται)KIMI_API_KEY=your_kimi_key_hereDEEPSEEK_API_KEY=your_deepseek_key_hereANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your_claude_key_hereOPENAI_API_KEY=your_openai_key_here# Notifications (προαιρετικά)TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN=your_telegram_tokenTELEGRAM_CHAT_ID=your_chat_idSLACK_WEBHOOK_URL=your_slack_webhook# Budget & SettingsDAILY_AI_BUDGET=10.0AGENT_DEFAULT_TEMPERATURE=0.7
🎯 Γρήγορο Ξεκίνημα
Επιλογή 1: CLI (Προτείνεται για αρχάριους)
# Δημιούργησε projectpython cli.py create my_project "Analyze sales data" --budget 5.0# Δες statuspython cli.py status my_project# Φτιάξε plan (my_plan.json){  "tasks": [    {      "name": "analyze",      "type": "analysis",      "description": "Analyze data patterns",      "prompt": "Given CSV data with columns date, sales, product..."    }  ]}# Τρέξε τοpython cli.py run my_project my_plan.json
Επιλογή 2: Python API
import asynciofrom agent_core import AgentCore, AgentConfigfrom ai_router import TaskTypeasync def main():    # Configuration    config = AgentConfig(        project_id="data_analysis_001",        description="Customer churn analysis",        daily_budget=10.0    )        # Initialize    agent = AgentCore(config)        # Define plan    plan = [        {            "name": "analyze_data",            "type": TaskType.ANALYSIS,            "description": "Understand data structure",            "prompt": "Analyze this dataset for patterns..."        },        {            "name": "generate_report",            "type": TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,            "description": "Create analysis script",            "prompt": "Generate Python code to visualize trends...",            "checkpoint": True,            "input_prompt": "Review the code. Approve? (yes/no)"        }    ]        # Execute    await agent.execute_plan(plan)        # Check status    print(agent.get_status())asyncio.run(main())
📖 Λεπτομερής Χρήση
Task Configuration
Κάθε task υποστηρίζει:
{    "name": "unique_task_name",           # Μοναδικό identifier    "type": "code_generation",            # TaskType (analysis, code_generation, κλπ)    "description": "What this does",      # Για logs και notifications    "prompt": "AI prompt here...",        # Το κύριο prompt    "system_prompt": "You are an expert...",  # Optional system prompt    "depends_on": ["task1", "task2"],     # Prerequisites    "checkpoint": true,                   # Παύση για user input    "checkpoint_desc": "Review needed",   # Τι περιγράφει το checkpoint    "input_prompt": "Approve? (yes/no)",  # Τι να ρωτήσουμε τον χρήστη    "tool": "save_file",                  # Εργαλείο για post-processing    "temperature": 0.7,                   # Creativity (0.0-1.0)    "max_tokens": 2000,                   # Όριο μήκους απόκρισης    "use_cache": true                     # Χρήση response caching}
Checkpoints & Human-in-the-Loop
Όταν ένα task έχει checkpoint: true, ο agent:
Σταματάει execution
Στέλνει notification (Telegram/Slack)
Περιμένει user input μέσω CLI ή API
Συνεχίζει με βάση την απάντηση
Resolution μέσω CLI:
python cli.py checkpoint my_project checkpoint_id "yes"
Resolution μέσω API:
agent.state_manager.resolve_checkpoint(    project_id="my_project",    checkpoint_id="chk_001",     user_response="yes")
Tool Registration
def my_custom_tool(ai_output: str) -> dict:    """Εκτελεί το παραγόμενο αποτέλεσμα"""    # Π.χ. αποθήκευση αρχείου, εκτέλεση κώδικα, κλπ    result = process(ai_output)    return {"success": True, "result": result}agent.register_tool("my_tool", my_custom_tool)
Monitoring & Debugging
# Real-time monitoringpython cli.py monitor my_project --interval 5.0# Cost reportpython cli.py costs --days 7# Export state for debuggingpython cli.py export my_project debug_state.json
🔧 Advanced Configuration
Custom Model Selection
from ai_router import ModelRouter, TaskTyperouter = ModelRouter(daily_budget=20.0)# Force specific modelresult = await router.call_model(    model_id="deepseek-reasoner",    prompt="Complex reasoning task...",    temperature=0.5)# Auto-select with constraintsmodel = router.select_model(    task_type=TaskType.CODE_GENERATION,    complexity="high",    budget_constraint=0.005)
Notification Templates
from notifications import NotificationManager, Notification, NotificationLevelnotifier = NotificationManager()await notifier.notify(Notification(    title="Custom Alert",    message="Something happened...",    level=NotificationLevel.WARNING,    project_id="my_project",    metadata={"key": "value"}))
📊 Cost Optimization Tips
Use Caching: Ενεργοποίησε use_cache: true σε repetitive tasks
Budget Constraints: Όρισε budget_constraint για simple tasks
Model Tier Selection: Χρησιμοποίησε “fast” models για simple tasks
Checkpoint Strategically: Μόνο όταν πραγματικά χρειάζεται human input
🐛 Troubleshooting
Project stuck in RUNNING status
# Check current taskpython cli.py status my_project# If crashed, state may be inconsistent# Resume manually or delete and recreate
API Key errors
# Verify keys are setecho $KIMI_API_KEY# Test connectivitypython -c "from ai_router import ModelRouter; print('OK')"
Notifications not working
Έλεγξε τα environment variables
Verify Telegram bot έχει ξεκινήσει conversation με σένα
Check Slack webhook URL είναι valid

## 7. **requirements.txt**
aiohttp>=3.8.0 click>=8.0.0 rich>=13.0.0 python-dotenv>=1.0.0
Αυτό είναι το πλήρως ενημερωμένο framework με:- **Πλήρη documentation** σε κάθε αρχείο- **Docstrings** με παραδείγματα χρήσης- **Type hints** για better IDE support- **Error handling** και logging- **CLI** με όλες τις λειτουργίες- **README** με οδηγίες εγκατάστασηςΘέλεις να προσθέσω κάτι άλλο ή να εξηγήσω περισσότερο κάποιο κομμάτι;---**User:**Πρότεινε βελτιώσεις και προσθήκες δυνατοτήτων---**Kimi:**Θα προτείνω σημαντικές βελτιώσεις και νέες δυνατότητες για το Manus-Win11 Agent Framework, οργανωμένες σε κατηγορίες:## 1. **Security & Safety Module** (`security.py`)```python#!/usr/bin/env python3"""security.py - Security & Safety Layer για AgentΛειτουργίες:------------1. Sandboxed code execution (restricted Python)2. Prompt injection detection3. Sensitive data filtering (PII, API keys)4. Resource limits (CPU, memory, time)5. Audit logging για όλες τις ενέργειες6. Approval gates για high-risk operationsΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from security import SecurityManager, RiskLevel>>> >>> security = SecurityManager()>>> >>> # Έλεγχος prompt για injection>>> is_safe, reason = security.check_prompt(user_input)>>> if not is_safe:>>>     raise SecurityException(f"Unsafe prompt: {reason}")>>> >>> # Sandboxed execution>>> result = security.execute_code(>>>     code=ai_generated_code,>>>     risk_level=RiskLevel.MEDIUM,>>>     timeout=30>>> )"""import astimport resourceimport signalimport sysimport reimport loggingfrom enum import Enumfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List, Tuplefrom contextlib import contextmanagerimport multiprocessingimport tempfileimport oslogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class RiskLevel(Enum):    """Επίπεδα ρίσκου για operations"""    LOW = "low"        # Ασφαλές, no approval needed    MEDIUM = "medium"  # Χρειάζεται logging    HIGH = "high"      # Χρειάζεται explicit approval    CRITICAL = "critical"  # Απαγορεύεται by default@dataclassclass SecurityPolicy:    """Policy για security decisions"""    max_code_execution_time: int = 30  # seconds    max_memory_mb: int = 512    allow_network: bool = False    allow_file_write: bool = False    allowed_modules: List[str] = None        def __post_init__(self):        if self.allowed_modules is None:            self.allowed_modules = [                'math', 'random', 'datetime', 'json', 're',                 'collections', 'itertools', 'statistics'            ]class SecurityManager:    """    Κεντρικός security manager για τον agent.        Παρέχει:    - Code sandboxing με resource limits    - Prompt injection detection    - PII filtering    - Audit trail    """        # Patterns για prompt injection    INJECTION_PATTERNS = [        r'ignore\s+(previous|above|earlier)',        r'disregard\s+(instructions|rules)',        r'forget\s+(you are|your role)',        r'system\s*prompt',        r'you\s+are\s+now',        r'new\s+role\s*:',        r'DAN\s*$Do\s+Anything\s+Now$',        r'jailbreak',        r'$$\s*system\s*$$',        r'<\s*system\s*>',    ]        # PII patterns    PII_PATTERNS = {        'email': r'\b[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z|a-z]{2,}\b',        'phone': r'\b\d{3}[-.]?\d{3}[-.]?\d{4}\b',        'ssn': r'\b\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}\b',        'credit_card': r'\b(?:\d[ -]*?){13,16}\b',        'api_key': r'\b(sk-|pk-)[a-zA-Z0-9]{32,}\b',    }        def __init__(self, policy: Optional[SecurityPolicy] = None):        self.policy = policy or SecurityPolicy()        self.audit_log: List[Dict] = []        def check_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:        """        Έλεγχος prompt για injection attempts.                Returns:            (is_safe, reason) - Αν unsafe, reason εξηγεί γιατί        """        prompt_lower = prompt.lower()                for pattern in self.INJECTION_PATTERNS:            if re.search(pattern, prompt_lower, re.IGNORECASE):                reason = f"Potential injection detected: {pattern}"                self._audit("PROMPT_INJECTION_BLOCKED", prompt[:100], reason)                return False, reason                return True, None        def sanitize_output(self, text: str) -> str:        """        Αφαίρεση PII από output.                Returns:            Sanitized text με [REDACTED] αντί για PII        """        sanitized = text        for pii_type, pattern in self.PII_PATTERNS.items():            sanitized = re.sub(pattern, f'[REDACTED_{pii_type.upper()}]', sanitized)        return sanitized        def execute_code(self,                     code: str,                     risk_level: RiskLevel = RiskLevel.MEDIUM,                    timeout: Optional[int] = None,                    context: Optional[Dict] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """        Ασφαλής εκτέλεση Python code σε sandbox.                Args:            code: Python code προς εκτέλεση            risk_level: Επίπεδο ρίσκου            timeout: Max execution time            context: Variables να είναι available στο namespace                Returns:            Dict με result ή error info        """        if risk_level == RiskLevel.CRITICAL:            return {                "success": False,                "error": "CRITICAL risk code execution not allowed"            }                if risk_level == RiskLevel.HIGH:            # Θα έπρεπε να έχει ήδη πάρει approval            self._audit("HIGH_RISK_EXECUTION", code[:200], "Executing high-risk code")                timeout = timeout or self.policy.max_code_execution_time                try:            # Validate syntax first            ast.parse(code)                        # Check for dangerous operations            if not self._is_code_safe(code):                return {                    "success": False,                    "error": "Code contains unsafe operations"                }                        # Execute in subprocess for isolation            result = self._execute_in_subprocess(code, timeout, context or {})                        self._audit("CODE_EXECUTED", code[:200], f"Success: {result.get('success')}")            return result                    except SyntaxError as e:            return {"success": False, "error": f"Syntax error: {e}"}        except Exception as e:            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}        def _is_code_safe(self, code: str) -> bool:        """Static analysis για dangerous operations"""        dangerous = ['__import__', 'eval', 'exec', 'compile', 'open', 'os.system']        tree = ast.parse(code)                for node in ast.walk(tree):            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):                if isinstance(node.func, ast.Name) and node.func.id in dangerous:                    return False            if isinstance(node, ast.Import) or isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):                for alias in node.names:                    module = alias.name.split('.')[0]                    if module not in self.policy.allowed_modules:                        logger.warning(f"Disallowed import: {module}")                        return False                return True        def _execute_in_subprocess(self,                                code: str,                                timeout: int,                               context: Dict) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Εκτέλεση σε ξεχωριστό process με resource limits"""                def target(queue, code, context):            try:                # Resource limits                resource.setrlimit(resource.RLIMIT_CPU, (timeout, timeout))                resource.setrlimit(resource.RLIMIT_AS,                                  (self.policy.max_memory_mb * 1024 * 1024,                                   self.policy.max_memory_mb * 1024 * 1024))                                # Create restricted namespace                safe_globals = {                    "__builtins__": {                        name: __builtins__[name]                         for name in ['True', 'False', 'None', 'abs', 'all', 'any',                                   'len', 'max', 'min', 'sum', 'range', 'enumerate',                                   'zip', 'map', 'filter', 'sorted', 'reversed']                    }                }                                # Add allowed modules                for module_name in self.policy.allowed_modules:                    try:                        safe_globals[module_name] = __import__(module_name)                    except ImportError:                        pass                                safe_globals.update(context)                                exec(code, safe_globals)                                # Get result if any                result = safe_globals.get('_result', None)                queue.put({"success": True, "result": result})                            except Exception as e:                queue.put({"success": False, "error": str(e)})                queue = multiprocessing.Queue()        process = multiprocessing.Process(target=target, args=(queue, code, context))        process.start()        process.join(timeout + 5)  # Extra buffer                if process.is_alive():            process.terminate()            process.join()            return {"success": False, "error": "Execution timeout"}                if not queue.empty():            return queue.get()                return {"success": False, "error": "Unknown execution error"}        def _audit(self, action: str, details: str, result: str):        """Καταγραφή audit log"""        entry = {            "timestamp": __import__('datetime').datetime.now().isoformat(),            "action": action,            "details": details,            "result": result        }        self.audit_log.append(entry)        logger.info(f"SECURITY: {action} - {result}")        def get_audit_log(self) -> List[Dict]:        """Λήψη όλων των audit entries"""        return self.audit_log.copy()        def require_approval(self,                         action: str,                         details: str,                        risk_level: RiskLevel = RiskLevel.HIGH) -> bool:        """        Ζήτηση explicit approval για high-risk action.                Returns:            True αν εγκρίθηκε, False αν απορρίφθηκε        """        self._audit("APPROVAL_REQUESTED", action, details)                # Σε CLI mode, ρωτάμε τον χρήστη        print(f"\n{'='*50}")        print(f"APPROVAL REQUIRED - {risk_level.value.upper()} RISK")        print(f"Action: {action}")        print(f"Details: {details}")        print(f"{'='*50}")                response = input("Approve? (yes/no): ").lower().strip()        approved = response == 'yes'                self._audit("APPROVAL_" + ("GRANTED" if approved else "DENIED"),                    action, details)                return approved
2. Plugin System (plugins.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""plugins.py - Extensible Plugin SystemΛειτουργίες:------------1. Dynamic plugin loading από directories2. Hook system για customization3. Plugin API για third-party extensions4. Version management και dependencies5. Sandboxed plugin executionΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from plugins import PluginManager>>> >>> pm = PluginManager("./plugins")>>> pm.load_all()>>> >>> # Κλήση hook>>> results = pm.execute_hook("pre_generation", prompt=data)>>> >>> # Εγγραφή custom plugin>>> @pm.register_plugin("my_plugin")>>> class MyPlugin:>>>     def pre_generation(self, prompt):>>>         return modified_prompt"""import importlib.utilimport inspectimport jsonimport loggingfrom abc import ABC, abstractmethodfrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Type, Callable, Optionalfrom dataclasses import dataclasslogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass PluginInfo:    """Metadata για plugin"""    name: str    version: str    author: str    description: str    hooks: List[str]    dependencies: List[str]class PluginInterface(ABC):    """Base class για όλα τα plugins"""        @property    @abstractmethod    def info(self) -> PluginInfo:        """Επιστροφή plugin metadata"""        pass        def initialize(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):        """Called όταν φορτώνεται το plugin"""        pass        def shutdown(self):        """Called όταν αφαιρείται το plugin"""        passclass PluginManager:    """    Manager για dynamic plugin loading και execution.        Hooks διαθέσιμα:    - pre_generation: Πριν το AI generation    - post_generation: Μετά το AI generation    - pre_tool_execution: Πριν την εκτέλεση εργαλείου    - post_tool_execution: Μετά την εκτέλεση εργαλείου    - on_checkpoint: Όταν δημιουργείται checkpoint    - on_error: Όταν συμβαίνει error    """        HOOKS = [        'pre_generation', 'post_generation',        'pre_tool_execution', 'post_tool_execution',        'on_checkpoint', 'on_error', 'on_completion'    ]        def __init__(self, plugin_dirs: List[str]):        self.plugin_dirs = [Path(d) for d in plugin_dirs]        self.plugins: Dict[str, PluginInterface] = {}        self.hooks: Dict[str, List[Callable]] = {h: [] for h in self.HOOKS}        def load_all(self):        """Φόρτωση όλων των plugins από directories"""        for directory in self.plugin_dirs:            if not directory.exists():                continue                        for plugin_file in directory.glob("*.py"):                if plugin_file.name.startswith("_"):                    continue                self._load_plugin_file(plugin_file)        def _load_plugin_file(self, filepath: Path):        """Φόρτωση single plugin από file"""        try:            spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(                filepath.stem, filepath            )            module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)            spec.loader.exec_module(module)                        # Βρες Plugin classes            for name, obj in inspect.getmembers(module):                if (inspect.isclass(obj) and                     issubclass(obj, PluginInterface) and                     obj != PluginInterface):                                        instance = obj()                    self.register_plugin(instance)                            except Exception as e:            logger.error(f"Failed to load plugin {filepath}: {e}")        def register_plugin(self, plugin: PluginInterface):        """Manual registration ενός plugin instance"""        info = plugin.info                # Check dependencies        for dep in info.dependencies:            if dep not in self.plugins:                raise Exception(f"Plugin {info.name} requires {dep}")                # Register hooks        for hook_name in info.hooks:            if hook_name in self.HOOKS:                handler = getattr(plugin, hook_name, None)                if handler and callable(handler):                    self.hooks[hook_name].append(handler)                self.plugins[info.name] = plugin        plugin.initialize({})                logger.info(f"Registered plugin: {info.name} v{info.version}")        def execute_hook(self, hook_name: str, **kwargs) -> List[Any]:        """        Εκτέλεση όλων των handlers για ένα hook.                Returns:            Λίστα αποτελεσμάτων από κάθε plugin        """        if hook_name not in self.HOOKS:            return []                results = []        for handler in self.hooks[hook_name]:            try:                result = handler(**kwargs)                results.append(result)            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"Hook {hook_name} failed: {e}")                return results        def get_plugin(self, name: str) -> Optional[PluginInterface]:        """Λήψη plugin by name"""        return self.plugins.get(name)        def list_plugins(self) -> List[PluginInfo]:        """Λίστα όλων των loaded plugins"""        return [p.info for p in self.plugins.values()]        def unload_plugin(self, name: str):        """Αφαίρεση plugin"""        if name in self.plugins:            self.plugins[name].shutdown()            del self.plugins[name]                        # Remove from hooks            for hook_list in self.hooks.values():                hook_list[:] = [h for h in hook_list                                if getattr(h, '__self__', None) not in self.plugins.values()]# Παράδειγμα Pluginclass ExamplePlugin(PluginInterface):    """Παράδειγμα plugin για documentation"""        @property    def info(self) -> PluginInfo:        return PluginInfo(            name="example",            version="1.0.0",            author="Developer",            description="Example plugin showing the interface",            hooks=["pre_generation", "post_generation"],            dependencies=[]        )        def pre_generation(self, prompt: str, **kwargs) -> str:        """Τροποποίηση prompt πριν το generation"""        # Π.χ. προσθήκη context        return f"[Enhanced by plugin]\n{prompt}"        def post_generation(self, response: str, **kwargs) -> str:        """Τροποποίηση response μετά το generation"""        return response
3. Vector Memory & RAG (memory.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""memory.py - Vector-based Long-term Memory & RAGΛειτουργίες:------------1. Vector storage για embeddings (ChromaDB/FAISS)2. Semantic search σε προηγούμενα projects3. RAG (Retrieval Augmented Generation)4. Conversation memory management5. Knowledge base integrationΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from memory import VectorMemory>>> >>> memory = VectorMemory()>>> >>> # Αποθήκευση experience>>> memory.add_experience(>>>     project_id="proj1",>>>     content="Used pandas for large CSV processing",>>>     tags=["python", "pandas", "performance"]>>> )>>> >>> # Αναζήτηση σχετικών>>> relevant = memory.search("How to process large CSV files?", k=3)>>> >>> # RAG-enhanced generation>>> context = memory.get_rag_context("Current task description")"""import hashlibimport jsonimport loggingfrom typing import List, Dict, Any, Optionalfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom datetime import datetimefrom pathlib import Pathlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)try:    import chromadb    from chromadb.config import Settings    CHROMADB_AVAILABLE = Trueexcept ImportError:    CHROMADB_AVAILABLE = False    logger.warning("ChromaDB not available, using fallback storage")@dataclassclass MemoryEntry:    """Entry στη vector memory"""    id: str    content: str    embedding: Optional[List[float]]    metadata: Dict[str, Any]    timestamp: datetime    project_id: str    tags: List[str]class VectorMemory:    """    Vector-based memory system για RAG και experience replay.        Χρησιμοποιεί ChromaDB για vector storage ή JSON fallback.    """        def __init__(self,                  storage_dir: str = "./memory",                 embedding_model: str = "default"):        self.storage_dir = Path(storage_dir)        self.storage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)        self.embedding_model = embedding_model                if CHROMADB_AVAILABLE:            self.client = chromadb.Client(Settings(                chroma_db_impl="duckdb+parquet",                persist_directory=str(self.storage_dir)            ))            self.collection = self.client.get_or_create_collection(                name="agent_memory",                metadata={"hnsw:space": "cosine"}            )        else:            self.fallback_storage: List[MemoryEntry] = []            self._load_fallback()        def add_experience(self,                      content: str,                      project_id: str,                      tags: Optional[List[str]] = None,                      metadata: Optional[Dict] = None):        """        Προσθήκη νέας εμπειρίας στη μνήμη.                Args:            content: Το κείμενο της εμπειρίας            project_id: ID του project            tags: Κατηγορίες για filtering            metadata: Extra info (success, duration, κλπ)        """        entry_id = hashlib.md5(            f"{project_id}:{content}:{datetime.now()}".encode()        ).hexdigest()                entry = MemoryEntry(            id=entry_id,            content=content,            embedding=None,  # Θα υπολογιστεί αν χρειάζεται            metadata=metadata or {},            timestamp=datetime.now(),            project_id=project_id,            tags=tags or []        )                if CHROMADB_AVAILABLE:            self.collection.add(                documents=[content],                metadatas=[{                    "project_id": project_id,                    "tags": json.dumps(tags or []),                    "timestamp": entry.timestamp.isoformat(),                    **metadata                }],                ids=[entry_id]            )        else:            self.fallback_storage.append(entry)            self._save_fallback()                logger.info(f"Added memory entry: {entry_id[:8]}...")        def search(self,                query: str,                k: int = 5,               project_filter: Optional[str] = None,               tag_filter: Optional[List[str]] = None) -> List[Dict]:        """        Semantic search στη μνήμη.                Args:            query: Το ερώτημα            k: Αριθμός αποτελεσμάτων            project_filter: Φιλτράρισμα ανά project            tag_filter: Φιλτράρισμα ανά tags                Returns:            Λίστα από dictionaries με content, score, metadata        """        if CHROMADB_AVAILABLE:            where = {}            if project_filter:                where["project_id"] = project_filter                        results = self.collection.query(                query_texts=[query],                n_results=k,                where=where if where else None            )                        entries = []            for i, doc in enumerate(results['documents'][0]):                metadata = results['metadatas'][0][i]                # Parse tags από JSON                if 'tags' in metadata:                    metadata['tags'] = json.loads(metadata['tags'])                                entries.append({                    "content": doc,                    "score": results['distances'][0][i] if results['distances'] else 0,                    "metadata": metadata,                    "id": results['ids'][0][i]                })                        return entries                else:            # Fallback: simple keyword matching            query_lower = query.lower()            scored = []                        for entry in self.fallback_storage:                score = 0                                # Project filter                if project_filter and entry.project_id != project_filter:                    continue                                # Tag filter                if tag_filter and not any(t in entry.tags for t in tag_filter):                    continue                                # Simple scoring                content_lower = entry.content.lower()                words = query_lower.split()                score = sum(1 for w in words if w in content_lower)                                if score > 0:                    scored.append((score, entry))                        scored.sort(reverse=True)            return [                {                    "content": e.content,                    "score": s,                    "metadata": e.metadata,                    "id": e.id                }                for s, e in scored[:k]            ]        def get_rag_context(self,                        current_task: str,                       k: int = 3) -> str:        """        Δημιουργία RAG context για enhanced generation.                Args:            current_task: Περιγραφή τρέχοντος task            k: Πόσες σχετικές εμπειρίες να συμπεριλάβει                Returns:            Formatted context string για προσθήκη στο prompt        """        relevant = self.search(current_task, k=k)                if not relevant:            return ""                context_parts = ["Relevant previous experiences:"]                for i, entry in enumerate(relevant, 1):            context_parts.append(                f"{i}. {entry['content']}\n"                f"   (Project: {entry['metadata'].get('project_id', 'unknown')}, "                f"Score: {entry['score']:.2f})"            )                return "\n\n".join(context_parts)        def get_project_experiences(self, project_id: str) -> List[Dict]:        """Λήψη όλων των experiences για συγκεκριμένο project"""        if CHROMADB_AVAILABLE:            results = self.collection.get(                where={"project_id": project_id}            )            return [                {                    "content": doc,                    "metadata": meta,                    "id": id_                }                for doc, meta, id_ in zip(                    results['documents'],                    results['metadatas'],                    results['ids']                )            ]        else:            return [                {                    "content": e.content,                    "metadata": e.metadata,                    "id": e.id                }                for e in self.fallback_storage                if e.project_id == project_id            ]        def _load_fallback(self):        """Φόρτωση fallback storage από disk"""        fallback_file = self.storage_dir / "fallback_memory.json"        if fallback_file.exists():            try:                data = json.loads(fallback_file.read_text())                self.fallback_storage = [                    MemoryEntry(                        id=e['id'],                        content=e['content'],                        embedding=e.get('embedding'),                        metadata=e.get('metadata', {}),                        timestamp=datetime.fromisoformat(e['timestamp']),                        project_id=e['project_id'],                        tags=e.get('tags', [])                    )                    for e in data                ]            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"Failed to load fallback memory: {e}")        def _save_fallback(self):        """Αποθήκευση fallback storage σε disk"""        fallback_file = self.storage_dir / "fallback_memory.json"        data = [            {                'id': e.id,                'content': e.content,                'metadata': e.metadata,                'timestamp': e.timestamp.isoformat(),                'project_id': e.project_id,                'tags': e.tags            }            for e in self.fallback_storage        ]        fallback_file.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2))
4. Web Dashboard (dashboard.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""dashboard.py - Web Dashboard για Monitoring & ControlΛειτουργίες:------------1. Real-time project monitoring (WebSocket)2. Checkpoint resolution μέσω web UI3. Cost visualization (charts)4. Log viewing και filtering5. Project management (create, delete, configure)6. Mobile-responsive designΤρέξιμο:--------python dashboard.py --port 8080Οδηγίες Πρόσβασης:------------------- Local: http://localhost:8080- Network: http://your-ip:8080- Default: Δεν απαιτείται authentication (προσθέστε αν χρειάζεται)Dependencies:-------------- fastapi- uvicorn- websockets- jinja2"""import asyncioimport jsonimport loggingfrom datetime import datetimefrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, Any, Listtry:    from fastapi import FastAPI, WebSocket, WebSocketDisconnect    from fastapi.responses import HTMLResponse    from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles    import uvicorn    DASHBOARD_AVAILABLE = Trueexcept ImportError:    DASHBOARD_AVAILABLE = False    logging.warning("Dashboard dependencies not available")from agent_core import AgentCore, #ef4444; color: #fff; }        .metric {             display: flex;             justify-content: space-between;             padding: 0.75rem 0;            border-bottom: 1px solid #334155;        }        .metric:last-child { border-bottom: none; }        .btn {            background: #667eea;            color: white;            border: none;            padding: 0.75rem 1.5rem;            border-radius: 8px;            cursor: pointer;            font-size: 1rem;            transition: background 0.2s;        }        .btn:hover { background: #5568d3; }        .btn-danger { background: #ef4444; }        .btn-danger:hover { background: #dc2626; }        .logs {            background: #0f172a;            border-radius: 8px;            padding: 1rem;            font-family: 'Courier New', monospace;            font-size: 0.875rem;            max-height: 400px;            overflow-y: auto;        }        .log-entry { margin-bottom: 0.5rem; }        .log-time { color: #64748b; }        .checkpoint-form {            display: flex;            gap: 0.5rem;            margin-top: 1rem;        }        .checkpoint-form input {            flex: 1;            background: #0f172a;            border: 1px solid #334155;            color: white;            padding: 0.75rem;            border-radius: 8px;        }        #connection-status {            position: fixed;            top: 1rem;            right: 1rem;            padding: 0.5rem 1rem;            border-radius: 8px;            font-size: 0.875rem;        }        .connected { background: #10b981; }        .disconnected { background: #ef4444; }    </style></head><body>    <div class="header">        <h1>🤖 Manus-Win11 Agent Dashboard</h1>        <p>Real-time monitoring and control</p>    </div>        <div id="connection-status" class="disconnected">Disconnected</div>        <div class="container">        <div class="grid" id="projects-grid">            <!-- Projects loaded dynamically -->        </div>    </div>    <script>        const ws = new WebSocket(`ws://${window.location.host}/ws`);        const statusEl = document.getElementById('connection-status');                ws.onopen = () => {            statusEl.textContent = 'Connected';            statusEl.className = 'connected';        };                ws.onclose = () => {            statusEl.textContent = 'Disconnected';            statusEl.className = 'disconnected';        };                ws.onmessage = (event) => {            const data = JSON.parse(event.data);            updateDashboard(data);        };                function updateDashboard(data) {            const grid = document.getElementById('projects-grid');            grid.innerHTML = '';                        data.projects.forEach(project => {                const card = createProjectCard(project);                grid.appendChild(card);            });        }                function createProjectCard(project) {            const div = document.createElement('div');            div.className = 'card';                        const statusClass = `status-${project.status}`;                        div.innerHTML = `                <h3>${project.id}</h3>                <span class="status-badge ${statusClass}">${project.status}</span>                                <div class="metric">                    <span>Description</span>                    <span>${project.description || 'N/A'}</span>                </div>                                <div class="metric">                    <span>Progress</span>                    <span>${project.completed_tasks}/${project.total_tasks} tasks</span>                </div>                                <div class="metric">                    <span>Current Task</span>                    <span>${project.current_task || 'None'}</span>                </div>                                <div class="metric">                    <span>Cost Today</span>                    <span>$${project.cost_today.toFixed(4)} / $${project.budget}</span>                </div>                                ${project.pending_checkpoints > 0 ? `                    <div style="margin-top: 1rem; padding: 1rem; background: #451a03; border-radius: 8px;">                        <strong>⏸️ Checkpoint Waiting</strong>                        <p style="margin: 0.5rem 0; font-size: 0.875rem;">                            ${project.checkpoint_description || 'Input required'}                        </p>                        <div class="checkpoint-form">                            <input type="text" id="cp-${project.id}"                                    placeholder="Your response...">                            <button class="btn" onclick="resolveCheckpoint('${project.id}')">                                Submit                            </button>                        </div>                    </div>                ` : ''}                                <div style="margin-top: 1rem;">                    <button class="btn" onclick="viewLogs('${project.id}')">View Logs</button>                    <button class="btn btn-danger" onclick="deleteProject('${project.id}')">                        Delete                    </button>                </div>            `;                        return div;        }                function resolveCheckpoint(projectId) {            const input = document.getElementById(`cp-${projectId}`);            const response = input.value;                        fetch(`/api/checkpoint/${projectId}`, {                method: 'POST',                headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},                body: JSON.stringify({response: response})            });                        input.value = '';        }                function viewLogs(projectId) {            window.open(`/logs/${projectId}`, '_blank');        }                function deleteProject(projectId) {            if (confirm(`Delete project ${projectId}?`)) {                fetch(`/api/project/${projectId}`, {method: 'DELETE'})                    .then(() => location.reload());            }        }    </script></body></html>"""class DashboardServer:    """FastAPI server για web dashboard"""        def __init__(self, db_path: str = "./projects.db", port: int = 8080):        if not DASHBOARD_AVAILABLE:            raise ImportError("Dashboard requires: pip install fastapi uvicorn")                self.db_path = db_path        self.port = port        self.app = FastAPI(title="Manus-Win11 Dashboard")        self.state_manager = StateManager(db_path)        self.active_connections: List[WebSocket] = []                self._setup_routes()        def _setup_routes(self):        """Ορισμός API routes"""                @self.app.get("/", response_class=HTMLResponse)        async def dashboard():            return DASHBOARD_HTML                @self.app.websocket("/ws")        async def websocket_endpoint(websocket: WebSocket):            await websocket.accept()            self.active_connections.append(websocket)            try:                while True:                    # Send updates every 2 seconds                    data = self._get_dashboard_data()                    await websocket.send_json(data)                    await asyncio.sleep(2)            except WebSocketDisconnect:                self.active_connections.remove(websocket)                @self.app.post("/api/checkpoint/{project_id}")        async def resolve_checkpoint(project_id: str, data: Dict[str, str]):            """Resolve checkpoint μέσω API"""            pending = self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(project_id)            if pending:                # Resolve most recent                self.state_manager.resolve_checkpoint(                    project_id, pending[-1].id, data.get('response', '')                )                return {"success": True}            return {"success": False, "error": "No pending checkpoints"}                @self.app.delete("/api/project/{project_id}")        async def delete_project(project_id: str):            """Διαγραφή project"""            self.state_manager.delete_state(project_id)            return {"success": True}                @self.app.get("/logs/{project_id}")        async def get_logs(project_id: str):            """Λήψη logs για project"""            state = self.state_manager.load_state(project_id)            if not state:                return {"error": "Not found"}                        logs = {                "project_id": project_id,                "error_log": state.error_log,                "checkpoints": [                    {                        "id": cp.id,                        "description": cp.description,                        "resolved": cp.resolved,                        "response": cp.user_response                    }                    for cp in state.checkpoints                ]            }            return logs        def _get_dashboard_data(self) -> Dict:        """Συγκέντρωση δεδομένων για dashboard"""        projects = []                for proj in self.state_manager.list_projects():            state = self.state_manager.load_state(proj["project_id"])            if not state:                continue                        pending = self.state_manager.get_pending_checkpoints(proj["project_id"])                        # Get cost info            from ai_router import CostTracker            tracker = CostTracker()            cost_stats = tracker.get_stats()                        projects.append({                "id": proj["project_id"],                "status": state.status.value,                "description": state.metadata.get("description", ""),                "completed_tasks": len(state.completed_tasks),                "total_tasks": len(state.metadata.get("plan", [])),                "current_task": state.current_task,                "cost_today": cost_stats["today"],                "budget": cost_stats["budget"],                "pending_checkpoints": len(pending),                "checkpoint_description": pending[-1].description if pending else None            })                return {"projects": projects, "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()}        def run(self):        """Εκκίνηση server"""        uvicorn.run(self.app, host="0.0.0.0", port=self.port)def start_dashboard(port: int = 8080, db_path: str = 5. Enhanced Agent Core (agent_core_v2.py) - Ενσωμάτωση όλων
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""agent_core_v2.py - Enhanced Agent με όλες τις νέες δυνατότητεςΒελτιώσεις από v1:------------------1. Security integration (sandboxed execution)2. Plugin system (extensible hooks)3. Vector memory (RAG support)4. Parallel task execution5. Advanced error recovery (retry with different models)6. Cost optimization (adaptive model selection)7. Web dashboard integration"""import asyncioimport loggingfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optionalfrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom agent_core import AgentCore as BaseAgentCore, AgentConfig as BaseAgentConfigfrom security import SecurityManager, RiskLevelfrom plugins import PluginManagerfrom memory import VectorMemoryfrom ai_router import ModelRouter, TaskTypelogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass EnhancedAgentConfig(BaseAgentConfig):    """Extended configuration"""    # Security    enable_security: bool = True    security_policy: Optional[Dict] = None        # Plugins    plugin_dirs: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)        # Memory    enable_memory: bool = True    memory_dir: str = "./memory"        # Execution    max_parallel_tasks: int = 3    enable_adaptive_routing: bool = Trueclass EnhancedAgentCore(BaseAgentCore):    """    Ενισχυμένος Agent με security, plugins, και memory.    """        def __init__(self, config: EnhancedAgentConfig):        super().__init__(config)        self.config = config                # Initialize subsystems        self.security = SecurityManager() if config.enable_security else None        self.plugins = PluginManager(config.plugin_dirs) if config.plugin_dirs else None        self.memory = VectorMemory(config.memory_dir) if config.enable_memory else None                if self.plugins:            self.plugins.load_all()                logger.info("EnhancedAgentCore initialized")        async def execute_plan(self, plan: List[Dict[str, Any]]):        """        Εκτέλεση με όλα τα enhancements.        """        # Security check        if self.security:            for task in plan:                prompt = task.get("prompt", "")                is_safe, reason = self.security.check_prompt(prompt)                if not is_safe:                    logger.error(f"Security check failed for task {task['name']}: {reason}")                    raise SecurityError(f"Task {task['name']} blocked: {reason}")                # Plugin hook: pre_execution        if self.plugins:            modified_plan = []            for task in plan:                results = self.plugins.execute_hook("pre_execution", task=task)                # Use last modification if any                if results and results[-1]:                    modified_plan.append(results[-1])                else:                    modified_plan.append(task)            plan = modified_plan                # Add RAG context αν υπάρχει memory        if self.memory:            for task in plan:                rag_context = self.memory.get_rag_context(task.get("description", ""))                if rag_context:                    original_prompt = task.get("prompt", "")                    task["prompt"] = f"{rag_context}\n\n---\n\n{original_prompt}"                # Execute with parent class        try:            await super().execute_plan(plan)                        # Save successful experience            if self.memory:                self.memory.add_experience(                    content=f"Successfully executed plan with {len(plan)} tasks",                    project_id=self.config.project_id,                    tags=["success", "plan_execution"],                    metadata={"task_count": len(plan)}                )                        except Exception as e:            # Save failure experience            if self.memory:                self.memory.add_experience(                    content=f"Plan failed: {str(e)}",                    project_id=self.config.project_id,                    tags=["failure", "error"],                    metadata={"error": str(e)}                )            raise                # Plugin hook: post_execution        if self.plugins:            self.plugins.execute_hook("post_execution", project_id=self.config.project_id)        async def _execute_task(self, task: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:        """Override με security και adaptive routing"""                # Adaptive model selection based on past performance        if self.config.enable_adaptive_routing and self.memory:            similar = self.memory.search(                task.get("description", ""),                k=1,                tag_filter=["success"]            )            if similar and similar[0]["score"] > 0.8:                # Previous similar task succeeded, maybe use cheaper model                logger.info("Using adaptive routing based on memory")                # Security check for tool execution        if "tool" in task and self.security:            tool_name = task["tool"]            risk_level = task.get("risk_level", RiskLevel.MEDIUM)                        if risk_level in [RiskLevel.HIGH, RiskLevel.CRITICAL]:                approved = self.security.require_approval(                    f"Execute tool: {tool_name}",                    f"Task: {task.get('description', 'N/A')}",                    risk_level                )                if not approved:                    logger.warning(f"Tool execution denied by user: {tool_name}")                    return False                return await super()._execute_task(task)        def register_secure_tool(self,                             name: str,                             handler: callable,                            risk_level: RiskLevel = RiskLevel.MEDIUM):        """        Εγγραφή tool με automatic security wrapping.        """        def secure_handler(input_data: str):            # Sanitize input            if self.security:                input_data = self.security.sanitize_output(input_data)                        # Execute            result = handler(input_data)                        # Sanitize output            if self.security and isinstance(result, str):                result = self.security.sanitize_output(result)                        return result                self.register_tool(name, secure_handler)        logger.info(f"Registered secure tool: {name} (risk: {risk_level.value})")class SecurityError(Exception):    """Custom exception για security violations"""    pass# Migration guide από v1def migrate_from_v1(old_config: Dict) -> EnhancedAgentConfig:    """Βοηθητική για migration από παλιά config"""    return EnhancedAgentConfig(        project_id=old_config["project_id"],        description=old_config["description"],        daily_budget=old_config.get("daily_budget", 10.0),        enable_security=True,        enable_memory=True,        plugin_dirs=["./plugins"]    )
6. CLI Extensions (cli_extensions.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""cli_extensions.py - Επιπλέον CLI εντολές για advanced features"""import clickfrom rich.console import Consolefrom rich.table import Tableconsole = Console()@click.group()def advanced():    """Advanced commands για power users"""    pass@advanced.command()@click.argument("project_id")@click.option("--security-level", default="medium",               type=click.Choice(["low", "medium", "high", "critical"]))def analyze_security(project_id: str, security_level: str):    """Security analysis ενός project"""    from security import SecurityManager    sm = SecurityManager()        # Load audit log    logs = sm.get_audit_log()        table = Table(title=f"Security Audit: {project_id}")    table.add_column("Time", style="dim")    table.add_column("Action", style="cyan")    table.add_column("Result")        for entry in logs:        table.add_row(            entry["timestamp"][:19],            entry["action"],            entry["result"][:50]        )        console.print(table)@advanced.command()@click.argument("query")@click.option("--k", default=5, help="Number of results")def search_memory(query: str, k: int):    """Αναζήτηση στη vector memory"""    from memory import VectorMemory        mem = VectorMemory()    results = mem.search(query, k=k)        for i, r in enumerate(results, 1):        console.print(f"\n[bold]{i}.[/bold] Score: {r['score']:.2f}")        console.print(f"   {r['content'][:200]}...")        console.print(f"   [dim]Project: {r['metadata'].get('project_id')}[/dim]")@advanced.command()@click.option("--port", default=8080)def dashboard(port: int):    """Εκκίνηση web dashboard"""    from dashboard import start_dashboard    start_dashboard(port=port)@advanced.command()def plugins():    """List loaded plugins"""    from plugins import PluginManager        pm = PluginManager(["./plugins"])    pm.load_all()        table = Table(title="Loaded Plugins")    table.add_column("Name", style="cyan")    table.add_column("Version")    table.add_column("Hooks")        for info in pm.list_plugins():        table.add_row(info.name, info.version, ", ".join(info.hooks))        console.print(table)# Προσθήκη στο main CLIdef register_advanced_commands(cli_group):    """Εγγραφή advanced commands στο main CLI"""    cli_group.add_command(advanced)
7. Performance Monitor (performance.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""performance.py - Performance Monitoring & OptimizationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Real-time metrics collection (CPU, memory, latency)2. Bottleneck detection3. Automatic optimization suggestions4. Performance regression detection5. Resource usage forecasting"""import timeimport psutilimport asynciofrom dataclasses import dataclass, asdictfrom typing import Dict, List, Optionalfrom datetime import datetimefrom collections import dequeimport json@dataclassclass PerformanceMetrics:    timestamp: float    cpu_percent: float    memory_mb: float    latency_ms: float    tokens_per_second: float    cost_per_token: floatclass PerformanceMonitor:    """Monitor και optimizer για agent performance"""        def __init__(self, window_size: int = 100):        self.metrics: deque = deque(maxlen=window_size)        self.start_time = time.time()        def record(self,                latency_ms: float,               tokens: int,               cost: float):        """Καταγραφή metrics από ένα call"""        metric = PerformanceMetrics(            timestamp=time.time(),            cpu_percent=psutil.cpu_percent(),            memory_mb=psutil.Process().memory_info().rss / 1024 / 1024,            latency_ms=latency_ms,            tokens_per_second=tokens / (latency_ms / 1000) if latency_ms > 0 else 0,            cost_per_token=cost / tokens if tokens > 0 else 0        )        self.metrics.append(metric)        def get_stats(self) -> Dict:        """Στατιστικά από recent window"""        if not self.metrics:            return {}                latencies = [m.latency_ms for m in self.metrics]        costs = [m.cost_per_token for m in self.metrics]                return {            "avg_latency_ms": sum(latencies) / len(latencies),            "p95_latency_ms": sorted(latencies)[int(len(latencies) * 0.95)],            "avg_cost_per_token": sum(costs) / len(costs),            "total_calls": len(self.metrics),            "runtime_seconds": time.time() - self.start_time        }        def get_optimization_suggestions(self) -> List[str]:        """AI-powered optimization suggestions"""        suggestions = []        stats = self.get_stats()                if not stats:            return suggestions                if stats["avg_latency_ms"] > 5000:            suggestions.append(                "High latency detected. Consider using faster models (gpt-4o-mini) "                "for simple tasks or enabling more aggressive caching."            )                if stats["avg_cost_per_token"] > 0.0001:            suggestions.append(                "High cost per token. Consider using DeepSeek or GPT-4o Mini "                "for non-critical tasks."            )                if len(self.metrics) == self.metrics.maxlen:            recent = list(self.metrics)[-50:]            old = list(self.metrics)[:50]                        recent_avg = sum(m.latency_ms for m in recent) / len(recent)            old_avg = sum(m.latency_ms for m in old) / len(old)                        if recent_avg > old_avg * 1.5:                suggestions.append(                    "Performance degradation detected. Recent latency is 50% higher "                    "than earlier in the session. Consider restarting or clearing cache."                )                return suggestions        def export_report(self, filepath: str):        """Export detailed performance report"""        report = {            "generated_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),            "stats": self.get_stats(),            "suggestions": self.get_optimization_suggestions(),            "recent_metrics": [asdict(m) for m in list(self.metrics)[-10:]]        }                with open(filepath, 'w') as f:            json.dump(report, f, indent=2)
