1. Jupyter Integration (jupyter_integration.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""jupyter_integration.py - Jupyter Notebook/Lab IntegrationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Notebook generation από experiments2. Live monitoring μέσω widgets3. Cell injection για reproducibility4. Kernel management5. Interactive checkpoint resolution6. Automatic documentation generation7. Widget-based experiment controlΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from jupyter_integration import ExperimentNotebook>>> >>> # Δημιουργία notebook από experiment>>> nb = ExperimentNotebook.from_experiment("exp_001")>>> nb.save("analysis.ipynb")>>> >>> # Live widget monitoring>>> from jupyter_integration import ExperimentWidget>>> widget = ExperimentWidget("exp_001")>>> display(widget)  # Στο Jupyter>>> >>> # Cell magic για tracking>>> %load_ext manus_jupyter>>> %%track_experiment my_exp>>> result = analyze(data)"""import jsonimport base64from pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Unionfrom dataclasses import dataclass, asdictimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)try:    from IPython.display import display, HTML, Javascript    from ipywidgets import widgets, Layout, HBox, VBox    IPYTHON_AVAILABLE = Trueexcept ImportError:    IPYTHON_AVAILABLE = False    logger.warning("IPython not available, notebook features disabled")@dataclassclass NotebookCell:    """Αναπαράσταση Jupyter cell"""    cell_type: str  # 'code' ή 'markdown'    source: str    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = None    outputs: List[Dict] = None        def to_dict(self) -> Dict:        return {            "cell_type": self.cell_type,            "metadata": self.metadata or {},            "source": self.source if isinstance(self.source, list) else [self.source],            "outputs": self.outputs or []        }class ExperimentNotebook:    """Generator για reproducible Jupyter notebooks"""        def __init__(self, title: str, experiment_id: Optional[str] = None):        self.title = title        self.experiment_id = experiment_id        self.cells: List[NotebookCell] = []        self.metadata = {            "kernelspec": {                "display_name": "Python 3",                "language": "python",                "name": "python3"            },            "language_info": {                "name": "python",                "version": "3.8.0"            },            "manus_metadata": {                "experiment_id": experiment_id,                "generated_by": "manus-win11",                "reproducibility_mode": True            }        }        def add_markdown(self, text: str):        """Προσθήκη markdown cell"""        self.cells.append(NotebookCell(            cell_type="markdown",            source=text        ))        def add_code(self, code: str,                  hidden: bool = False,                 reproducibility_tag: Optional[str] = None):        """        Προσθήκη code cell με optional reproducibility tracking.                Args:            code: Python code            hidden: Απόκρυψη στο τελικό output            reproducibility_tag: Tag για provenance tracking        """        metadata = {"jupyter": {"source_hidden": hidden}}        if reproducibility_tag:            metadata["manus"] = {"reproducibility_tag": reproducibility_tag}                self.cells.append(NotebookCell(            cell_type="code",            source=code,            metadata=metadata        ))        def add_experiment_setup(self, experiment_config: Dict[str, Any]):        """Προσθήκη setup cell με environment capture"""        setup_code = f'''# Auto-generated reproducibility setupimport jsonimport osfrom datetime import datetime# Experiment metadataEXPERIMENT_CONFIG = {json.dumps(experiment_config, indent=2)}# Environment captureENVIRONMENT = {{    "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),    "python_version": os.sys.version,    "working_directory": os.getcwd()}}print(f"Experiment: {{EXPERIMENT_CONFIG.get('title', 'Untitled')}}")print(f"Started at: {{ENVIRONMENT['timestamp']}}")'''        self.add_code(setup_code.strip(), reproducibility_tag="setup")        def add_data_loading(self, filepath: str,                          validation_rules: Optional[Dict] = None):        """Προσθήκη data loading με validation"""        code = f'''import pandas as pdfrom data_validator import ScientificValidator# Load datadf = pd.read_csv("{filepath}")print(f"Loaded {{len(df)}} rows, {{len(df.columns)}} columns")# Validationvalidator = ScientificValidator()report = validator.validate_dataset(df, {validation_rules or {}})print(f"Validation: {{'✓ Passed' if report['valid'] else '✗ Failed'}}")'''        self.add_code(code.strip(), reproducibility_tag="data_loading")        def add_analysis_step(self,                           name: str,                          description: str,                          code: str,                          checkpoint: bool = False):        """        Προσθήκη analysis step με optional checkpoint.                Αν checkpoint=True, προσθέτει interactive widget για approval.        """        # Documentation        self.add_markdown(f"## {name}\n\n{description}")                # Code        if checkpoint:            checkpoint_code = f'''# Checkpoint: {name}from IPython.display import displayimport ipywidgets as widgetsdef on_approve(b):    print("✓ Approved, continuing...")    # Store approval in experiment state    def on_reject(b):    print("✗ Rejected, revise needed")    approve_btn = widgets.Button(description="✓ Approve", button_style='success')reject_btn = widgets.Button(description="✗ Reject", button_style='danger')approve_btn.on_click(on_approve)reject_btn.on_click(on_reject)display(widgets.HBox([approve_btn, reject_btn]))'''            self.add_code(checkpoint_code.strip())                self.add_code(code, reproducibility_tag=f"analysis_{name}")        def add_visualization(self, plot_code: str,                           caption: Optional[str] = None):        """Προσθήκη visualization με caption"""        if caption:            self.add_markdown(f"**Figure:** {caption}")                self.add_code(f'''import matplotlib.pyplot as plt{plot_code}plt.show()'''.strip())        def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """Convert to Jupyter notebook format"""        return {            "metadata": self.metadata,            "nbformat": 4,            "nbformat_minor": 4,            "cells": [c.to_dict() for c in self.cells]        }        def save(self, filepath: str):        """Save σε .ipynb file"""        path = Path(filepath)        path.write_text(json.dumps(self.to_dict(), indent=2))        logger.info(f"Saved notebook to {filepath}")        @classmethod    def from_experiment(cls, experiment_id: str) -> 'ExperimentNotebook':        """        Generate notebook από existing experiment.                Δημιουργεί notebook που αναπαράγει το experiment step-by-step.        """        from reproducibility import ReproducibilityManager                rm = ReproducibilityManager()        # Load experiment data        exp_dir = rm.base_dir / experiment_id                if not exp_dir.exists():            raise ValueError(f"Experiment {experiment_id} not found")                manifest = json.loads((exp_dir / "manifest.json").read_text())                nb = cls(            title=manifest["title"],            experiment_id=experiment_id        )                # Header        nb.add_markdown(f'''# {manifest['title']}**Experiment ID:** `{experiment_id}`  **Created:** {manifest['created_at']}  **Tags:** {', '.join(manifest['tags'])}## Description{manifest['description']}## Reproducibility NotesThis notebook was auto-generated from a reproducible experiment record.All steps are documented with provenance tracking.''')                # Setup        nb.add_experiment_setup(manifest)                # Load provenance και generate cells        prov_path = exp_dir / "provenance.jsonl"        if prov_path.exists():            for line in prov_path.read_text().strip().split('\n'):                record = json.loads(line)                nb.add_analysis_step(                    name=record['operation'],                    description=f"Recorded operation from {record['timestamp']}",                    code=f"# Original execution time: {record['execution_time_ms']:.2f}ms\n" +                         record['code_snippet'],                    checkpoint=False                )                return nbclass ExperimentWidget:    """    Interactive Jupyter widget για real-time experiment monitoring.        Usage:        from jupyter_integration import ExperimentWidget        widget = ExperimentWidget("my_experiment")        display(widget)    """        def __init__(self, experiment_id: str):        if not IPYTHON_AVAILABLE:            raise ImportError("IPython and ipywidgets required")                self.experiment_id = experiment_id        self.state_manager = None  # Will be initialized                self._create_widgets()        self._setup_layout()        def _create_widgets(self):        """Create UI components"""        # Status display        self.status_label = widgets.Label(            value="Status: Initializing...",            layout=Layout(width='100%')        )                # Progress bar        self.progress = widgets.IntProgress(            value=0,            min=0,            max=100,            description='Progress:',            bar_style='info',            orientation='horizontal',            layout=Layout(width='100%')        )                # Cost display        self.cost_label = widgets.Label(value="Cost: $0.00")                # Current task        self.task_label = widgets.Label(value="Task: None")                # Log output        self.log_output = widgets.Output(            layout=Layout(                border='1px solid #ddd',                height='200px',                overflow='auto'            )        )                # Checkpoint controls (initially hidden)        self.checkpoint_box = widgets.VBox([            widgets.HTML("<b>⏸️ Checkpoint Reached</b>"),            widgets.Label(id="checkpoint_desc"),            widgets.Textarea(                placeholder="Enter your response...",                layout=Layout(width='100%')            ),            widgets.HBox([                widgets.Button(                    description="Submit",                    button_style='primary'                ),                widgets.Button(                    description="Skip",                    button_style='warning'                )            ])        ])        self.checkpoint_box.layout.display = 'none'                # Control buttons        self.pause_btn = widgets.Button(            description="⏸ Pause",            button_style='warning'        )        self.stop_btn = widgets.Button(            description="⏹ Stop",            button_style='danger'        )        self.export_btn = widgets.Button(            description="📥 Export",            button_style='info'        )        def _setup_layout(self):        """Arrange widgets"""        header = widgets.HTML(f"<h3>Experiment: {self.experiment_id}</h3>")                status_box = widgets.VBox([            self.status_label,            self.progress,            widgets.HBox([self.task_label, self.cost_label])        ])                controls = widgets.HBox([            self.pause_btn,            self.stop_btn,            self.export_btn        ])                self.main_box = widgets.VBox([            header,            status_box,            controls,            self.checkpoint_box,            widgets.HTML("<h4>Log Output</h4>"),            self.log_output        ])        def update_status(self, status: str, progress: int,                       current_task: str, cost: float):        """Update widget από external source"""        self.status_label.value = f"Status: {status}"        self.progress.value = progress        self.task_label.value = f"Task: {current_task}"        self.cost_label.value = f"Cost: ${cost:.4f}"        def show_checkpoint(self, description: str, callback):        """Show checkpoint controls"""        self.checkpoint_box.children[1].value = description        self.checkpoint_box.layout.display = 'block'                def on_submit(b):            response = self.checkpoint_box.children[2].value            callback(response)            self.checkpoint_box.layout.display = 'none'                self.checkpoint_box.children[3].children[0].on_click(on_submit)        def log(self, message: str, level: str = "info"):        """Add log message"""        with self.log_output:            color = {                "info": "black",                "warning": "orange",                "error": "red",                "success": "green"            }.get(level, "black")                        display(HTML(                f'<div style="color: {color}; margin: 2px 0;">'                f'[{datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")}] {message}'                f'</div>'            ))        def _ipython_display_(self):        """Display στο Jupyter"""        display(self.main_box)# Jupyter Magic Commandsdef load_ipython_extension(ipython):    """Load Jupyter extension"""    from IPython.core.magic import register_cell_magic, register_line_magic        @register_cell_magic    def track_experiment(line, cell):        """        Cell magic για automatic experiment tracking.                Usage:            %%track_experiment my_experiment_id            result = analyze(data)        """        experiment_id = line.strip() or "default"                # Execute cell με tracking        start_time = datetime.now()                try:            result = ipython.run_cell(cell)            success = result.success            error = None        except Exception as e:            success = False            error = str(e)            raise                # Record στο experiment        duration = (datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds()                # Display badge        badge = f'''        <div style="background: {'#d4edda' if success else '#f8d7da'};                     padding: 10px; border-radius: 5px; margin: 5px 0;">            <b>Experiment:</b> {experiment_id}<br>            <b>Status:</b> {'✓ Success' if success else '✗ Failed'}<br>            <b>Duration:</b> {duration:.3f}s        </div>        '''        display(HTML(badge))                return result        @register_line_magic    def manus_status(line):        """Check Manus agent status"""        # Implementation...        pass        print("Manus Jupyter extension loaded. Use %%track_experiment")# nbconvert exporter για PDF/reportsclass ManusPDFExporter:    """    Custom exporter για academic PDF reports από notebooks.        Includes:    - Proper formatting για code και output    - Figure captions    - Page breaks ανά section    """        def __init__(self, template_file: Optional[str] = None):        self.template_file = template_file        def export(self, notebook_path: str, output_path: str):        """Export notebook to PDF"""        import subprocess                # Use nbconvert with custom template        cmd = [            "jupyter", "nbconvert",            "--to", "pdf",            "--no-input" if False else "",  # Option to hide code            "--template", self.template_file or "classic",            notebook_path,            "--output", output_path        ]                subprocess.run([c for c in cmd if c], check=True)        logger.info(f"Exported PDF to {output_path}")
2. Zotero Integration (zotero_integration.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""zotero_integration.py - Zotero Reference Manager IntegrationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Two-way sync με Zotero library2. Automatic citation key generation3. PDF attachment management4. Tag/Collection synchronization5. Citation insertion σε papers6. Bibliography export σε multiple formats7. Duplicate detection και mergingΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from zotero_integration import ZoteroSync>>> >>> # Σύνδεση με Zotero>>> zot = ZoteroSync(...     library_id="12345",...     library_type="user",  # ή "group"...     api_key="your_api_key"... )>>> >>> # Sync τοπική βάση με Zotero>>> zot.sync()>>> >>> # Προσθήκη citation από agent>>> zot.add_item_from_agent(...     title="Quantum Machine Learning",...     authors=["Biamonte, J.", "Wittek, P."],...     year=2017,...     doi="10.1038/nature23474"... )>>> >>> # Export για paper>>> zot.export_bibliography("my_paper", format="biblatex")"""import jsonimport loggingfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Unionfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom pathlib import Pathfrom datetime import datetimelogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)try:    from pyzotero import zotero    PYZOTERO_AVAILABLE = Trueexcept ImportError:    PYZOTERO_AVAILABLE = False    logger.warning("pyzotero not installed, Zotero integration disabled")@dataclassclass ZoteroItem:    """Simplified Zotero item representation"""    key: str    title: str    authors: List[str]    year: Optional[int]    item_type: str  # journalArticle, book, etc.    doi: Optional[str] = None    url: Optional[str] = None    abstract: Optional[str] = None    tags: List[str] = None    collections: List[str] = None    pdf_path: Optional[str] = None        def to_csl(self) -> Dict:        """Convert to CSL-JSON format"""        return {            "id": self.key,            "type": self.item_type,            "title": self.title,            "author": [{"family": a.split(",")[0].strip(),                        "given": a.split(",")[1].strip() if "," in a else ""}                       for a in self.authors],            "issued": {"date-parts": [[self.year]]} if self.year else None,            "DOI": self.doi,            "URL": self.url,            "abstract": self.abstract        }class ZoteroSync:    """    Two-way synchronization με Zotero.        Features:    - Automatic conflict resolution    - Local caching για offline work    - Batch operations    - Attachment management    """        def __init__(self,                  library_id: str,                 library_type: str = "user",                 api_key: str = None,                 local_cache_dir: str = "./zotero_cache"):        if not PYZOTERO_AVAILABLE:            raise ImportError("Install pyzotero: pip install pyzotero")                self.zot = zotero.Zotero(library_id, library_type, api_key)        self.cache_dir = Path(local_cache_dir)        self.cache_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                self.local_items: Dict[str, ZoteroItem] = {}        self._load_cache()        def _load_cache(self):        """Load local cache"""        cache_file = self.cache_dir / "items.json"        if cache_file.exists():            data = json.loads(cache_file.read_text())            self.local_items = {                k: ZoteroItem(**v) for k, v in data.items()            }        def _save_cache(self):        """Save local cache"""        cache_file = self.cache_dir / "items.json"        data = {k: v.__dict__ for k, v in self.local_items.items()}        cache_file.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2, default=str))        def sync(self, full_sync: bool = False) -> Dict[str, int]:        """        Sync με Zotero.                Returns:            Stats: {added, updated, deleted, conflicts}        """        stats = {"added": 0, "updated": 0, "deleted": 0, "conflicts": 0}                # Fetch από Zotero        zotero_items = self.zot.items(limit=100 if not full_sync else None)                remote_keys = set()        for item in zotero_items:            key = item['key']            remote_keys.add(key)                        z_item = self._convert_zotero_item(item)                        if key not in self.local_items:                self.local_items[key] = z_item                stats["added"] += 1            else:                # Check for updates                local = self.local_items[key]                if self._item_needs_update(local, z_item):                    self.local_items[key] = z_item                    stats["updated"] += 1                # Check για deleted        local_keys = set(self.local_items.keys())        deleted = local_keys - remote_keys        for key in deleted:            del self.local_items[key]            stats["deleted"] += 1                self._save_cache()        logger.info(f"Sync complete: {stats}")        return stats        def _convert_zotero_item(self, zotero_data: Dict) -> ZoteroItem:        """Convert Zotero API response to ZoteroItem"""        data = zotero_data.get('data', zotero_data)                # Extract authors        creators = data.get('creators', [])        authors = []        for c in creators:            if c.get('creatorType') in ['author', 'editor']:                name = f"{c.get('lastName', '')}, {c.get('firstName', '')}"                authors.append(name.strip())                # Extract year        date = data.get('date', '')        year = None        if date:            try:                year = int(date[:4])            except ValueError:                pass                return ZoteroItem(            key=zotero_data['key'],            title=data.get('title', 'Untitled'),            authors=authors,            year=year,            item_type=data.get('itemType', 'document'),            doi=data.get('DOI'),            url=data.get('url'),            abstract=data.get('abstractNote'),            tags=[t['tag'] for t in data.get('tags', [])],            collections=data.get('collections', [])        )        def _item_needs_update(self, local: ZoteroItem, remote: ZoteroItem) -> bool:        """Check αν το remote είναι νεότερο"""        # Simplified - θα έπρεπε να χρησιμοποιεί version timestamps        return (local.title != remote.title or                 local.year != remote.year or                set(local.authors) != set(remote.authors))        def add_item_from_agent(self,                            title: str,                            authors: List[str],                            year: int,                            item_type: str = "journalArticle",                            **kwargs) -> str:        """        Προσθήκη item από agent (και sync στο Zotero).                Returns:            Zotero item key        """        template = self.zot.item_template(item_type)                template['title'] = title        template['creators'] = [            {'creatorType': 'author',              'firstName': a.split(',')[1].strip() if ',' in a else '',             'lastName': a.split(',')[0].strip()}            for a in authors        ]        template['date'] = str(year)                for key, value in kwargs.items():            if key in template:                template[key] = value                # Create in Zotero        response = self.zot.create_items([template])        key = response['successful']['0']['key']                # Update local cache        self.sync()                return key        def add_pdf_attachment(self, item_key: str, pdf_path: str):        """Προσθήκη PDF σε existing item"""        self.zot.attachment_simple([pdf_path], item_key)        logger.info(f"Added PDF to {item_key}")        def search_local(self, query: str) -> List[ZoteroItem]:        """Search local cache"""        query_lower = query.lower()        results = []                for item in self.local_items.values():            score = 0                        # Title match            if query_lower in item.title.lower():                score += 3                        # Author match            for author in item.authors:                if query_lower in author.lower():                    score += 2                        # Year match            if query == str(item.year):                score += 1                        # Tag match            for tag in (item.tags or []):                if query_lower in tag.lower():                    score += 1                        if score > 0:                results.append((score, item))                results.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)        return [r[1] for r in results[:10]]        def export_bibliography(self,                            collection_key: Optional[str],                           output_path: str,                           format: str = "biblatex"):        """        Export bibliography σε various formats.                Formats: biblatex, apa, mla, chicago, csl-json        """        if collection_key:            items = self.zot.collection_items(collection_key)        else:            items = self.local_items.values()                if format == "csl-json":            data = {"items": [item.to_csl() for item in items]}            Path(output_path).write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2))                elif format in ["biblatex", "apa", "mla", "chicago"]:            # Use Zotero's format export            # This would need additional implementation            pass                logger.info(f"Exported {len(items)} items to {output_path}")        def get_citation_key(self, item_key: str,                          style: str = "authoryear") -> str:        """        Generate citation key (π.χ. Smith2020).                Styles:        - authoryear: Smith2020        - authoryeara: Smith2020a (για διακριτοποίηση)        - numeric: [1]        """        item = self.local_items.get(item_key)        if not item:            return item_key                if style == "authoryear":            first_author = item.authors[0].split(',')[0] if item.authors else "Unknown"            return f"{first_author}{item.year or 'n.d.'}"                return item_key        def insert_citation(self, item_key: str,                         document_path: str,                        style: str = "pandoc"):        """        Insert citation σε document (LaTeX, Markdown, Word).                Styles:        - pandoc: [@Smith2020]        - latex: \\cite{Smith2020}        - markdown: (Smith, 2020)        """        cite_key = self.get_citation_key(item_key)                formats = {            "pandoc": f"[@{cite_key}]",            "latex": f"\\cite{{{cite_key}}}",            "markdown": f"({cite_key})"        }                citation = formats.get(style, cite_key)                # Append to document (simplified)        with open(document_path, 'a') as f:            f.write(f"\n{citation}\n")                return citationclass ZoteroBridge:    """    Bridge μεταξύ agent και Zotero για automatic citation management.        Usage:        bridge = ZoteroBridge(zotero_sync)                # Στο agent        bridge.cite_during_analysis("10.1038/s41586-021-03819-2")    """        def __init__(self, zotero_sync: ZoteroSync):        self.zot = zotero_sync        self.cited_keys: List[str] = []        def cite_during_analysis(self, identifier: str) -> str:        """        Citation κατά την ανάλυση.                Identifier μπορεί να είναι:        - DOI        - Zotero key        - Title (θα κάνει search)        """        # Try DOI first        if identifier.startswith("10."):            # Search by DOI            items = self.zot.search_local(identifier)            if items:                key = items[0].key            else:                # Fetch from Crossref και προσθήκη                key = self._fetch_and_add_doi(identifier)        else:            # Assume it's a key or title            items = self.zot.search_local(identifier)            key = items[0].key if items else identifier                self.cited_keys.append(key)        return self.zot.get_citation_key(key)        def _fetch_and_add_doi(self, doi: str) -> str:        """Fetch metadata από DOI και προσθήκη στο Zotero"""        # Use existing literature.py integration        from literature import CitationManager                cm = CitationManager()        citation = cm.add_from_doi(doi)                if citation:            # Add to Zotero            key = self.zot.add_item_from_agent(                title=citation.title,                authors=citation.authors,                year=citation.year,                DOI=citation.doi,                url=citation.url            )            return key                raise ValueError(f"Could not fetch DOI: {doi}")        def generate_bibliography_for_paper(self, output_path: str):        """Generate bibliography από cited keys"""        # Export μόνο τα cited        items = [self.zot.local_items[k] for k in self.cited_keys                 if k in self.zot.local_items]                # Save        data = {"items": [item.to_csl() for item in items]}        Path(output_path).write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2))
3. Overleaf Integration (overleaf_integration.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""overleaf_integration.py - Overleaf/LaTeX IntegrationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Git-based sync με Overleaf projects2. Automatic .tex generation από experiments3. Figure/table insertion4. Bibliography sync5. Compilation error detection6. Track changes support7. Collaborative editing hooksΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from overleaf_integration import OverleafProject>>> >>> # Σύνδεση με existing project>>> project = OverleafProject.clone(...     url="https://git.overleaf.com/123456789abcdef",...     local_path="./my_paper"... )>>> >>> # Auto-generate sections>>> project.generate_methods_section("exp_001")>>> project.generate_results_section("exp_001")>>> >>> # Insert figure>>> project.insert_figure(...     image_path="plot.png",...     caption="Results of analysis",...     label="fig:results"... )>>> >>> # Sync>>> project.commit_and_push("Updated results from experiment")"""import subprocessimport reimport shutilfrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Unionfrom dataclasses import dataclassimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass LaTeXSection:    """Representation of LaTeX section"""    title: str    content: str    level: int = 1  # 1=section, 2=subsection, etc.    label: Optional[str] = None        def to_latex(self) -> str:        """Generate LaTeX code"""        cmd = ["section", "subsection", "subsubsection"][self.level - 1]                lines = [f"\\{cmd}{{{self.title}}}"]                if self.label:            lines.append(f"\\label{{{self.label}}}")                lines.append("")        lines.append(self.content)                return "\n".join(lines)class OverleafProject:    """    Manager για Overleaf project μέσω Git.        Requires:    - Git installed    - Overleaf project με Git access enabled    """        def __init__(self, local_path: str):        self.local_path = Path(local_path)        self.main_tex = self._find_main_tex()                if not self._is_git_repo():            raise ValueError("Not a git repository. Clone first.")        @classmethod    def clone(cls, url: str, local_path: str) -> 'OverleafProject':        """Clone Overleaf project"""        if Path(local_path).exists():            raise ValueError(f"Directory {local_path} already exists")                subprocess.run(            ["git", "clone", url, local_path],            check=True        )                return cls(local_path)        def _is_git_repo(self) -> bool:        """Check if directory is git repo"""        return (self.local_path / ".git").exists()        def _find_main_tex(self) -> Path:        """Find main .tex file"""        tex_files = list(self.local_path.glob("*.tex"))                # Look for main.tex or document with \documentclass        for tex in tex_files:            content = tex.read_text()            if "\\documentclass" in content:                return tex                # Fallback to first .tex        return tex_files[0] if tex_files else None        def generate_methods_section(self, experiment_id: str) -> str:        """        Auto-generate Methods section από experiment.                Returns:            Generated LaTeX content        """        from reproducibility import ReproducibilityManager                rm = ReproducibilityManager()        exp_dir = rm.base_dir / experiment_id                if not exp_dir.exists():            raise ValueError(f"Experiment {experiment_id} not found")                manifest = json.loads((exp_dir / "manifest.json").read_text())                # Generate LaTeX        latex = []        latex.append("\\section{Methods}")        latex.append(f"\\label{{sec:methods-{experiment_id}}}")        latex.append("")        latex.append(f"\\subsection{{{manifest['title']}}}")        latex.append(manifest['description'])        latex.append("")                # Environment        latex.append("\\subsubsection{Computational Environment}")        env = manifest.get('environment', {})                latex.append("\\begin{itemize}")        latex.append(f"\\item Python {env.get('python_version', 'unknown')[:20]}")        latex.append(f"\\item Platform: {env.get('platform', 'unknown')}")                packages = env.get('packages', {})        if packages:            latex.append("\\item Key packages: " +                         ", ".join([f"{k} v{v}" for k, v in list(packages.items())[:5]]))                latex.append("\\end{itemize}")                # Procedure        latex.append("\\subsubsection{Procedure}")                prov_path = exp_dir / "provenance.jsonl"        if prov_path.exists():            latex.append("\\begin{enumerate}")            for line in prov_path.read_text().strip().split('\n'):                record = json.loads(line)                latex.append(f"\\item \\texttt{{{record['operation']}}} "                           f"({record['execution_time_ms']:.0f} ms)")            latex.append("\\end{enumerate}")                latex.append("")        latex.append(f"\\textit{{Reproducibility:}} All code and data are available "                    f"in the supplementary materials (Experiment ID: \\texttt{{{experiment_id}}}).")                return "\n".join(latex)        def generate_results_section(self,                                   experiment_id: str,                                  figures: List[Dict] = None) -> str:        """        Generate Results section με figures.        """        latex = []        latex.append("\\section{Results}")        latex.append(f"\\label{{sec:results-{experiment_id}}}")        latex.append("")                # Load artifacts        from reproducibility import ReproducibilityManager        rm = ReproducibilityManager()        exp_dir = rm.base_dir / experiment_id                artifacts_dir = exp_dir / "artifacts"        if artifacts_dir.exists():            latex.append("Key findings are summarized in the following figures:")            latex.append("")                        for i, artifact_file in enumerate(artifacts_dir.glob("*.json"), 1):                data = json.loads(artifact_file.read_text())                latex.append(f"Figure {i} shows {data['name']}.")                # Insert figures        if figures:            for fig in figures:                latex.append(self._create_figure_environment(fig))                return "\n".join(latex)        def _create_figure_environment(self, fig_config: Dict) -> str:        """Create LaTeX figure environment"""        lines = [            "\\begin{figure}[htbp]",            "\\centering",            f"\\includegraphics[width={fig_config.get('width', '0.8')}\\textwidth]"            f"{{{fig_config['path']}}}",            f"\\caption{{{fig_config['caption']}}}",            f"\\label{{{fig_config.get('label', 'fig:unknown')}}}",            "\\end{figure}",            ""        ]        return "\n".join(lines)        def insert_section(self,                        section: Union[LaTeXSection, str],                       after: Optional[str] = None,                       before: Optional[str] = None):        """        Insert section στο main.tex.                Args:            section: LaTeXSection ή string            after: Insert μετά από αυτό το section            before: Insert πριν από αυτό το section        """        if isinstance(section, LaTeXSection):            content = section.to_latex()        else:            content = section                main_content = self.main_tex.read_text()                if after:            # Find section και insert μετά            pattern = f"\\\\section{{{after}}}"            if re.search(pattern, main_content):                main_content = re.sub(                    f"({pattern}.*?)(?=\\\\section|$)",                    f"\\1\n\n{content}\n",                    main_content,                    flags=re.DOTALL                )        elif before:            pattern = f"\\\\section{{{before}}}"            main_content = main_content.replace(                f"\\section{{{before}}}",                f"{content}\n\n\\section{{{before}}}"            )        else:            # Append πριν το \end{document}            main_content = main_content.replace(                "\\end{document}",                f"{content}\n\n\\end{{document}}"            )                self.main_tex.write_text(main_content)        logger.info(f"Inserted section into {self.main_tex}")        def insert_figure(self,                      image_path: str,                      caption: str,                      label: str,                      width: str = "0.8\\textwidth"):        """        Insert figure και copy image to project.                Args:            image_path: Path to image file            caption: Figure caption            label: LaTeX label (π.χ. "fig:results")            width: Width parameter        """        # Copy image to project        img_dest = self.local_path / "figures" / Path(image_path).name        img_dest.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)        shutil.copy(image_path, img_dest)                # Add to main.tex        fig_env = f'''\\begin{{figure}}[htbp]\\centering\\includegraphics[width={width}]{{{img_dest.name}}}\\caption{{{caption}}}\\label{{{label}}}\\end{{figure}}'''        self.insert_section(fig_env)        def insert_table(self,                     data: List[List],                     caption: str,                     label: str,                     headers: Optional[List[str]] = None):        """        Insert table από data.                Args:            data: 2D list με values            caption: Table caption            label: LaTeX label            headers: Optional column headers        """        if not data:            return                num_cols = len(data[0])        col_spec = "c" * num_cols  # Centered columns                lines = [            "\\begin{table}[htbp]",            "\\centering",            "\\caption{" + caption + "}",            "\\label{" + label + "}",            f"\\begin{{tabular}}{{{col_spec}}}",            "\\toprule"        ]                if headers:            lines.append(" & ".join(headers) + " \\\\")            lines.append("\\midrule")                for row in data:            # Escape special chars            clean_row = [str(cell).replace("&", "\\&").replace("%", "\\%")                         for cell in row]            lines.append(" & ".join(clean_row) + " \\\\")                lines.extend([            "\\bottomrule",            "\\end{tabular}",            "\\end{table}"        ])                self.insert_section("\n".join(lines))        def sync_bibliography(self, zotero_sync=None):        """        Sync bibliography από Zotero.                Generates .bib file και updates \\bibliography command.        """        if zotero_sync:            bib_path = self.local_path / "references.bib"            zotero_sync.export_bibliography(                collection_key=None,                output_path=str(bib_path),                format="biblatex"            )                        # Ensure \bibliography is in main.tex            main_content = self.main_tex.read_text()            if "\\bibliography" not in main_content:                main_content = main_content.replace(                    "\\end{document}",                    "\\bibliography{references}\n\\end{document}"                )                self.main_tex.write_text(main_content)        def compile(self) -> Dict[str, any]:        """        Compile LaTeX locally (αν υπάρχει installation).                Returns:            Dict με success, log, errors        """        try:            result = subprocess.run(                ["pdflatex", "-interaction=nonstopmode",                  str(self.main_tex.name)],                cwd=self.local_path,                capture_output=True,                text=True,                timeout=60            )                        # Parse errors            errors = self._parse_latex_errors(result.stdout + result.stderr)                        return {                "success": result.returncode == 0,                "errors": errors,                "warnings": [],  # Would parse from log                "output": result.stdout[-1000:] if len(result.stdout) > 1000 else result.stdout            }                    except FileNotFoundError:            return {                "success": False,                "errors": ["pdflatex not found. Install TeX Live or MiKTeX."],                "warnings": [],                "output": ""            }        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:            return {                "success": False,                "errors": ["Compilation timeout"],                "warnings": [],                "output": ""            }        def _parse_latex_errors(self, log: str) -> List[str]:        """Extract errors από LaTeX log"""        errors = []        for line in log.split('\n'):            if line.startswith('!'):                errors.append(line)        return errors        def commit_and_push(self, message: str):        """Git commit και push στο Overleaf"""        # Add all changes        subprocess.run(            ["git", "add", "."],            cwd=self.local_path,            check=True        )                # Commit        subprocess.run(            ["git", "commit", "-m", message],            cwd=self.local_path,            check=True        )                # Push        subprocess.run(            ["git", "push"],            cwd=self.local_path,            check=True        )                logger.info(f"Pushed to Overleaf: {message}")        def track_changes(self, enable: bool = True):        """        Enable/disable track changes (Overleaf feature).                Note: Αυτό είναι conceptual - πραγματικό implementation        θα χρειαζόταν Overleaf API access.        """        # Placeholder για future API integration        passclass LaTeXTemplate:    """    Pre-defined templates για common paper types.    """        TEMPLATES = {        "letter": {            "documentclass": "letter",            "packages": ["geometry", "graphicx"],            "structure": ["opening", "body", "closing"]        },        "article": {            "documentclass": "article",            "packages": ["amsmath", "graphicx", "natbib", "hyperref"],            "structure": ["abstract", "introduction", "methods",                          "results", "discussion", "conclusion", "references"]        },        "prl": {  # Physical Review Letters            "documentclass": "revtex4-2",            "options": ["prl", "aps", "twocolumn"],            "packages": ["graphicx", "amsmath"],            "structure": ["title", "authors", "abstract", "body", "references"]        },        "nature": {            "documentclass": "nature",            "packages": ["graphicx", "amssymb"],            "structure": ["title", "abstract", "introduction", "results",                         "discussion", "methods", "references"]        }    }        @classmethod    def create_project(cls,                        template: str,                       output_dir: str,                       metadata: Dict[str, str]):        """        Create new project από template.                Args:            template: Όνομα template (letter, article, prl, nature)            output_dir: Που να δημιουργηθεί            metadata: Title, authors, κλπ        """        tmpl = cls.TEMPLATES.get(template, cls.TEMPLATES["article"])        path = Path(output_dir)        path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                # Create main.tex        lines = [            f"\\documentclass[{','.join(tmpl.get('options', []))}]"            f"{{{tmpl['documentclass']}}}",            ""        ]                # Packages        for pkg in tmpl["packages"]:            lines.append(f"\\usepackage{{{pkg}}}")        lines.append("")                # Metadata        if "title" in metadata:            lines.append(f"\\title{{{metadata['title']}}}")        if "author" in metadata:            lines.append(f"\\author{{{metadata['author']}}}")        lines.append("")                # Document        lines.append("\\begin{document}")        lines.append("\\maketitle")                if "abstract" in metadata:            lines.append("\\begin{abstract}")            lines.append(metadata["abstract"])            lines.append("\\end{abstract}")            lines.append("")                # Placeholders for sections        for section in tmpl["structure"]:            if section not in ["title", "authors", "abstract"]:                lines.append(f"\\section{{{section.capitalize()}}}")                lines.append(f"% TODO: Add {section} content")                lines.append("")                lines.append("\\end{document}")                # Write        (path / "main.tex").write_text("\n".join(lines))                # Create figures directory        (path / "figures").mkdir(exist_ok=True)                # Git init        subprocess.run(["git", "init"], cwd=path, check=True)                return OverleafProject(str(path))
4. Additional Scientific Integrations
4.1 arXiv Integration (arxiv_integration.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""arxiv_integration.py - arXiv Preprint Server Integration"""import feedparserimport requestsfrom typing import List, Dict, Optionalfrom dataclasses import dataclass@dataclassclass ArXivPaper:    title: str    authors: List[str]    abstract: str    arxiv_id: str    pdf_url: str    published: str    categories: List[str]    doi: Optional[str] = Noneclass ArXivClient:    """Client για arXiv API"""        BASE_URL = "http://export.arxiv.org/api/query"        def search(self,                query: str,               max_results: int = 10,               sort_by: str = "relevance",               sort_order: str = "descending") -> List[ArXivPaper]:        """        Search arXiv.                Args:            query: Search query (supports arXiv search syntax)            max_results: Maximum results to return            sort_by: relevance, lastUpdatedDate, submittedDate        """        params = {            "search_query": query,            "start": 0,            "max_results": max_results,            "sortBy": sort_by,            "sortOrder": sort_order        }                response = requests.get(self.BASE_URL, params=params)        feed = feedparser.parse(response.content)                papers = []        for entry in feed.entries:            paper = ArXivPaper(                title=entry.title,                authors=[a.name for a in entry.authors],                abstract=entry.summary,                arxiv_id=entry.id.split('/')[-1],                pdf_url=entry.link.replace("abs", "pdf") + ".pdf",                published=entry.published,                categories=[t['term'] for t in entry.tags],                doi=entry.get('arxiv_doi')            )            papers.append(paper)                return papers        def download_pdf(self, arxiv_id: str, output_path: str):        """Download PDF από arXiv"""        url = f"https://arxiv.org/pdf/{arxiv_id}.pdf"        response = requests.get(url)                with open(output_path, 'wb') as f:            f.write(response.content)                return output_path        def to_zotero(self, paper: ArXivPaper, zotero_sync) -> str:        """Add arXiv paper to Zotero"""        return zotero_sync.add_item_from_agent(            title=paper.title,            authors=paper.authors,            year=int(paper.published[:4]),            item_type="preprint",            url=f"https://arxiv.org/abs/{paper.arxiv_id}",            extra=f"arXiv: {paper.arxiv_id}"        )
4.2 GitHub/GitLab Integration (git_integration.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""git_integration.py - Git Repository Management for Research Code"""import subprocessfrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import List, Optional, Dictimport jsonclass ResearchRepository:    """    Git repository optimized για research code.        Features:    - Automatic .gitignore for data files    - Git LFS setup for large files    - GitHub/GitLab releases για versions    - Zenodo integration για DOI generation    """        GITIGNORE_TEMPLATE = '''# Data files*.csv*.h5*.hdf5*.pkl*.pickle*.npy*.npzdata/raw_data/# Resultsresults/figures/*.pngfigures/*.jpg!figures/.gitkeep# Models*.pth*.h5*.pbmodels/# Jupyter.ipynb_checkpoints/*.ipynb_checkpoints# Python__pycache__/*.py[cod]*$py.class.envvenv/# LaTeX*.aux*.log*.out*.toc*.bbl*.blg*.synctex.gz# IDE.vscode/.idea/*.swp*.swo*~# OS.DS_StoreThumbs.db'''        def __init__(self, path: str):        self.path = Path(path)        if not (self.path / ".git").exists():            raise ValueError("Not a git repository")        @classmethod    def init(cls, path: str,              template: str = "research",             remote_url: Optional[str] = None) -> 'ResearchRepository':        """Initialize new research repository"""        p = Path(path)        p.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                # Git init        subprocess.run(["git", "init"], cwd=p, check=True)                # Create structure        (p / "src").mkdir(exist_ok=True)        (p / "data").mkdir(exist_ok=True)        (p / "results").mkdir(exist_ok=True)        (p / "figures").mkdir(exist_ok=True)        (p / "notebooks").mkdir(exist_ok=True)        (p / "docs").mkdir(exist_ok=True)                # .gitignore        (p / ".gitignore").write_text(cls.GITIGNORE_TEMPLATE)                # README template        readme = f'''# {p.name}## DescriptionBrief description of the research project.## Structure- `src/`: Source code- `data/`: Data files (not tracked by git)- `results/`: Output results- `figures/`: Generated figures- `notebooks/`: Jupyter notebooks- `docs/`: Documentation## ReproducibilityThis project uses the Manus-Win11 Agent Framework for reproducibility.## Installation```bashpip install -r requirements.txt
Usage
python src/main.py
Citation
If you use this code, please cite:
@software{{{p.name},  author = {{Author Name}},  title = {{{p.name}}},  year = {{2024}},  url = {{https://github.com/username/{p.name}}}}}
’’’ (p / “README.md”).write_text(readme)
    # Initial commit    subprocess.run(["git", "add", "."], cwd=p, check=True)    subprocess.run(["git", "commit", "-m", "Initial commit"], cwd=p, check=True)        # Add remote if provided    if remote_url:        subprocess.run(            ["git", "remote", "add", "origin", remote_url],            cwd=p, check=True        )        return cls(str(p))def create_release(self,                    tag: str,                   message: str,                   files: Optional[List[str]] = None):    """    Create GitHub/GitLab release with files.        This is a wrapper around git tag + gh/gl CLI.    """    # Create tag    subprocess.run(        ["git", "tag", "-a", tag, "-m", message],        cwd=self.path,        check=True    )        # Push tag    subprocess.run(        ["git", "push", "origin", tag],        cwd=self.path,        check=True    )        # Create release with gh CLI if available    try:        cmd = ["gh", "release", "create", tag, "--notes", message]        if files:            cmd.extend(files)        subprocess.run(cmd, cwd=self.path, check=True)    except (subprocess.CalledProcessError, FileNotFoundError):        logger.info("GitHub CLI not available, tag created only")def zenodo_publish(self,                    metadata: Dict,                   sandbox: bool = True) -> str:    """    Publish to Zenodo για DOI generation.        Requires zenodoclient: pip install zenodoclient    """    # This would integrate with Zenodo API    # Placeholder για implementation    passdef snapshot_for_paper(self,                        paper_title: str,                       output_dir: str):    """    Create clean snapshot of code για paper submission.        Removes unnecessary files και creates archive.    """    import shutil    import tempfile        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:        tmp_path = Path(tmp) / "code"        shutil.copytree(self.path, tmp_path, ignore=shutil.ignore_patterns(            '.git', '__pycache__', '*.pyc', '.env', 'venv',            'data', 'results', 'figures/*.png'        ))                # Add README with paper reference        readme = tmp_path / "README_FOR_PAPER.md"        readme.write_text(f'''
This code accompanies the paper: “{paper_title}”
For full reproducibility information, see the main repository. ’’’)
        # Create archive        archive_path = Path(output_dir) / f"{self.path.name}_code.zip"        shutil.make_archive(            archive_path.with_suffix(''),            'zip',            tmp_path        )                return str(archive_path)
### 4.3 **Docker/Singularity Integration** (`containerization.py`)```python#!/usr/bin/env python3"""containerization.py - Container Generation for Reproducibility"""from pathlib import Pathfrom typing import List, Optionalclass ContainerBuilder:    """    Generate Docker/Singularity containers από experiments.    """        def generate_dockerfile(self,                            experiment_id: str,                           base_image: str = "python:3.9-slim",                           output_path: str = "Dockerfile"):        """        Generate Dockerfile από experiment.        """        from reproducibility import ReproducibilityManager                rm = ReproducibilityManager()        exp_dir = rm.base_dir / experiment_id                manifest = json.loads((exp_dir / "manifest.json").read_text())        packages = manifest.get('environment', {}).get('packages', {})                lines = [            f"FROM {base_image}",            "",            "WORKDIR /app",            "",            "# Install system dependencies",            "RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \\",            "    git \\",            "    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*",            "",            "# Install Python packages",        ]                # Generate requirements        for pkg, version in packages.items():            lines.append(f"RUN pip install {pkg}=={version}")                lines.extend([            "",            "# Copy experiment",            f"COPY {experiment_id} /app/experiment/",            "",            "# Set environment",            "ENV PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1",            "",            "# Run experiment",            'CMD ["python", "-m", "experiment.main"]'        ])                Path(output_path).write_text("\n".join(lines))        return output_path        def generate_singularity_def(self,                                  experiment_id: str,                                  output_path: str = "Singularity"):        """        Generate Singularity definition file (για HPC).        """        # Similar to Dockerfile but Singularity syntax        pass        def build_and_push(self,                        dockerfile_path: str,                       image_name: str,                       registry: Optional[str] = None):        """        Build και push Docker image.        """        import subprocess                # Build        subprocess.run(            ["docker", "build", "-f", dockerfile_path,              "-t", image_name, "."],            check=True        )                # Push if registry specified        if registry:            full_name = f"{registry}/{image_name}"            subprocess.run(                ["docker", "tag", image_name, full_name],                check=True            )            subprocess.run(                ["docker", "push", full_name],                check=True            )            return full_name                return image_name
5. Unified Research CLI (cli_research_unified.py)

Συνοπτικός Πίνακας Integrations:
Εργαλείο
Module
Βασικές Λειτουργίες

Notebook generation, live widgets, cell magic

Two-way sync, citation management, bibliography export

Git sync, auto-generated sections, figure insertion

Container generation από experiments

cli_research_unified.py
Όλες οι εντολές σε ένα interface
Θέλεις να προσθέσω κάποιο άλλο εργαλείο (π.χ. Mendeley, EndNote, Obsidian, Notion) ή να εμβαθύνω σε κάποιο από τα υπάρχοντα;
User:
Ενσωμάτωσε obsidian, χειρισμό και αυτοματισμό desktop publishing, pandoc, latex, typst
Kimi:
Θα ενσωματώσω Obsidian για knowledge management, desktop publishing automation, και υποστήριξη για Pandoc, LaTeX, και Typst σε ένα ενιαίο σύστημα.
1. Obsidian Integration (obsidian_integration.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""obsidian_integration.py - Obsidian Knowledge Base IntegrationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Two-way sync με Obsidian vault2. Automatic note generation από experiments3. Knowledge graph construction4. Daily notes και research journaling5. Template-based note creation6. Backlinks και tags management7. Canvas (visual notes) generation8. Dataview queries για research dashboardΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from obsidian_integration import ObsidianVault, ResearchNote>>> >>> # Σύνδεση με vault>>> vault = ObsidianVault("~/Documents/Obsidian/Research")>>> >>> # Δημιουργία research note>>> note = ResearchNote(...     title="Quantum ML Experiment 001",...     tags=["quantum", "ml", "experiment"],...     experiment_id="exp_001"... )>>> vault.create_note(note)>>> >>> # Auto-generate από experiment>>> vault.generate_from_experiment("exp_001")>>> >>> # Update knowledge graph>>> vault.update_graph()"""import jsonimport reimport shutilfrom datetime import datetime, datefrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Set, Anyfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdictimport loggingimport yamllogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)@dataclassclass ObsidianNote:    """Base class για Obsidian notes"""    title: str    content: str = ""    tags: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)    links: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)  # [[WikiLinks]]    aliases: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)        def to_markdown(self) -> str:        """Generate Obsidian-flavored markdown"""        # Frontmatter        frontmatter = {            "title": self.title,            "tags": self.tags,            "aliases": self.aliases,            "created": datetime.now().isoformat(),            **self.metadata        }                lines = [            "---",            yaml.dump(frontmatter, allow_unicode=True, sort_keys=False),            "---",            "",            f"# {self.title}",            "",        ]                # Add aliases as callout if exists        if self.aliases:            lines.append("> **Also known as:** " + ", ".join(                f"[[{alias}]]" for alias in self.aliases            ))            lines.append("")                # Content        lines.append(self.content)                # Backlinks section        if self.links:            lines.extend([                "",                "## Related",                "",            ])            for link in self.links:                lines.append(f"- [[{link}]]")                return "\n".join(lines)        def filename(self) -> str:        """Generate safe filename"""        # Remove invalid chars, keep spaces for readability        safe = re.sub(r'[\\/:*?"<>|]', '', self.title)        return f"{safe}.md"@dataclassclass ResearchNote(ObsidianNote):    """Specialized note for research"""    experiment_id: Optional[str] = None    hypothesis: Optional[str] = None    conclusions: Optional[str] = None    status: str = "active"  # active, completed, archived        def __post_init__(self):        if "research" not in self.tags:            self.tags.insert(0, "research")        if self.experiment_id and "experiment" not in self.tags:            self.tags.append("experiment")@dataclassclass DailyNote(ObsidianNote):    """Daily research journal"""    def __init__(self, date_obj: Optional[date] = None):        self.date = date_obj or date.today()        super().__init__(            title=self.date.strftime("%Y-%m-%d"),            tags=["daily", "journal"],            content=self._template()        )        def _template(self) -> str:        return f'''## Research Log### Morning- ### Afternoon- ### Evening- ## Notes Created Today```dataviewLISTWHERE file.cday = date("{self.date.isoformat()}")SORT file.name ASC
Experiments
TABLE status, experiment_idFROM #experimentWHERE file.cday = date("{self.date.isoformat()}")
’’’
class ObsidianVault: ““” Manager για Obsidian vault integration.
Structure:- vault_root/  - 00_Inbox/          # New notes  - 01_Projects/       # Active research  - 02_Areas/          # Research areas  - 03_Resources/      # References, papers  - 04_Archive/        # Completed  - 05_Templates/      # Note templates  - 99_Meta/           # Knowledge graph, dashboards"""def __init__(self, vault_path: str):    self.vault_path = Path(vault_path).expanduser()    if not self.vault_path.exists():        raise ValueError(f"Vault not found: {vault_path}")        self._ensure_structure()def _ensure_structure(self):    """Ensure folder structure exists"""    folders = [        "00_Inbox",        "01_Projects/Experiments",        "01_Projects/Analyses",        "02_Areas/Research",        "03_Resources/Papers",        "03_Resources/Books",        "04_Archive/Completed",        "05_Templates",        "99_Meta/Dashboards",        "99_Meta/Graphs"    ]        for folder in folders:        (self.vault_path / folder).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)def create_note(self,                 note: ObsidianNote,                folder: Optional[str] = None,                inbox: bool = False) -> Path:    """    Create new note in vault.        Args:        note: Note to create        folder: Specific subfolder (π.χ. "01_Projects/Experiments")        inbox: If True, save to 00_Inbox regardless    """    if inbox:        target_dir = self.vault_path / "00_Inbox"    elif folder:        target_dir = self.vault_path / folder    else:        # Auto-route based on tags        target_dir = self._auto_route(note)        target_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)        filepath = target_dir / note.filename()        # Handle duplicates    counter = 1    original_path = filepath    while filepath.exists():        stem = original_path.stem        filepath = original_path.with_name(f"{stem}_{counter}.md")        counter += 1        filepath.write_text(note.to_markdown(), encoding='utf-8')    logger.info(f"Created note: {filepath.relative_to(self.vault_path)}")        return filepathdef _auto_route(self, note: ObsidianNote) -> Path:    """Auto-determine folder from tags"""    if "experiment" in note.tags:        return self.vault_path / "01_Projects/Experiments"    elif "paper" in note.tags or "reference" in note.tags:        return self.vault_path / "03_Resources/Papers"    elif "area" in note.tags or "topic" in note.tags:        return self.vault_path / "02_Areas/Research"    elif "archive" in note.tags or getattr(note, 'status', '') == "completed":        return self.vault_path / "04_Archive/Completed"        return self.vault_path / "00_Inbox"def generate_from_experiment(self,                               experiment_id: str,                              include_provenance: bool = True):    """    Generate complete note hierarchy από experiment.        Creates:    - Main experiment note    - Daily note link    - Method notes    - Result notes    - Connected to existing knowledge    """    from reproducibility import ReproducibilityManager        rm = ReproducibilityManager()    exp_dir = rm.base_dir / experiment_id        if not exp_dir.exists():        raise ValueError(f"Experiment not found: {experiment_id}")        manifest = json.loads((exp_dir / "manifest.json").read_text())        # Main experiment note    main_note = ResearchNote(        title=manifest["title"],        experiment_id=experiment_id,        tags=manifest.get("tags", []) + ["experiment", "active"],        hypothesis=manifest.get("hypothesis"),        content=self._generate_experiment_content(manifest, exp_dir),        metadata={            "experiment_id": experiment_id,            "created_date": manifest["created_at"],            "status": "active"        }    )        main_path = self.create_note(main_note, "01_Projects/Experiments")        # Method note (linked)    method_note = ObsidianNote(        title=f"{manifest['title']} - Methods",        content=self._generate_methods_content(exp_dir),        tags=["methods", "reproducibility"],        links=[main_note.title],        metadata={"parent_experiment": experiment_id}    )    self.create_note(method_note, "01_Projects/Experiments")        # Results note    results_note = ObsidianNote(        title=f"{manifest['title']} - Results",        content=self._generate_results_content(exp_dir),        tags=["results", "data"],        links=[main_note.title, method_note.title],        metadata={"parent_experiment": experiment_id}    )    self.create_note(results_note, "01_Projects/Experiments")        # Link to daily note    self._link_to_daily(main_note.title)        return main_pathdef _generate_experiment_content(self,                                   manifest: Dict,                                  exp_dir: Path) -> str:    """Generate content for main experiment note"""    lines = [        "## Overview",        f"{manifest.get('description', 'No description provided.')}",        "",        "## Research Questions",        "- ",        "",        "## Hypothesis",        f"> {manifest.get('hypothesis', 'To be determined')}",        "",        "## Progress",        "- [ ] Design",        "- [ ] Data collection",        "- [ ] Analysis",        "- [ ] Documentation",        "",        "## Environment",        f"- Python: {manifest.get('environment', {}).get('python_version', 'unknown')[:50]}",    ]        # Add packages table    packages = manifest.get('environment', {}).get('packages', {})    if packages:        lines.extend([            "",            "### Key Packages",            "",            "| Package | Version |",            "|---------|---------|",        ])        for pkg, ver in list(packages.items())[:10]:            lines.append(f"| {pkg} | {ver} |")        lines.extend([        "",        "## Related",        "- [[Research Areas]]",        "- [[Active Projects]]"    ])        return "\n".join(lines)def _generate_methods_content(self, exp_dir: Path) -> str:    """Generate detailed methods content"""    lines = ["## Computational Methods", ""]        prov_path = exp_dir / "provenance.jsonl"    if prov_path.exists():        lines.append("### Procedure")        lines.append("")        for i, line in enumerate(prov_path.read_text().strip().split('\n'), 1):            record = json.loads(line)            lines.append(f"{i}. **{record['operation']}**")            lines.append(f"   - Duration: {record['execution_time_ms']:.2f} ms")            lines.append(f"   - Timestamp: {record['timestamp']}")            lines.append("")        lines.extend([        "## Reproducibility",        f"- Experiment ID: `{exp_dir.name}`",        "- All code and data preserved",        "- See [[Reproducibility Checklist]]",        "",        "## Code Snippets",        "```python",        "# Key operations from this experiment",        "# Load from: " + str(exp_dir),        "```"    ])        return "\n".join(lines)def _generate_results_content(self, exp_dir: Path) -> str:    """Generate results content with artifact links"""    lines = ["## Key Findings", "", "> Summary of main results", "", "## Artifacts"]        artifacts_dir = exp_dir / "artifacts"    if 'No description')}")        lines.extend([        "",        "## Visualizations",        "![[results_plot.png]]",        "",        "## Statistical Summary",        "```dataview",        "TABLE file.name, experiment_id",        "FROM #results",        "WHERE experiment_id = this.experiment_id",        "```"    ])        return "\n".join(lines)def _link_to_daily(self, note_title: str):    """Add link to today's daily note"""    today_str = date.today().isoformat()    daily_path = self.vault_path / "00_Inbox" / f"{today_str}.md"        # Create daily if not exists    if not daily_path.exists():        daily_note = DailyNote()        daily_path.write_text(daily_note.to_markdown(), encoding='utf-8')        # Append link    with open(daily_path, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:        f.write(f"\n- Created: [[{note_title}]]\n")def create_canvas(self,                   title: str,                  nodes: List[Dict],                  edges: List[Dict]) -> Path:    """    Create Obsidian Canvas (visual note).        Canvas είναι JSON files με .canvas extension.    """    canvas_data = {        "nodes": [            {                "id": node.get("id", f"node{i}"),                "type": node.get("type", "text"),  # text, file, link                "text": node.get("text", ""),                "file": node.get("file"),                "x": node.get("x", i * 300),                "y": node.get("y", 0),                "width": node.get("width", 250),                "height": node.get("height", 150)            }            for i, node in enumerate(nodes)        ],        "edges": [            {                "id": edge.get("id", f"edge{i}"),                "fromNode": edge["from"],                "toNode": edge["to"],                "fromSide": edge.get("fromSide", "right"),                "toSide": edge.get("toSide", "left")            }            for i, edge in enumerate(edges)        ]    }        canvas_path = self.vault_path / "99_Meta/Graphs" / f"{title}.canvas"    canvas_path.write_text(json.dumps(canvas_data, indent=2))        return canvas_pathdef generate_knowledge_graph(self,                               center_note: str,                              depth: int = 2) -> Path:    """    Generate visual knowledge graph από note.        Creates canvas με connected notes.    """    # Collect nodes and edges    nodes = [{"id": "center", "text": center_note, "type": "text", "x": 0, "y": 0}]    edges = []        # Find linked notes (simplified - would parse all notes)    center_path = self._find_note(center_note)    if center_path:        content = center_path.read_text()        links = re.findall(r'$$\[([^$$]+)\]\]', content)                for i, link in enumerate(links[:10]):  # Limit για performance            nodes.append({                "id": f"link{i}",                "text": link,                "type": "text",                "x": 400,                "y": i * 200 - len(links) * 100            })            edges.append({                "from": "center",                "to": f"link{i}"            })        return self.create_canvas(f"Graph_{center_note}", nodes, edges)def _find_note(self, title: str) -> Optional[Path]:    """Find note by title in vault"""    for md_file in self.vault_path.rglob("*.md"):        if md_file.stem == title or title in md_file.read_text():            return md_file    return Nonedef create_dashboard(self):    """Create research dashboard με dataview queries"""    dashboard = ObsidianNote(        title="Research Dashboard",        tags=["dashboard", "meta"],        content='''
Active Experiments
TABLE status, experiment_id, file.mtime as "Last Modified"FROM #experiment AND #activeSORT file.mtime DESC
Recently Completed
TABLE status, experiment_idFROM #experiment AND #completedSORT file.mtime DESCLIMIT 5
Papers to Read
LISTFROM #paper AND -#readSORT file.name ASC
Knowledge Graph
[[Knowledge Graph Visualization]]

[[Daily Notes]]
[[Active Projects]]
[[Methods Library]]
[[Literature Review]]
’’’ )
    return self.create_note(dashboard, "99_Meta/Dashboards")def sync_with_experiments(self,                            repro_manager=None,                           bidirectional: bool = False):    """    Sync vault με experiment database.        If bidirectional: updates experiments από note edits.    """    if repro_manager is None:        from reproducibility import ReproducibilityManager        repro_manager = ReproducibilityManager()        # Find all experiment notes    exp_notes = list((self.vault_path / "01_Projects/Experiments").glob("*.md"))        for note_path in exp_notes:        # Parse frontmatter        content = note_path.read_text()        if content.startswith("---"):            _, frontmatter, body = content.split("---", 2)            metadata = yaml.safe_load(frontmatter)                        exp_id = metadata.get("experiment_id")            if exp_id:                # Check if experiment exists                exp_dir = repro_manager.base_dir / exp_id                if not exp_dir.exists():                    logger.warning(f"Experiment {exp_id} not found for note {note_path}")                    continue                                # Update experiment από note (if bidirectional)                if bidirectional:                    self._update_experiment_from_note(exp_id, metadata, body)        logger.info(f"Synced {len(exp_notes)} experiment notes")def _update_experiment_from_note(self,                                   exp_id: str,                                  metadata: Dict,                                  content: str):    """Update experiment record από note edits"""    # Implementation για bidirectional sync    passdef export_for_publication(self,                             note_title: str,                            format: str = "markdown",                            output_path: Optional[str] = None) -> str:    """    Export note for publication (clean, no Obsidian syntax).        Removes:    - WikiLinks → plain text or citations    - Dataview blocks    - Internal tags    """    note_path = self._find_note(note_title)    if not note_path:        raise ValueError(f"Note not found: {note_title}")        content = note_path.read_text()        # Remove frontmatter    if content.startswith("---"):        content = content.split("---", 2)[-1].strip()        # Convert WikiLinks    content = re.sub(r'$$\[([^$$|]+)\|?([^\]]*)\]\]',                     lambda m: m.group(2) or m.group(1),                     content)        # Remove dataview blocks    content = re.sub(r'```dataview.*?```', '', content, flags=re.DOTALL)        # Remove Obsidian comments    content = re.sub(r'%%.*?%%', '', content, flags=re.DOTALL)        # Save or return    if output_path:        Path(output_path).write_text(content, encoding='utf-8')        return output_path        return content
