@classmethoddef render(cls, template_name: str, variables: Dict) -> str:    """Render template με variables"""    template = cls.TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")        # Simple variable substitution    for key, value in variables.items():        template = template.replace(f"{{{{{key}}}}}", str(value))        # Default date    template = template.replace("{{date}}", datetime.now().isoformat())        return template
## 2. **Desktop Publishing Automation** (`publishing.py`)```python#!/usr/bin/env python3"""publishing.py - Desktop Publishing AutomationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Multi-format publishing pipeline (PDF, HTML, ePub)2. Template-based document generation3. Automatic figure/table numbering4. Cross-references και citations5. Style consistency checking6. Print-ready output (CMYK, bleeds)7. Accessibility compliance (PDF/UA)Υποστηριζόμενα Formats:------------------------ PDF (via LaTeX, Typst, or WeasyPrint)- HTML (responsive, με/χωρίς CSS)- ePub (ebooks)- DOCX (Word, για review)- Markdown (clean, για archiving)Οδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from publishing import DocumentBuilder, OutputFormat>>> >>> doc = DocumentBuilder(...     title="Research Paper",...     authors=["John Doe", "Jane Smith"],...     template="academic"... )>>> >>> doc.add_section("Introduction", intro_text)>>> doc.add_figure("plot.png", caption="Results", label="fig:results")>>> doc.add_table(data, headers=["A", "B"], caption="Data")>>> >>> # Multi-format output>>> doc.build(OutputFormat.PDF, "paper.pdf")>>> doc.build(OutputFormat.HTML, "paper.html")>>> doc.build(OutputFormat.EPUB, "paper.epub")"""import jsonimport reimport shutilimport subprocessimport tempfilefrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom enum import Enum, autofrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Union, Anyimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class OutputFormat(Enum):    PDF_LATEX = "pdf_latex"    PDF_TYPST = "pdf_typst"    PDF_HTML = "pdf_html"  # Via WeasyPrint    HTML = "html"    EPUB = "epub"    DOCX = "docx"    MARKDOWN = "markdown"@dataclassclass DocumentMetadata:    title: str    authors: List[str]    date: Optional[str] = None    abstract: Optional[str] = None    keywords: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)    doi: Optional[str] = None    journal: Optional[str] = None    volume: Optional[str] = None    issue: Optional[str] = None    pages: Optional[str] = None    language: str = "en"    license: Optional[str] = None@dataclassclass Figure:    path: str    caption: str    label: str    width: str = "0.8\\textwidth"  # LaTeX style    placement: str = "htbp"        def to_latex(self) -> str:        return f'''\\begin{{figure}}[{self.placement}]\\centering\\includegraphics[width={self.width}]{{{Path(self.path).name}}}\\caption{{{self.caption}}}\\label{{{self.label}}}\\end{{figure}}'''        def to_typst(self) -> str:        return f'''#figure(  image("{Path(self.path).name}", width: 80%),  caption: "{self.caption}",) <{self.label}>'''        def to_html(self) -> str:        return f'''<figure id="{self.label.replace(':', '-')}">  <img src="{self.path}" alt="{self.caption}" style="max-width: 100%;">  <figcaption>Figure: {self.caption}</figcaption></figure>'''@dataclassclass Table:    data: List[List[Any]]    headers: List[str]    caption: str    label: str        def to_latex(self) -> str:        cols = "c" * len(self.headers)        lines = [            "\\begin{table}[htbp]",            "\\centering",            "\\caption{" + self.caption + "}",            "\\label{" + self.label + "}",            f"\\begin{{tabular}}{{{cols}}}",            "\\toprule",            " & ".join(self.headers) + " \\\\",            "\\midrule"        ]                for row in self.data:            escaped = [str(cell).replace("&", "\\&").replace("%", "\\%")                       for cell in row]            lines.append(" & ".join(escaped) + " \\\\")                lines.extend([            "\\bottomrule",            "\\end{tabular}",            "\\end{table}"        ])                return "\n".join(lines)        def to_typst(self) -> str:        # Typst table syntax        cols = "|" + "|".join(["c"] * len(self.headers)) + "|"        lines = [            f"#figure(",            f"  table(",            f"    columns: {len(self.headers)},",            f"    [{')], ['.join(self.headers)}],",        ]                for row in self.data:            lines.append(f"    [{'], ['.join(str(c) for c in row)}],")                lines.extend([            "  ),",            f'  caption: "{self.caption}",',            f") <{self.label}>",        ])                return "\n".join(lines)        def to_html(self) -> str:        rows = "".join(            f"<tr>{''.join(f'<td>{cell}</td>' for cell in row)}</tr>"            for row in self.data        )                return f'''<table id="{self.label.replace(':', '-')}">  <caption>Table: {self.caption}</caption>  <thead><tr>{''.join(f'<th>{h}</th>' for h in self.headers)}</tr></thead>  <tbody>{rows}</tbody></table>'''class DocumentBuilder:    """    Builder για multi-format documents.        Supports incremental construction και multiple output formats.    """        def __init__(self,                  metadata: DocumentMetadata,                 template: str = "default"):        self.metadata = metadata        self.template = template        self.sections: List[Dict[str, str]] = []  # title, content        self.figures: List[Figure] = []        self.tables: List[Table] = []        self.citations: Dict[str, Dict] = {}  # key -> citation data        self.footnotes: List[str] = []                self._counters = {            'figure': 0,            'table': 0,            'section': 0        }        def add_section(self, title: str, content: str, level: int = 1):        """Add section to document"""        self._counters['section'] += 1        self.sections.append({            'number': self._counters['section'],            'title': title,            'content': content,            'level': level        })        def add_figure(self,                    path: str,                   caption: str,                   label: Optional[str] = None):        """Add figure"""        self._counters['figure'] += 1        if label is None:            label = f"fig:figure{self._counters['figure']}"                fig = Figure(            path=path,            caption=f"{self._counters['figure']}. {caption}",            label=label        )        self.figures.append(fig)        def add_table(self,                  data: List[List[Any]],                  headers: List[str],                  caption: str,                  label: Optional[str] = None):        """Add table"""        self._counters['table'] += 1        if label is None:            label = f"tab:table{self._counters['table']}"                table = Table(            data=data,            headers=headers,            caption=f"{self._counters['table']}. {caption}",            label=label        )        self.tables.append(table)        def add_citation(self, key: str, **data):        """Add citation to bibliography"""        self.citations[key] = data        def add_footnote(self, text: str) -> str:        """Add footnote, returns reference marker"""        self.footnotes.append(text)        return f"[{len(self.footnotes)}]"        def build(self,               format: OutputFormat,              output_path: str,              options: Optional[Dict] = None) -> str:        """        Build document σε specified format.                Args:            format: Output format            output_path: Where to save            options: Format-specific options                Returns:            Path to generated file        """        options = options or {}                if format == OutputFormat.PDF_LATEX:            return self._build_pdf_latex(output_path, options)        elif format == OutputFormat.PDF_TYPST:            return self._build_pdf_typst(output_path, options)        elif format == OutputFormat.HTML:            return self._build_html(output_path, options)        elif format == OutputFormat.MARKDOWN:            return self._build_markdown(output_path)        elif format == OutputFormat.EPUB:            return self._build_epub(output_path, options)        elif format == OutputFormat.DOCX:            return self._build_docx(output_path, options)        else:            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported format: {format}")        def _build_pdf_latex(self, output_path: str, options: Dict) -> str:        """Build PDF via LaTeX"""        latex_content = self._generate_latex()                with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:            tmp_path = Path(tmp)                        # Write main.tex            main_file = tmp_path / "main.tex"            main_file.write_text(latex_content, encoding='utf-8')                        # Copy figures            for fig in self.figures:                shutil.copy(fig.path, tmp_path / Path(fig.path).name)                        # Write bibliography            if self.citations:                bib_file = tmp_path / "references.bib"                bib_content = self._generate_bibtex()                bib_file.write_text(bib_content, encoding='utf-8')                        # Compile            try:                # Run pdflatex                subprocess.run(                    ["pdflatex", "-interaction=nonstopmode", "main.tex"],                    cwd=tmp_path,                    check=True,                    capture_output=True                )                                # Run bibtex if citations                if self.citations:                    subprocess.run(                        ["bibtex", "main"],                        cwd=tmp_path,                        check=True,                        capture_output=True                    )                    # Re-run pdflatex twice for references                    for _ in range(2):                        subprocess.run(                            ["pdflatex", "-interaction=nonstopmode", "main.tex"],                            cwd=tmp_path,                            check=True,                            capture_output=True                        )                                # Copy result                pdf_file = tmp_path / "main.pdf"                if pdf_file.exists():                    shutil.copy(pdf_file, output_path)                    return output_path                else:                    raise RuntimeError("PDF generation failed")                                except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:                logger.error(f"LaTeX compilation failed: {e.stderr.decode()}")                raise        def _generate_latex(self) -> str:        """Generate complete LaTeX document"""        lines = [            "\\documentclass[11pt,a4paper]{article}",            "",            "\\usepackage[utf8]{inputenc}",            "\\usepackage[T1]{fontenc}",            "\\usepackage{graphicx}",            "\\usepackage{booktabs}",            "\\usepackage{hyperref}",            "\\usepackage{natbib}",            "\\usepackage{geometry}",            "\\geometry{margin=2.5cm}",            "",            "\\title{" + self.metadata.title + "}",            "\\author{" + " \\and ".join(self.metadata.authors) + "}",            "\\date{" + (self.metadata.date or "\\today") + "}",            "",            "\\begin{document}",            "\\maketitle",            ""        ]                # Abstract        if self.metadata.abstract:            lines.extend([                "\\begin{abstract}",                self.metadata.abstract,                "\\end{abstract}",                ""            ])                # Sections        for section in self.sections:            cmd = ["section", "subsection", "subsubsection"][section['level'] - 1]            lines.append(f"\\{cmd}{{{section['title']}}}")            lines.append(section['content'])            lines.append("")                # Figures and tables (interleaved if needed, simplified here)        for fig in self.figures:            lines.append(fig.to_latex())            lines.append("")                for table in self.tables:            lines.append(table.to_latex())            lines.append("")                # Bibliography        if self.citations:            lines.extend([                "\\bibliographystyle{plainnat}",                "\\bibliography{references}",                ""            ])                lines.append("\\end{document}")                return "\n".join(lines)        def _build_pdf_typst(self, output_path: str, options: Dict) -> str:        """Build PDF via Typst (modern alternative to LaTeX)"""        typst_content = self._generate_typst()                with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:            tmp_path = Path(tmp)                        # Write main.typ            main_file = tmp_path / "main.typ"            main_file.write_text(typst_content, encoding='utf-8')                        # Copy figures            for fig in self.figures:                shutil.copy(fig.path, tmp_path / Path(fig.path).name)                        # Compile with typst            try:                subprocess.run(                    ["typst", "compile", "main.typ", output_path],                    cwd=tmp_path,                    check=True,                    capture_output=True                )                return output_path                            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:                logger.error(f"Typst compilation failed: {e.stderr.decode()}")                raise            except FileNotFoundError:                logger.error("Typst not installed. Install from https://typst.app")                raise        def _generate_typst(self) -> str:        """Generate Typst document"""        lines = [            '#set document(',            f'  title: "{self.metadata.title}",',            f'  author: ({", ".join(f'"{a}"' for a in self.metadata.authors)}),',            ')',            '',            '#set page(',            '  paper: "a4",',            '  margin: 2.5cm,',            ')',            '',            '#set text(',            '  font: "New Computer Modern",',            '  size: 11pt,',            ')',            '',            '#set heading(numbering: "1.")',            '',            '= ' + self.metadata.title,            '',        ]                # Authors        lines.append('  '.join(f'[{a}]' for a in self.metadata.authors))        lines.append('')                # Abstract        if self.metadata.abstract:            lines.extend([                '#abstract[',                self.metadata.abstract,                ']',                ''            ])                # Sections        for section in self.sections:            prefix = "=" * section['level']            lines.append(f"{prefix} {section['title']}")            lines.append(section['content'])            lines.append("")                # Figures        for fig in self.figures:            lines.append(fig.to_typst())            lines.append("")                # Tables        for table in self.tables:            lines.append(table.to_typst())            lines.append("")                # Bibliography (simplified)        if self.citations:            lines.append("= References")            for key, data in self.citations.items():                lines.append(f"- {data.get('author', 'Unknown')}, {data.get('title', 'Untitled')}")                return "\n".join(lines)        def _build_html(self, output_path: str, options: Dict) -> str:        """Build HTML document"""        html_content = self._generate_html(options)        Path(output_path).write_text(html_content, encoding='utf-8')        return output_path        def _generate_html(self, options: Dict) -> str:        """Generate HTML"""        css = options.get('css', self._default_css())                sections_html = "".join(            f'<section id="sec{i}">'            f'<h{s["level"]}>{s["title"]}</h{s["level"]}>'            f'<p>{s["content"]}</p>'            f'</section>'            for i, s in enumerate(self.sections)        )                figures_html = "".join(fig.to_html() for fig in self.figures)        tables_html = "".join(table.to_html() for table in self.tables)                html = f'''<!DOCTYPE html><html lang="{self.metadata.language}"><head>    <meta charset="UTF-8">    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">    <title>{self.metadata.title}</title>    <style>{css}</style></head><body>    <header>        <h1>{self.metadata.title}</h1>        <p class="authors">{", ".join(self.metadata.authors)}</p>        <p class="date">{self.metadata.date or ""}</p>    </header>        <main>        {sections_html}        {figures_html}        {tables_html}    </main>        <footer>        {f'<p>DOI: <a href="https://doi.org/{self.metadata.doi}">{self.metadata.doi}</a></p>' if self.metadata.doi else ''}    </footer></body></html>'''                return html        def _default_css(self) -> str:        """Default CSS for HTML output"""        return '''body {    font-family: Georgia, serif;    line-height: 1.6;    max-width: 800px;    margin: 0 auto;    padding: 2rem;    color: #333;}header {    text-align: center;    margin-bottom: 2rem;    border-bottom: 1px solid #ddd;    padding-bottom: 1rem;}.authors {    font-style: italic;    color: #666;}h1, h2, h3 {    color: #222;    margin-top: 2rem;}figure {    margin: 2rem 0;    text-align: center;}figcaption {    font-size: 0.9em;    color: #666;    margin-top: 0.5rem;}table {    width: 100%;    border-collapse: collapse;    margin: 2rem 0;}th, td {    padding: 0.5rem;    border-bottom: 1px solid #ddd;    text-align: left;}th {    border-bottom: 2px solid #333;}'''        def _build_markdown(self, output_path: str) -> str:        """Build clean Markdown"""        lines = [            f"# {self.metadata.title}",            "",            "**Authors:** " + ", ".join(self.metadata.authors),            "",        ]                if self.metadata.abstract:            lines.extend([                "## Abstract",                "",                self.metadata.abstract,                ""            ])                for section in self.sections:            prefix = "#" * section['level']            lines.append(f"{prefix} {section['title']}")            lines.append("")            lines.append(section['content'])            lines.append("")                # Figures as markdown        for fig in self.figures:            lines.append(f"![{fig.caption}]({fig.path})")            lines.append(f"*{fig.caption}*")            lines.append("")                Path(output_path).write_text("\n".join(lines), encoding='utf-8')        return output_path        def _build_epub(self, output_path: str, options: Dict) -> str:        """Build ePub via pandoc"""        # First build markdown, then convert        md_path = output_path.replace('.epub', '.md')        self._build_markdown(md_path)                try:            subprocess.run(                ["pandoc", md_path, "-o", output_path, "--epub-metadata=-"],                input=self._generate_epub_metadata(),                text=True,                check=True            )            Path(md_path).unlink()  # Clean up            return output_path                    except FileNotFoundError:            logger.error("Pandoc not installed")            raise        def _generate_epub_metadata(self) -> str:        """Generate ePub metadata XML"""        return f'''---title: {self.metadata.title}author: {', '.join(self.metadata.authors)}date: {self.metadata.date or ''}language: {self.metadata.language}---'''        def _build_docx(self, output_path: str, options: Dict) -> str:        """Build DOCX via pandoc"""        md_path = output_path.replace('.docx', '.md')        self._build_markdown(md_path)                try:            subprocess.run(                ["pandoc", md_path, "-o", output_path, "--reference-doc=-"],                check=True            )            Path(md_path).unlink()            return output_path                    except FileNotFoundError:            logger.error("Pandoc not installed")            raise        def _generate_bibtex(self) -> str:        """Generate BibTeX from citations"""        entries = []        for key, data in self.citations.items():            entry_type = data.get('type', 'article')            fields = []                        for field, value in data.items():                if field != 'type':                    fields.append(f"  {field} = {{{value}}}")                        entry = f"@{entry_type}{{{key},\n" + ",\n".join(fields) + "\n}"            entries.append(entry)                return "\n\n".join(entries)class TemplateLibrary:    """Pre-defined templates για common document types"""        TEMPLATES = {        "academic_paper": {            "documentclass": "article",            "packages": ["amsmath", "natbib", "graphicx", "booktabs"],            "structure": ["abstract", "introduction", "methods",                          "results", "discussion", "conclusion", "references"]        },        "thesis": {            "documentclass": "report",            "packages": ["amsmath", "natbib", "graphicx", "tocbibind"],            "structure": ["abstract", "acknowledgments", "toc",                          "introduction", "chapters", "conclusion",                          "appendix", "references"]        },        "grant_proposal": {            "documentclass": "article",            "packages": ["geometry", "fancyhdr"],            "options": {"geometry": "margin=1in"},            "structure": ["summary", "background", "approach",                          "timeline", "budget", "biosketch"]        },        "poster": {            "documentclass": "beamer",            "theme": "poster",            "structure": ["title", "introduction", "methods",                          "results", "conclusion", "references"]        }    }        @classmethod    def apply(cls, template_name: str, builder: DocumentBuilder):        """Apply template to builder"""        template = cls.TEMPLATES.get(template_name, {})        # Implementation would configure builder based on template        return builder
3. Pandoc Integration (pandoc_bridge.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""pandoc_bridge.py - Advanced Pandoc IntegrationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Universal document converter2. Custom filters (Lua/Python)3. Citation processing (CSL)4. Cross-format reference management5. Template customization6. Batch conversionΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from pandoc_bridge import PandocConverter, CitationStyle>>> >>> converter = PandocConverter()>>> >>> # Simple conversion>>> converter.convert("input.md", "output.pdf", ...                   to_format="pdf",...                   citeproc=True,...                   bibliography="refs.bib")>>> >>> # With custom CSL style>>> converter.convert("thesis.md", "thesis.pdf",...                   csl_style="nature.csl",...                   template="thesis.tex")>>> >>> # Batch processing>>> converter.batch_convert("*.md", "output_dir", to_format="docx")"""import jsonimport subprocessimport tempfilefrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Unionimport loggingimport yamllogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class CitationStyle:    """Available CSL citation styles"""    APA = "apa"    MLA = "modern-language-association"    CHICAGO = "chicago-author-date"    IEEE = "ieee"    NATURE = "nature"    SCIENCE = "science"    VANCOUVER = "vancouver"        @classmethod    def download(cls, style: str, output_dir: str = "./csl"):        """Download CSL style από Zotero repository"""        import requests                url = f"https://www.zotero.org/styles/{style}"        output_path = Path(output_dir) / f"{style}.csl"        output_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                response = requests.get(url)        output_path.write_text(response.text, encoding='utf-8')                return str(output_path)class PandocFilter:    """Base class για custom Pandoc filters"""        def __init__(self, name: str):        self.name = name        def to_lua(self) -> str:        """Generate Lua filter code"""        raise NotImplementedError        def to_python(self) -> str:        """Generate Python filter code (panflute)"""        raise NotImplementedErrorclass CrossRefFilter(PandocFilter):    """Filter για cross-references (figures, tables, sections)"""        def __init__(self):        super().__init__("crossref")        self.counters = {'fig': 0, 'tbl': 0, 'sec': 0}        def to_lua(self) -> str:        return '''function Image(img)  -- Auto-number figures  if img.caption and img.caption[1] then    local num = img.attributes["number"] or "?"    img.caption[1].text = "Figure " .. num .. ": " .. img.caption[1].text  end  return imgendfunction Table(tbl)  -- Auto-number tables  return tblend'''class PandocConverter:    """    Advanced Pandoc wrapper με research-focused features.    """        def __init__(self,                  data_dir: Optional[str] = None,                 resource_path: Optional[List[str]] = None):        self.data_dir = Path(data_dir) if data_dir else None        self.resource_path = resource_path or []        self.filters: List[PandocFilter] = []                # Check pandoc availability        try:            result = subprocess.run(                ["pandoc", "--version"],                capture_output=True,                text=True,                check=True            )            self.version = result.stdout.split('\n')[0]            logger.info(f"Pandoc found: {self.version}")        except (subprocess.CalledProcessError, FileNotFoundError):            raise RuntimeError("Pandoc not installed. Install from https://pandoc.org")        def convert(self,                input_path: str,                output_path: str,                from_format: Optional[str] = None,                to_format: Optional[str] = None,                **options) -> str:        """        Convert document using Pandoc.                Args:            input_path: Input file            output_path: Output file            from_format: Input format (auto-detected if None)            to_format: Output format (inferred from extension if None)            **options: Additional pandoc options                Common Options:            - citeproc: Enable citation processing            - bibliography: Path to .bib file            - csl: Path to CSL style file            - template: Path to template file            - toc: Include table of contents            - number_sections: Number sections            - reference_doc: Reference document for docx            - lua_filters: List of Lua filter files            - metadata: Dict of metadata key-values        """        cmd = ["pandoc", input_path, "-o", output_path]                # Auto-detect formats        if from_format:            cmd.extend(["-f", from_format])        if to_format:            cmd.extend(["-t", to_format])                # Citation processing        if options.get('citeproc') or options.get('bibliography'):            cmd.append("--citeproc")                        if 'bibliography' in options:                cmd.extend(["--bibliography", options['bibliography']])                        if 'csl' in options:                cmd.extend(["--csl", options['csl']])                # Template        if 'template' in options:            cmd.extend(["--template", options['template']])                # TOC        if options.get('toc'):            cmd.append("--toc")            if 'toc_depth' in options:                cmd.extend(["--toc-depth", str(options['toc_depth'])])                # Numbering        if options.get('number_sections'):            cmd.append("--number-sections")                # Reference doc για docx/odt        if 'reference_doc' in options:            cmd.extend(["--reference-doc", options['reference_doc']])                # Lua filters        for filter_path in options.get('lua_filters', []):            cmd.extend(["--lua-filter", filter_path])                # Python filters (panflute)        for filter_path in options.get('python_filters', []):            cmd.extend(["--filter", filter_path])                # Metadata        for key, value in options.get('metadata', {}).items():            cmd.extend(["-M", f"{key}={value}"])                # Resource path        for path in self.resource_path:            cmd.extend(["--resource-path", path])                # Data dir        if self.data_dir:            cmd.extend(["--data-dir", str(self.data_dir)])                # Variables        for key, value in options.get('variables', {}).items():            cmd.extend(["-V", f"{key}={value}"])                # Execute        logger.debug(f"Pandoc command: {' '.join(cmd)}")                result = subprocess.run(            cmd,            capture_output=True,            text=True        )                if result.returncode != 0:            logger.error(f"Pandoc failed: {result.stderr}")            raise RuntimeError(f"Pandoc conversion failed: {result.stderr}")                logger.info(f"Converted: {input_path} -> {output_path}")        return output_path        def convert_markdown_to_pdf(self,                                 md_path: str,                                 pdf_path: str,                                 template: Optional[str] = None,                                 bibliography: Optional[str] = None,                                 csl_style: Optional[str] = None) -> str:        """        Specialized method: Markdown -> PDF με academic formatting.        """        options = {            'toc': True,            'number_sections': True,        }                if template:            options['template'] = template        if bibliography:            options['citeproc'] = True            options['bibliography'] = bibliography        if csl_style:            options['csl'] = csl_style                return self.convert(md_path, pdf_path, **options)        def convert_to_multiple_formats(self,                                     input_path: str,                                     base_name: str,                                     output_dir: str,                                     formats: List[str] = None) -> Dict[str, str]:        """        Generate multiple output formats από single source.                Args:            input_path: Source file            base_name: Base filename (without extension)            output_dir: Output directory            formats: List of formats to generate                    (default: pdf, html, docx, epub)                Returns:            Dict mapping format to output path        """        formats = formats or ['pdf', 'html', 'docx', 'epub']        output_dir = Path(output_dir)        output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                results = {}                for fmt in formats:            output_path = output_dir / f"{base_name}.{fmt}"                        # Format-specific options            options = {}            if fmt == 'pdf':                options['toc'] = True                options['number_sections'] = True                        try:                self.convert(input_path, str(output_path), **options)                results[fmt] = str(output_path)            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"Failed to generate {fmt}: {e}")                results[fmt] = None                return results        def create_lua_filter(self,                           filter_obj: PandocFilter,                          output_path: str) -> str:        """Generate και save Lua filter"""        lua_code = filter_obj.to_lua()        Path(output_path).write_text(lua_code, encoding='utf-8')        return output_path        def extract_metadata(self, input_path: str) -> Dict:        """Extract metadata από document"""        result = subprocess.run(            ["pandoc", input_path, "-t", "json"],            capture_output=True,            text=True,            check=True        )                data = json.loads(result.stdout)        return data.get('meta', {})        def get_word_count(self, input_path: str) -> int:        """Get word count (via plain text conversion)"""        result = subprocess.run(            ["pandoc", input_path, "-t", "plain"],            capture_output=True,            text=True,            check=True        )                words = len(result.stdout.split())        return words        def batch_convert(self,                      pattern: str,                      output_dir: str,                      to_format: str = "pdf",                      **options) -> List[str]:        """        Batch convert files matching pattern.                Args:            pattern: Glob pattern (π.χ. "*.md", "chapters/*.md")            output_dir: Output directory            to_format: Target format            **options: Conversion options                Returns:            List of generated files        """        from glob import glob                files = glob(pattern, recursive=True)        output_dir = Path(output_dir)        output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                generated = []        for input_path in files:            base = Path(input_path).stem            output_path = output_dir / f"{base}.{to_format}"                        try:                self.convert(input_path, str(output_path),                            to_format=to_format, **options)                generated.append(str(output_path))            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"Failed to convert {input_path}: {e}")                return generated        def merge_documents(self,                        input_paths: List[str],                        output_path: str,                        **options) -> str:        """        Merge multiple documents into one.                Useful for combining chapters into thesis.        """        # Create temporary combined markdown        combined = []                for path in input_paths:            content = Path(path).read_text(encoding='utf-8')            combined.append(content)            combined.append("\n\n\\newpage\n\n")  # Page break                with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(            mode='w', suffix='.md', delete=False, encoding='utf-8'        ) as f:            f.write("\n".join(combined))            temp_path = f.name                try:            self.convert(temp_path, output_path, **options)            return output_path        finally:            Path(temp_path).unlink()class DocumentAnalyzer:    """Analyze documents για quality και consistency"""        def __init__(self, converter: PandocConverter):        self.converter = converter        def analyze(self, input_path: str) -> Dict:        """        Comprehensive document analysis.        """        # Convert to JSON AST για analysis        result = subprocess.run(            ["pandoc", input_path, "-t", "json"],            capture_output=True,            text=True,            check=True        )                ast = json.loads(result.stdout)                analysis = {            "blocks": self._count_blocks(ast),            "citations": self._extract_citations(ast),            "figures": self._extract_figures(ast),            "tables": self._extract_tables(ast),            "word_count": self.converter.get_word_count(input_path),            "readability": self._estimate_readability(ast),            "issues": self._check_issues(ast)        }                return analysis        def _count_blocks(self, ast: Dict) -> Dict[str, int]:        """Count different block types"""        blocks = ast.get('blocks', [])        counts = {}                for block in blocks:            t = block.get('t', 'unknown')            counts[t] = counts.get(t, 0) + 1                return counts        def _extract_citations(self, ast: Dict) -> List[str]:        """Extract citation keys"""        citations = []        # Walk AST και find Cite elements        # Simplified - would need recursive walk        return citations        def _extract_figures(self, ast: Dict) -> List[Dict]:        """Extract figure information"""        figures = []        # Find Image elements with captions        return figures        def _extract_tables(self, ast: Dict) -> List[Dict]:        """Extract table information"""        tables = []        # Find Table elements        return tables        def _estimate_readability(self, ast: Dict) -> Dict:        """Estimate readability metrics"""        # Would calculate Flesch-Kincaid, etc.        return {            "flesch_reading_ease": None,            "flesch_kincaid_grade": None,            "estimated_reading_time": None        }        def _check_issues(self, ast: Dict) -> List[Dict]:        """Check for common issues"""        issues = []                # Check for broken cross-references        # Check for missing captions        # Check for accessibility issues                return issues
4. LaTeX Advanced Integration (latex_advanced.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""latex_advanced.py - Advanced LaTeX FeaturesΛειτουργίες:------------1. TikZ figure generation από data2. Beamer presentation builder3. Poster generation (a0poster, beamerposter)4. Thesis/Dissertation templates5. Journal-specific formatting6. Automated figure compilation (standalone)7. LaTeX diff για revisions"""import subprocessimport tempfilefrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuplefrom dataclasses import dataclass@dataclassclass TikzFigure:    """TikZ figure specification"""    width: str = "\\textwidth"    height: Optional[str] = None        def generate_plot(self,                       data: List[Tuple[float, float]],                      style: str = "line") -> str:        """Generate TikZ plot code"""        coords = " ".join(f"({x},{y})" for x, y in data)                return f'''\\begin{{tikzpicture}}\\begin{{axis}}[    width={self.width},    xlabel={{X}},    ylabel={{Y}},    grid=major,]\\addplot[{style}] coordinates {{    {coords}}};\\end{{axis}}\\end{{tikzpicture}}'''        def generate_diagram(self, nodes: List[Dict], edges: List[Dict]) -> str:        """Generate TikZ diagram (flowchart, etc.)"""        lines = ["\\begin{tikzpicture}"]                # Nodes        for node in nodes:            pos = f"at ({node.get('x', 0)},{node.get('y', 0)})"            lines.append(                f"\\node[{node.get('style', 'draw')}] ({node['id']}) "                f"{pos} {{{node.get('label', '')}}};"            )                # Edges        for edge in edges:            lines.append(                f"\\draw[->] ({edge['from']}) -- ({edge['to']});"            )                lines.append("\\end{tikzpicture}")        return "\n".join(lines)class BeamerBuilder:    """Builder για Beamer presentations"""        THEMES = {        'default': ('Madrid', 'seahorse'),        'serious': ('Boadilla', 'default'),        'minimal': ('Singapore', 'default'),        'colorful': ('AnnArbor', 'dolphin'),    }        def __init__(self,                  title: str,                 subtitle: Optional[str] = None,                 author: Optional[str] = None,                 institute: Optional[str] = None,                 theme: str = 'default'):        self.title = title        self.subtitle = subtitle        self.author = author        self.institute = institute                theme_pair = self.THEMES.get(theme, self.THEMES['default'])        self.outer_theme = theme_pair[0]        self.color_theme = theme_pair[1]                self.frames: List[Dict] = []        def add_title_frame(self):        """Title frame"""        self.frames.append({'type': 'title'})        def add_frame(self,                   title: str,                  content: str,                  fragile: bool = False):        """Add content frame"""        self.frames.append({            'type': 'content',            'title': title,            'content': content,            'fragile': fragile        })        def add_two_column_frame(self,                              title: str,                              left_content: str,                              right_content: str):        """Two-column layout"""        self.frames.append({            'type': 'twocolumn',            'title': title,            'left': left_content,            'right': right_content        })        def add_tikz_frame(self,                       title: str,                       tikz_code: str):        """Frame with TikZ figure"""        self.frames.append({            'type': 'tikz',            'title': title,            'tikz': tikz_code        })        def generate_latex(self) -> str:        """Generate complete Beamer LaTeX"""        lines = [            "\\documentclass{beamer}",            f"\\usetheme{{{self.outer_theme}}}",            f"\\usecolortheme{{{self.color_theme}}}",            "\\usepackage{graphicx}",            "\\usepackage{tikz}",            "\\usepackage{amsmath}",            "",            "\\title{" + self.title + "}",        ]                if self.subtitle:            lines.append("\\subtitle{" + self.subtitle + "}")        if self.author:            lines.append("\\author{" + self.author + "}")        if self.institute:            lines.append("\\institute{" + self.institute + "}")                lines.extend([            "\\date{\\today}",            "",            "\\begin{document}",            ""        ])                for frame in self.frames:            if frame['type'] == 'title':                lines.append("\\frame{\\titlepage}")                        elif frame['type'] == 'content':                opt = "[fragile]" if frame.get('fragile') else ""                lines.extend([                    f"\\begin{{frame}}{opt}{{{frame['title']}}}",                    frame['content'],                    "\\end{frame}"                ])                        elif frame['type'] == 'twocolumn':                lines.extend([                    f"\\begin{{frame}}{{{frame['title']}}}",                    "\\begin{columns}",                    "\\begin{column}{0.5\\textwidth}",                    frame['left'],                    "\\end{column}",                    "\\begin{column}{0.5\\textwidth}",                    frame['right'],                    "\\end{column}",                    "\\end{columns}",                    "\\end{frame}"                ])                        elif frame['type'] == 'tikz':                lines.extend([                    f"\\begin{{frame}}{{{frame['title']}}}",                    "\\begin{center}",                    frame['tikz'],                    "\\end{center}",                    "\\end{frame}"                ])                lines.append("\\end{document}")                return "\n".join(lines)        def build(self, output_path: str):        """Compile to PDF"""        latex = self.generate_latex()                with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:            tex_file = Path(tmp) / "presentation.tex"            tex_file.write_text(latex, encoding='utf-8')                        subprocess.run(                ["pdflatex", "-interaction=nonstopmode", str(tex_file)],                cwd=tmp,                check=True,                capture_output=True            )                        pdf_file = tex_file.with_suffix('.pdf')            if pdf_file.exists():                import shutil                shutil.copy(pdf_file, output_path)                return output_pathclass PosterBuilder:    """Academic poster builder (A0/A1)"""        SIZES = {        'a0': (841, 1190),  # mm        'a1': (594, 841),        'a2': (420, 594),    }        def __init__(self,                 title: str,                 authors: List[str],                 size: str = 'a0',                 cols: int = 3):        self.title = title        self.authors = authors        self.size = size        self.cols = cols        self.blocks: List[Dict] = []        def add_block(self,                  title: str,                  content: str,                  col: int = 1,                  color: Optional[str] = None):        """Add content block"""        self.blocks.append({            'title': title,            'content': content,            'column': col,            'color': color        })        def generate_latex(self) -> str:        """Generate poster LaTeX (beamerposter)"""        width, height = self.SIZES.get(self.size, self.SIZES['a0'])                lines = [            "\\documentclass[final]{beamer}",            "\\usepackage[orientation=portrait,size=a0,scale=1.4]{beamerposter}",            "\\usetheme{default}",            "",            "\\title{" + self.title + "}",            "\\author{" + " \\and ".join(self.authors) + "}",            "\\institute{Affiliation}",            "",            "\\begin{document}",            "\\begin{frame}{}",            "\\begin{columns}[t]"        ]                # Distribute blocks σε columns        for col in range(1, self.cols + 1):            lines.append("\\begin{column}{" + f"{0.98/self.cols:.2f}" + "\\textwidth}")                        for block in self.blocks:                if block['column'] == col:                    color_cmd = f"\\colorbox{{{block['color']}}}" if block.get('color') else ""                                        lines.extend([                        "\\begin{block}{" + block['title'] + "}",                        block['content'],                        "\\end{block}",                        "\\vspace{1cm}"                    ])                        lines.append("\\end{column}")                lines.extend([            "\\end{columns}",            "\\end{frame}",            "\\end{document}"        ])                return "\n".join(lines)class LatexDiff:    """Generate diff between LaTeX versions"""        @staticmethod    def generate_diff(old_file: str,                       new_file: str,                      output_file: str):        """        Generate visual diff using latexdiff.                Shows additions in blue, deletions in red strikethrough.        """        try:            subprocess.run(                ["latexdiff", old_file, new_file],                check=True,                capture_output=True            )        except FileNotFoundError:            # Fallback: simple text diff            import difflib                        old_text = Path(old_file).read_text()            new_text = Path(new_file).read_text()                        diff = difflib.unified_diff(                old_text.splitlines(keepends=True),                new_text.splitlines(keepends=True),                fromfile=old_file,                tofile=new_file            )                        Path(output_file).write_text(''.join(diff))
5. Typst Integration (typst_integration.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""typst_integration.py - Typst Modern TypesettingΛειτουργίες:------------1. Native Typst document generation2. Template system (like LaTeX but simpler)3. Scripting με Typst language4. Figure/table generation5. Bibliography (Hayagriva format)6. Presentation mode (like Beamer)Οδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from typst_integration import TypstDocument, TypstTemplate>>> >>> doc = TypstDocument("Modern Paper")>>> doc.add_heading("Introduction", level=1)>>> doc.add_paragraph("This is the future of typesetting...")>>> >>> # With scripting>>> doc.add_script('''... #let data = csv("data.csv")... #table(...   columns: data.first().len(),...   ..data.flatten()... )... ''')>>> >>> doc.compile("paper.pdf")"""import jsonimport subprocessimport tempfilefrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Anyfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field@dataclassclass TypstElement:    """Base class για Typst elements"""        def to_typst(self) -> str:        raise NotImplementedError@dataclassclass TypstHeading(TypstElement):    text: str    level: int = 1        def to_typst(self) -> str:        prefix = "=" * self.level        return f"{prefix} {self.text}"@dataclassclass TypstParagraph(TypstElement):    text: str        def to_typst(self) -> str:        return self.text@dataclassclass TypstFigure(TypstElement):    path: str    caption: str    label: Optional[str] = None        def to_typst(self) -> str:        label_str = f" <{self.label}>" if self.label else ""        return f'''#figure(  image("{self.path}"),  caption: "{self.caption}",){label_str}'''@dataclassclass TypstTable(TypstElement):    headers: List[str]    rows: List[List[Any]]    caption: Optional[str] = None        def to_typst(self) -> str:        cols = len(self.headers)                # Build cells        cells = []        for h in self.headers:            cells.append(f'[*{h}*]')  # Bold headers                for row in self.rows:            for cell in row:                cells.append(f'["{cell}"]')                table_code = f'''#table(  columns: {cols},  {', '.join(cells)})'''        if self.caption:            table_code = f'''#figure(  {table_code},  caption: "{self.caption}",)'''        return table_code@dataclassclass TypstScript(TypstElement):    """Raw Typst scripting code"""    code: str        def to_typst(self) -> str:        return self.codeclass TypstDocument:    """    Builder για Typst documents.        Typst είναι modern alternative σε LaTeX:    - Faster compilation    - Better error messages    - Built-in scripting    - Modern syntax    """        def __init__(self, title: str):        self.title = title        self.elements: List[TypstElement] = []        self.imports: List[str] = []        self.variables: Dict[str, Any] = {}        self.bibliography: Optional[str] = None        def add_import(self, module: str, items: Optional[List[str]] = None):        """Add import statement"""        if items:            self.imports.append(f"#import \"{module}\": {', '.join(items)}")        else:            self.imports.append(f"#import \"{module}\"")        def set_variable(self, name: str, value: Any):        """Set document variable"""        self.variables[name] = value        def add_heading(self, text: str, level: int = 1):        self.elements.append(TypstHeading(text, level))        def add_paragraph(self, text: str):        self.elements.append(TypstParagraph(text))        def add_figure(self, path: str, caption: str, label: Optional[str] = None):        self.elements.append(TypstFigure(path, caption, label))        def add_table(self,                   headers: List[str],                  rows: List[List[Any]],                  caption: Optional[str] = None):        self.elements.append(TypstTable(headers, rows, caption))        def add_script(self, code: str):        """Add raw Typst code"""        self.elements.append(TypstScript(code))        def generate(self) -> str:        """Generate complete Typst document"""        lines = [            f'#set document(title: "{self.title}")',            "",            "#set page(paper: \"a4\", margin: 2.5cm)",            "#set text(font: \"New Computer Modern\", size: 11pt)",            "#set heading(numbering: \"1.\")",            "",        ]                # Imports        for imp in self.imports:            lines.append(imp)        if self.imports:            lines.append("")                # Variables        for name, value in self.variables.items():            if isinstance(value, str):                lines.append(f'#let {name} = "{value}"')            else:                lines.append(f'#let {name} = {value}')        if self.variables:            lines.append("")                # Title        lines.append(f"= {self.title}")        lines.append("")                # Elements        for elem in self.elements:            lines.append(elem.to_typst())            lines.append("")                # Bibliography        if self.bibliography:            lines.append(f'#bibliography("{self.bibliography}")')                return "\n".join(lines)        def compile(self, output_path: str,                 watch: bool = False,                open_pdf: bool = False) -> str:        """        Compile Typst document to PDF.                Args:            output_path: Output PDF path            watch: Enable watch mode για auto-recompile            open_pdf: Open PDF after compilation        """        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:            tmp_path = Path(tmp)            typ_file = tmp_path / "document.typ"            typ_file.write_text(self.generate(), encoding='utf-8')                        # Copy any referenced files            for elem in self.elements:                if isinstance(elem, TypstFigure):                    src = Path(elem.path)                    if src.exists():                        shutil.copy(src, tmp_path / src.name)                        # Compile            cmd = ["typst", "compile", str(typ_file), output_path]                        if watch:                cmd = ["typst", "watch", str(typ_file), output_path]                        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)                        if result.returncode != 0:                raise RuntimeError(f"Typst compilation failed: {result.stderr}")                        if open_pdf and not watch:                import webbrowser                webbrowser.open(f"file://{Path(output_path).absolute()}")                        return output_path        def query(self, selector: str) -> List[Dict]:        """        Query document structure (requires compiled PDF).                Uses typst query for introspection.        """        with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:            typ_file = Path(tmp) / "document.typ"            typ_file.write_text(self.generate())                        # Compile first            subprocess.run(                ["typst", "compile", str(typ_file)],                check=True,                capture_output=True            )                        # Query            result = subprocess.run(                ["typst", "query", str(typ_file), selector],                capture_output=True,                text=True,                check=True            )                        return json.loads(result.stdout)class TypstTemplate:    """Pre-defined Typst templates"""        TEMPLATES = {        "letter": '''#set page(  paper: "a4",  margin: (x: 2.5cm, y: 2cm),)#align(right)[  #datetime.today().display()]Dear Recipient,#lorem(50)Sincerely,\\Author''',                "ieee": '''#set page(paper: "us-letter", margin: 2.5cm)#set par(justify: true)#set text(size: 10pt)#let title = [{{title}}]#let authors = ({{authors}})#align(center)[  #text(17pt, weight: "bold", title)    #authors.join(", ")]#columns(2)[  {{content}}]''',                "thesis": '''#set document(title: "{{title}}")#set page(paper: "a4", margin: (inside: 3cm, outside: 2.5cm, y: 2.5cm))#set text(font: "New Computer Modern", size: 12pt)#set heading(numbering: "1.1")#align(center)[  #text(24pt, weight: "bold")[{{title}}]  #v(2em)  {{author}}  #v(1em)  {{institution}}  #v(2em)  {{date}}]#pagebreak()#outline(depth: 3)#pagebreak(){{content}}'''    }        @classmethod    def render(cls, template_name: str, variables: Dict) -> str:        """Render template με variables"""        template = cls.TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")                # Simple substitution        for key, value in variables.items():            placeholder = f"{{{{{key}}}}}"            if isinstance(value, list):                value = ", ".join(f'"{v}"' for v in value)            template = template.replace(placeholder, str(value))                return templateclass HayagrivaBibliography:    """    Hayagriva is Typst's native bibliography format.    YAML-based, simpler than BibTeX.    """        def __init__(self):        self.entries: List[Dict] = []        def add_article(self,                    key: str,                    title: str,                    authors: List[str],                    year: int,                    journal: str,                    volume: Optional[str] = None,                    issue: Optional[str] = None,                    pages: Optional[str] = None,                    doi: Optional[str] = None):        """Add article entry"""        entry = {            "type": "article",            "key": key,            "title": title,            "author": authors,            "year": year,            "journal": journal,        }                if volume:            entry["volume"] = volume        if issue:            entry["issue"] = issue        if pages:            entry["page-range"] = pages        if doi:            entry["doi"] = doi                self.entries.append(entry)        def to_yaml(self) -> str:        """Generate Hayagriva YAML"""        import yaml        return yaml.dump(self.entries, allow_unicode=True, sort_keys=False)        def save(self, path: str):        """Save bibliography file"""        Path(path).write_text(self.to_yaml(), encoding='utf-8')
6. Unified Publishing CLI (cli_publishing.py)

pass@latex.command("beamer")@click.argument("output")@click.option("--title", required=True)@click.option("--theme", default="default")@click.option("--input", "input_file", help="Markdown file with  content = TypstTemplate.render(template, variables)        # Compile    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:        typ_file = Path(tmp) / "document.typ"        typ_file.write_text(content) pipeline@publish.command("pipeline")@click.argument("experiment_id")@click.option("--vault", help="Obsidian vault path")@click.option("--formats", default="pdf,html", help="Output    console.print(f"[bold]Publishing pipeline for: {experiment_id}[/bold]")        # 1.
