Building documents...")    publish_path = Path(publish_dir)    publish_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)        # Create builder από experiment    # ... (implementation)        # 4. Multi-format output    console.print("4. Generating output formats...")    fmt_map = {        'pdf': OutputFormat.PDF_TYPST,  # Prefer Typst        'html': OutputFormat.HTML,        'docx': OutputFormat.DOCX,        'epub': OutputFormat.EPUB    }        for fmt in formats.split(','):        fmt = fmt.strip()        if fmt in fmt_map:            output_file = publish_path / f"{experiment_id}.{fmt}"            # Build...            console.print(f"   ✓ {output_file}")        console.print(f"[green]Publishing complete: {publish_dir}[/green]")if __name__ == "__main__":    publish()
Συνοπτικός Πίνακας Publishing Integrations:
Εργαλείο
Module
Βασικές Λειτουργίες
Obsidian
obsidian_integration.py
Vault sync, knowledge graphs, daily notes
Publishing
publishing.py
Multi-format builder (PDF/HTML/DOCX/ePub)
Pandoc
pandoc_bridge.py
Universal converter, CSL styles, batch processing
LaTeX
latex_advanced.py
Beamer, posters, TikZ, diffs
Typst
typst_integration.py
Modern typesetting, scripting, Hayagriva
Unified CLI
cli_publishing.py
Όλες οι εντολές σε ένα interface
Θέλεις να προσθέσω κάποιο άλλο εργαλείο (π.χ. Scribus για desktop publishing, InDesign integration, ή κάποιο συγκεκριμένο journal template) ή να εμβαθύνω σε κάποιο από τα υπάρχοντα;
User:
Indesign integration and automation
Kimi:
Θα προσθέσω πλήρη InDesign integration και automation για professional desktop publishing, με έμφαση σε data-driven layouts, automatic document generation, και XML-based workflows.
1. InDesign Core Integration (indesign_core.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""indesign_core.py - Adobe InDesign Automation CoreΛειτουργίες:------------1. COM/AppleScript bridge για InDesign control2. Document creation και manipulation3. Text frame management με styles4. Image placement και fitting5. Master page application6. Layer management7. Export to multiple formats (PDF, IDML, EPUB, HTML)8. Data merge για automatic layoutsΑπαιτήσεις:------------ Adobe InDesign (CC 2018 ή νεότερο)- Windows: pywin32- macOS: appscript ή subprocess για osascriptΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from indesign_core import InDesignApp, DocumentBuilder>>> >>> # Σύνδεση με running InDesign>>> indd = InDesignApp()>>> >>> # Δημιουργία document>>> doc = indd.create_document(...     page_size="A4",...     margins=(20, 20, 20, 20),  # mm...     columns=2... )>>> >>> # Add content>>> frame = doc.add_text_frame(...     x=20, y=50, width=170, height=200,...     content="Research Article Title"... )>>> frame.apply_style("Title")>>> >>> # Place image>>> img = doc.place_image("figure.png", x=20, y=100, width=80)>>> img.fit("proportional")>>> >>> # Export>>> doc.export_pdf("article.pdf", ...               preset="Smallest File Size",...               bleed=3)"""import osimport sysimport jsonimport tempfileimport subprocessfrom pathlib import Pathfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple, Union, Anyfrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom enum import Enumimport logginglogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class InDesignPlatform(Enum):    WINDOWS = "win32"    MACOS = "darwin"    UNSUPPORTED = "unsupported"class InDesignError(Exception):    """Custom exception για InDesign errors"""    pass@dataclassclass PageSize:    """Standard page sizes"""    name: str    width: float  # mm    height: float  # mm        # Standard sizes    A4 = ("A4", 210, 297)    A3 = ("A3", 297, 420)    A5 = ("A5", 148, 210)    LETTER = ("Letter", 215.9, 279.4)    LEGAL = ("Legal", 215.9, 355.6)    TABLOID = ("Tabloid", 279.4, 431.8)@dataclassclass InDesignMargins:    """Document margins"""    top: float    bottom: float    left: float    right: float        @classmethod    def uniform(cls, margin: float):        """Create uniform margins"""        return cls(margin, margin, margin, margin)        @classmethod    def symmetric(cls, inside: float, outside: float, top: float, bottom: float):        """Create symmetric margins (for facing pages)"""        return cls(top, bottom, inside, outside)@dataclassclass TextStyle:    """Paragraph/Character style definition"""    name: str    font_family: Optional[str] = None    font_size: Optional[float] = None  # pt    leading: Optional[float] = None  # pt    alignment: Optional[str] = None  # left, center, right, justify    space_before: Optional[float] = None  # mm    space_after: Optional[float] = None  # mm    color: Optional[str] = None  # hex or swatch name    bold: bool = False    italic: bool = False        def to_script_props(self) -> Dict:        """Convert to InDesign script properties"""        props = {}        if self.font_family:            props['appliedFont'] = self.font_family        if self.font_size:            props['pointSize'] = self.font_size        if self.leading:            props['leading'] = self.leading        if self.alignment:            align_map = {                'left': 1818584692,  # idLeftAlign                'center': 1667591796,  # idCenterAlign                'right': 1919379572,  # idRightAlign                'justify': 1785951334  # idLeftJustified            }            props['justification'] = align_map.get(self.alignment)        return propsclass InDesignBridge:    """    Platform-agnostic bridge to InDesign.        Handles Windows (COM) και macOS (AppleScript) differences.    """        def __init__(self):        self.platform = self._detect_platform()        self.app = None        self._connect()        def _detect_platform(self) -> InDesignPlatform:        """Detect operating system"""        if sys.platform == "win32":            return InDesignPlatform.WINDOWS        elif sys.platform == "darwin":            return InDesignPlatform.MACOS        else:            return InDesignPlatform.UNSUPPORTED        def _connect(self):        """Establish connection to InDesign"""        if self.platform == InDesignPlatform.WINDOWS:            self._connect_windows()        elif self.platform == InDesignPlatform.MACOS:            self._connect_macos()        else:            raise InDesignError(f"Unsupported platform: {sys.platform}")        def _connect_windows(self):        """Connect via COM on Windows"""        try:            import win32com.client            self.app = win32com.client.Dispatch("InDesign.Application")            logger.info(f"Connected to InDesign {self.app.Version}")        except ImportError:            raise InDesignError("pywin32 not installed. Run: pip install pywin32")        except Exception as e:            raise InDesignError(f"Cannot connect to InDesign: {e}")        def _connect_macos(self):        """Connect via AppleScript on macOS"""        # Check if InDesign is running        script = 'tell application "System Events" to return name of processes contains "Adobe InDesign"'        result = self._run_applescript(script)                if "true" not in result.lower():            raise InDesignError("InDesign is not running")                self.app = "applescript"  # Marker for AppleScript mode        logger.info("Connected to InDesign via AppleScript")        def _run_applescript(self, script: str) -> str:        """Execute AppleScript"""        result = subprocess.run(            ["osascript", "-e", script],            capture_output=True,            text=True        )        return result.stdout        def execute(self, script: str, language: str = "javascript") -> Any:        """        Execute script in InDesign.                Args:            script: Script code            language: "javascript" ή "applescript"        """        if self.platform == InDesignPlatform.WINDOWS:            # Use DoScript for JavaScript            return self.app.DoScript(script, 1246795079)  # idJavaScript        else:            # macOS: save to temp file και execute            if language == "javascript":                return self._execute_js_macos(script)            else:                return self._run_applescript(script)        def _execute_js_macos(self, script: str) -> str:        """Execute JavaScript on macOS via do script"""        # Escape quotes για AppleScript        escaped = script.replace('"', '\\"')                as_script = f'''        tell application "Adobe InDesign 2024"            do script "{escaped}" language javascript        end tell        '''                return self._run_applescript(as_script)        def create_document(self,                        width: float = 210,                       height: float = 297,                       margins: Optional[InDesignMargins] = None,                       columns: int = 1,                       gutter: float = 5,                       facing_pages: bool = False,                       pages: int = 1) -> 'InDesignDocument':        """Create new InDesign document"""                margins = margins or InDesignMargins.uniform(20)                script = f'''        var doc = app.documents.add({{            documentPreferences: {{                pageWidth: {width},                pageHeight: {height},                facingPages: {'true' if facing_pages else 'false'},                pagesPerDocument: {pages}            }},            marginPreferences: {{                top: {margins.top},                bottom: {margins.bottom},                left: {margins.left},                right: {margins.right},                columnCount: {columns},                columnGutter: {gutter}            }}        }});        doc.name;        '''                doc_name = self.execute(script)        return InDesignDocument(self, doc_name)        def open_document(self, path: str) -> 'InDesignDocument':        """Open existing document"""        script = f'''        var file = new File("{path.replace('\\', '/')}");        var doc = app.open(file);        doc.name;        '''                doc_name = self.execute(script)        return InDesignDocument(self, doc_name)        def quit(self, save_changes: bool = False):        """Quit InDesign"""        if self.platform == InDesignPlatform.WINDOWS:            self.app.Quit(save_changes)        else:            self._run_applescript('tell application "Adobe InDesign 2024" to quit')class InDesignDocument:    """Wrapper για InDesign document"""        def __init__(self, bridge: InDesignBridge, name: str):        self.bridge = bridge        self.name = name        self._page_counter = 0        def _doc_ref(self) -> str:        """Generate JavaScript reference to document"""        return f'app.documents.itemByName("{self.name}")'        def add_page(self,                  master_page: Optional[str] = None,                 at_end: bool = True) -> int:        """Add new page"""        self._page_counter += 1                master_ref = f'app.masterSpreads.itemByName("{master_page}")' if master_page else 'null'                script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var newPage = doc.pages.add({{            {'appliedMaster: ' + master_ref + ',' if master_page else ''}            {'atEnd: true' if at_end else ''}        }});        newPage.name;        '''                return self._page_counter        def add_text_frame(self,                       x: float,                       y: float,                       width: float,                       height: float,                       content: str = "",                       page_number: int = 1,                       layer: Optional[str] = None) -> 'TextFrame':        """Add text frame"""                script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var page = doc.pages[{page_number - 1}];        var frame = page.textFrames.add();        frame.geometricBounds = [{y}, {x}, {y + height}, {x + width}];        frame.contents = "{content.replace('"', '\\"')}";        {'frame.itemLayer = doc.layers.itemByName("' + layer + '");' if layer else ''}        frame.id;        '''                frame_id = self.bridge.execute(script)        return TextFrame(self.bridge, self, frame_id)        def place_image(self,                    image_path: str,                    x: float,                    y: float,                    width: Optional[float] = None,                    height: Optional[float] = None,                    page_number: int = 1) -> 'ImageFrame':        """Place image σε frame"""                script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var page = doc.pages[{page_number - 1}];        var frame = page.rectangles.add();        frame.geometricBounds = [{y}, {x},             {y + (height or 100)}, {x + (width or 100)}];                var imageFile = new File("{image_path.replace('\\', '/')}");        frame.place(imageFile);        frame.id;        '''                frame_id = self.bridge.execute(script)        return ImageFrame(self.bridge, self, frame_id)        def create_paragraph_style(self, style: TextStyle):        """Create paragraph style"""        props = style.to_script_props()        props_str = ", ".join(f"{k}: {v}" for k, v in props.items())                script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var style = doc.paragraphStyles.add({{            name: "{style.name}",            {props_str}        }});        '''                self.bridge.execute(script)        def create_master_page(self,                           name: str,                          based_on: Optional[str] = None) -> str:        """Create master spread"""        base_ref = f'app.masterSpreads.itemByName("{based_on}")' if based_on else 'null'                script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var master = doc.masterSpreads.add({{            name: "{name}",            baseName: {base_ref}        }});        "{name}";        '''                return self.bridge.execute(script)        def data_merge(self,                   data_source: str,                   template_page: int = 1) -> List[str]:        """        Data merge για automatic document generation.                Args:            data_source: Path to CSV ή XML file            template_page: Page with placeholder frames                Returns:            List of generated document paths        """        script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var dataFile = new File("{data_source.replace('\\', '/')}");                var merge = doc.dataMergeProperties;        merge.selectDataSource(dataFile);                // Create merged document        var mergedDoc = merge.mergeRecords();        var savePath = Folder.temp + "/merged_" + new Date().getTime() + ".indd";        mergedDoc.save(new File(savePath));        mergedDoc.close();                savePath;        '''                result = self.bridge.execute(script)        return [result]  # Could return multiple για multiple records        def export_pdf(self,                   output_path: str,                   preset: str = "High Quality Print",                   bleed: float = 0,                   marks: bool = False,                   spreads: bool = False):        """Export to PDF"""                script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var pdfExportPreset = app.pdfExportPresets.itemByName("{preset}");        var file = new File("{output_path.replace('\\', '/')}");                doc.exportFile(            ExportFormat.PDF_TYPE,            file,            false,  // showing options            pdfExportPreset        );                "Exported";        '''                # Add PDF export preferences        pref_script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        with (doc.pdfExportPreferences) {{            bleedBottom = {bleed};            bleedTop = {bleed};            bleedInside = {bleed};            bleedOutside = {bleed};            cropMarks = {'true' if marks else 'false'};            pageInformationMarks = {'true' if marks else 'false'};            exportReaderSpreads = {'true' if spreads else 'false'};        }}        '''                self.bridge.execute(pref_script)        self.bridge.execute(script)                logger.info(f"Exported PDF: {output_path}")        def export_idml(self, output_path: str):        """Export to IDML (InDesign Markup)"""        script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var file = new File("{output_path.replace('\\', '/')}");        doc.exportFile(ExportFormat.INDESIGN_MARKUP, file);        "Exported";        '''                self.bridge.execute(script)        def export_epub(self,                     output_path: str,                    cover_image: Optional[str] = None):        """Export to EPUB"""        script = f'''        var doc = {self._doc_ref()};        var file = new File("{output_path.replace('\\', '/')}");                with (doc.epubExportPreferences) {{            version = EpubVersion.EPUB3;            {'cover = new File("' + cover_image.replace('\\', '/') + '");' if cover_image else ''}        }}                doc.exportFile(ExportFormat.EPUB, file);        "Exported";        '''                self.bridge.execute(script)        def save(self, path: Optional[str] = None):        """Save document"""        if path:            script = f'''            var doc = {self._doc_ref()};            var file = new File("{path.replace('\\', '/')}");            doc.save(file);            '''        else:            script = f'{self._doc_ref()}.save();'                self.bridge.execute(script)        def close(self, save: bool = True):        """Close document"""        save_arg = 'SaveOptions.YES' if save else 'SaveOptions.NO'        script = f'{self._doc_ref()}.close({save_arg});'        self.bridge.execute(script)class TextFrame:    """Wrapper για text frame"""        def __init__(self, bridge: InDesignBridge, doc: InDesignDocument, frame_id: str):        self.bridge = bridge        self.doc = doc        self.id = frame_id        def _frame_ref(self) -> str:        return f'{self.doc._doc_ref()}.textFrames.itemByID({self.id})'        def set_content(self, text: str):        """Set text content"""        script = f'{self._frame_ref()}.contents = "{text.replace('"', '\\"')}";'        self.bridge.execute(script)        def apply_style(self, style_name: str):        """Apply paragraph style"""        script = f'''        var frame = {self._frame_ref()};        frame.paragraphs.everyItem().appliedParagraphStyle =             app.documents.itemByName("{self.doc.name}").paragraphStyles.itemByName("{style_name}");        '''        self.bridge.execute(script)        def set_geometry(self, x: float, y: float, width: float, height: float):        """Update frame geometry"""        script = f'''        {self._frame_ref()}.geometricBounds = [{y}, {x}, {y + height}, {x + width}];        '''        self.bridge.execute(script)        def link_to(self, other_frame: 'TextFrame'):        """Link text frame to another"""        script = f'''        {self._frame_ref()}.nextTextFrame = {other_frame._frame_ref()};        '''        self.bridge.execute(script)        def insert_content(self,                        content_type: str,                       data: Dict[str, Any]):        """        Insert dynamic content (XML, text variables, etc.)        """        if content_type == "xml":            # Insert XML element            tag = data.get('tag', 'Root')            xml_content = data.get('content', '')                        script = f'''            var frame = {self._frame_ref()};            var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{self.doc.name}");            var xmlElement = doc.xmlElements.add(doc.xmlTags.add("{tag}"));            xmlElement.contents = "{xml_content.replace('"', '\\"')}";            frame.placeXML(xmlElement);            '''            self.bridge.execute(script)class ImageFrame:    """Wrapper για image frame"""        def __init__(self, bridge: InDesignBridge, doc: InDesignDocument, frame_id: str):        self.bridge = bridge        self.doc = doc        self.id = frame_id        def _frame_ref(self) -> str:        return f'{self.doc._doc_ref()}.rectangles.itemByID({self.id})'        def fit(self, method: str = "proportional"):        """        Fit image to frame.                Methods:        - proportional: Fit proportionally        - fill: Fill frame (may crop)        - fit: Fit entirely (may leave space)        - stretch: Distort to fit        """        fit_constants = {            'proportional': 'FitOptions.PROPORTIONALLY',            'fill': 'FitOptions.FILL_PROPORTIONALLY',            'fit': 'FitOptions.FRAME_TO_CONTENT',            'stretch': 'FitOptions.CONTENT_TO_FRAME'        }                const = fit_constants.get(method, 'FitOptions.PROPORTIONALLY')                script = f'{self._frame_ref()}.fit({const});'        self.bridge.execute(script)        def set_geometry(self, x: float, y: float, width: float, height: float):        """Update frame geometry"""        script = f'''        {self._frame_ref()}.geometricBounds = [{y}, {x}, {y + height}, {x + width}];        '''        self.bridge.execute(script)        def apply_object_style(self, style_name: str):        """Apply object style"""        script = f'''        {self._frame_ref()}.appliedObjectStyle =             app.documents.itemByName("{self.doc.name}").objectStyles.itemByName("{style_name}");        '''        self.bridge.execute(script)
2. InDesign Templates & Automation (indesign_templates.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""indesign_templates.py - Pre-built InDesign Templates & AutomationΛειτουργίες:------------1. Research article templates2. Book/chapter templates3. Poster templates4. Report templates5. Catalog/brochure automation6. Data-driven layouts7. Style consistency checkingTemplates:----------- Academic Article (single/double column)- Research Report- Conference Poster (A0/A1)- Thesis/Dissertation- Annual Report- Product Catalog"""from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Anyfrom dataclasses import dataclassfrom pathlib import Pathimport jsonfrom indesign_core import (    InDesignBridge, InDesignDocument, TextStyle,     PageSize, InDesignMargins)@dataclassclass ArticleMetadata:    title: str    authors: List[str]    abstract: str    keywords: List[str]    journal: Optional[str] = None    volume: Optional[str] = None    issue: Optional[str] = None    year: Optional[int] = None    doi: Optional[str] = Noneclass ArticleTemplate:    """    Academic article template.        Supports single και double column layouts,    automatic figure/table numbering, reference formatting.    """        def __init__(self,                  columns: int = 2,                 page_size: tuple = PageSize.A4):        self.columns = columns        self.page_size = page_size        self.styles = self._define_styles()        def _define_styles(self) -> Dict[str, TextStyle]:        """Define paragraph styles"""        return {            "Title": TextStyle(                name="Title",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=18,                bold=True,                alignment="left",                space_after=6            ),            "Author": TextStyle(                name="Author",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=12,                alignment="left",                space_after=12            ),            "Abstract Title": TextStyle(                name="Abstract Title",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=10,                bold=True,                alignment="left",                space_before=12,                space_after=6            ),            "Abstract": TextStyle(                name="Abstract",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=9,                alignment="justify",                space_after=12            ),            "Heading 1": TextStyle(                name="Heading 1",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=12,                bold=True,                alignment="left",                space_before=12,                space_after=6            ),            "Heading 2": TextStyle(                name="Heading 2",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=10,                bold=True,                alignment="left",                space_before=6,                space_after=3            ),            "Body Text": TextStyle(                name="Body Text",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=10,                alignment="justify",                leading=12            ),            "Caption": TextStyle(                name="Caption",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=8,                alignment="left",                space_before=3,                space_after=6            ),            "Reference": TextStyle(                name="Reference",                font_family="Times New Roman",                font_size=8,                alignment="left",                leading=10            )        }        def create(self,                bridge: InDesignBridge,               metadata: ArticleMetadata) -> InDesignDocument:        """Create article document"""                # Create document        doc = bridge.create_document(            width=self.page_size[1],            height=self.page_size[2],            margins=InDesignMargins(20, 20, 20, 20),            columns=self.columns,            gutter=5,            facing_pages=False        )                # Create styles        for style in self.styles.values():            doc.create_paragraph_style(style)                # Page 1: Title, Authors, Abstract        y_pos = 20  # Start from top margin                # Title        title_frame = doc.add_text_frame(            x=20, y=y_pos,             width=170 if self.columns == 1 else 80,            height=30,            content=metadata.title        )        title_frame.apply_style("Title")        y_pos += 25                # Authors        authors_text = ", ".join(metadata.authors)        author_frame = doc.add_text_frame(            x=20, y=y_pos,            width=170 if self.columns == 1 else 80,            height=15,            content=authors_text        )        author_frame.apply_style("Author")        y_pos += 20                # Abstract        abstract_title = doc.add_text_frame(            x=20, y=y_pos, width=170, height=8,            content="Abstract"        )        abstract_title.apply_style("Abstract Title")        y_pos += 10                abstract_frame = doc.add_text_frame(            x=20, y=y_pos, width=170, height=40,            content=metadata.abstract        )        abstract_frame.apply_style("Abstract")        y_pos += 45                # Keywords        keywords_frame = doc.add_text_frame(            x=20, y=y_pos, width=170, height=10,            content="Keywords: " + ", ".join(metadata.keywords)        )        keywords_frame.apply_style("Body Text")                # Add body text frames για remaining pages        # (Would add more pages as needed)                return docclass PosterTemplate:    """    Academic poster template (A0/A1).        Grid-based layout με automatic sizing.    """        LAYOUTS = {        'classic': {            'columns': 3,            'header_height': 15,  # % of height            'sections': ['Introduction', 'Methods', 'Results',                         'Discussion', 'Conclusion', 'References']        },        'modern': {            'columns': 4,            'header_height': 12,            'sections': ['Background', 'Approach', 'Key Results',                        'Implications', 'Future Work']        }    }        def __init__(self,                 size: str = "A0",                 layout: str = "classic",                 colors: Optional[Dict] = None):        self.size = size        self.layout_config = self.LAYOUTS.get(layout, self.LAYOUTS['classic'])        self.colors = colors or {            'primary': '0x1a5490',            'secondary': '0x4a90c6',            'accent': '0xf39c12',            'text': '0x2c3e50',            'background': '0xffffff'        }                # Dimensions        self.dimensions = {            'A0': (841, 1189),            'A1': (594, 841)        }.get(size, (841, 1189))        def create(self,               bridge: InDesignBridge,               title: str,               authors: List[str],               institution: str,               logo_path: Optional[str] = None) -> InDesignDocument:        """Create poster document"""                width, height = self.dimensions                # Create document (single page)        doc = bridge.create_document(            width=width,            height=height,            margins=InDesignMargins.uniform(20),            columns=1,  # We'll handle columns manually            facing_pages=False,            pages=1        )                # Create color swatches        for name, hex_color in self.colors.items():            rgb = self._hex_to_rgb(hex_color)            script = f'''            var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}");            var color = doc.colors.add({{                name: "{name}",                model: ColorModel.PROCESS,                space: ColorSpace.RGB,                colorValue: [{rgb[0]}, {rgb[1]}, {rgb[2]}]            }});            '''            bridge.execute(script)                # Header        header_height = height * (self.layout_config['header_height'] / 100)                header_frame = doc.add_text_frame(            x=20, y=20,            width=width - 40,            height=header_height - 40,            content=title        )                # Style header        header_script = f'''        var frame = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}").textFrames[0];        frame.texts[0].appliedFont = app.fonts.itemByName("Arial Bold");        frame.texts[0].pointSize = 72;        frame.texts[0].fillColor = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}").colors.itemByName("primary");        frame.textFramePreferences.verticalJustification = VerticalJustification.CENTER_ALIGN;        '''        bridge.execute(header_script)                # Add authors        author_y = header_height - 30        author_frame = doc.add_text_frame(            x=20, y=author_y,            width=width - 40,            height=20,            content=", ".join(authors) + " | " + institution        )                # Grid layout for sections        cols = self.layout_config['columns']        col_width = (width - 40 - (cols - 1) * 15) / cols        section_height = (height - header_height - 60) / 2  # 2 rows                sections = self.layout_config['sections']                for i, section in enumerate(sections):            col = i % cols            row = i // cols                        x = 20 + col * (col_width + 15)            y = header_height + 20 + row * (section_height + 15)                        # Section background            bg_script = f'''            var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}");            var rect = doc.pages[0].rectangles.add();            rect.geometricBounds = [{y}, {x}, {y + section_height}, {x + col_width}];            rect.fillColor = doc.colors.itemByName("background");            rect.strokeColor = doc.colors.itemByName("primary");            rect.strokeWeight = 2;            '''            bridge.execute(bg_script)                        # Section title            title_frame = doc.add_text_frame(                x=x + 5, y=y + 5,                width=col_width - 10,                height=15,                content=section            )                        title_script = f'''            var frame = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}").textFrames[frame.textFrames.length - 1];            frame.texts[0].appliedFont = app.fonts.itemByName("Arial Bold");            frame.texts[0].pointSize = 36;            frame.texts[0].fillColor = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}").colors.itemByName("primary");            '''            bridge.execute(title_script)                        # Content placeholder            content_frame = doc.add_text_frame(                x=x + 5, y=y + 25,                width=col_width - 10,                height=section_height - 35,                content=f"Add {section} content here..."            )                return doc        def _hex_to_rgb(self, hex_color: int) -> tuple:        """Convert hex to RGB values (0-255)"""        hex_str = hex(hex_color)[2:].zfill(6)        return (            int(hex_str[0:2], 16),            int(hex_str[2:4], 16),            int(hex_str[4:6], 16)        )class CatalogAutomation:    """    Automated catalog/brochure generation from data.        Data-driven layout με repeating elements.    """        def __init__(self,                 template_doc: Optional[str] = None,                 items_per_page: int = 4):        self.template_doc = template_doc        self.items_per_page = items_per_page        def generate_from_data(self,                           bridge: InDesignBridge,                           data: List[Dict],                           output_path: str):        """        Generate catalog από data records.                Args:            data: List of dictionaries με item data                  (title, description, image, price, etc.)        """        # Create or open template        if self.template_doc and Path(self.template_doc).exists():            doc = bridge.open_document(self.template_doc)        else:            doc = bridge.create_document(                page_size=PageSize.A4,                margins=InDesignMargins.uniform(15)            )                # Calculate grid        cols = 2        rows = self.items_per_page // cols                item_width = (210 - 30 - 5) / cols  # A4 width - margins - gutter        item_height = (297 - 30 - 5 * (rows - 1)) / rows                current_page = 1        items_on_page = 0                for record in data:            # Calculate position            col = items_on_page % cols            row = items_on_page // cols                        x = 15 + col * (item_width + 5)            y = 15 + row * (item_height + 5)                        # Add item frame            self._add_catalog_item(doc, x, y, item_width, item_height, record)                        items_on_page += 1                        # New page if needed            if items_on_page >= self.items_per_page:                doc.add_page()                current_page += 1                items_on_page = 0                doc.save(output_path)        return doc        def _add_catalog_item(self,                          doc: InDesignDocument,                          x: float, y: float,                          width: float, height: float,                          data: Dict):        """Add single catalog item"""        # Image        if 'image' in data:            img = doc.place_image(                data['image'],                x=x, y=y,                width=width * 0.9            )            img.fit("proportional")            y += height * 0.5  # Move down for text                # Title        title_frame = doc.add_text_frame(            x=x, y=y,            width=width * 0.9,            height=10,            content=data.get('title', 'Untitled')        )                # Description        if 'description' in data:            desc_frame = doc.add_text_frame(                x=x, y=y + 12,                width=width * 0.9,                height=20,                content=data['description'][:200]  # Truncate            )                # Price        if 'price' in data:            price_frame = doc.add_text_frame(                x=x, y=y + 35,                width=width * 0.9,                height=8,                content=f"${data['price']:.2f}"            )class StyleChecker:    """Check document για style consistency"""        def __init__(self, bridge: InDesignBridge):        self.bridge = bridge        def check_document(self, doc: InDesignDocument) -> Dict[str, Any]:        """        Run style consistency checks.                Returns:            Dict με issues και recommendations        """        checks = {            'fonts': self._check_fonts(doc),            'colors': self._check_colors(doc),            'spacing': self._check_spacing(doc),            'accessibility': self._check_accessibility(doc)        }                return checks        def _check_fonts(self, doc: InDesignDocument) -> List[Dict]:        """Check font usage"""        script = f'''        var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}");        var fonts = {{}};                for (var i = 0; i < doc.allPageItems.length; i++) {{            var item = doc.allPageItems[i];            if (item.hasOwnProperty("texts")) {{                for (var j = 0; j < item.texts.length; j++) {{                    var font = item.texts[j].appliedFont.name;                    fonts[font] = (fonts[font] || 0) + 1;                }}            }}        }}                JSON.stringify(fonts);        '''                result = self.bridge.execute(script)        fonts = json.loads(result)                issues = []        if len(fonts) > 3:            issues.append({                'type': 'warning',                'message': f'Too many fonts used ({len(fonts)}). Consider limiting to 2-3.'            })                return issues        def _check_colors(self, doc: InDesignDocument) -> List[Dict]:        """Check color usage"""        # Implementation...        return []        def _check_spacing(self, doc: InDesignDocument) -> List[Dict]:        """Check consistent spacing"""        return []        def _check_accessibility(self, doc: InDesignDocument) -> List[Dict]:        """Check accessibility (contrast, alt text, etc.)"""        return []
3. InDesign XML Workflow (indesign_xml.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""indesign_xml.py - XML-based InDesign WorkflowsΛειτουργίες:------------1. XML structure generation από data2. Tagged text import3. Automatic layout από XML4. XSLT transformations5. Structured content management6. DTD validationΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from indesign_xml import XMLStructure, InDesignXML>>> >>> # Create XML structure>>> xml = XMLStructure("Article")>>> xml.add_element("Title", "Research Title")>>> xml.add_element("Author", "John Doe")>>> >>> with xml.add_container("Body") as body:>>>     with body.add_container("Section", attrs={"title": "Intro"}) as sec:>>>         sec.add_element("Paragraph", "Content...")>>> >>> # Import to InDesign>>> indd_xml = InDesignXML(document)>>> indd_xml.import_structure(xml)>>> indd_xml.layout_automatically()"""import xml.etree.ElementTree as ETfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any, Iteratorfrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom contextlib import contextmanagerimport jsonclass XMLElement:    """Represents XML element για InDesign"""        def __init__(self,                  tag: str,                 content: Optional[str] = None,                 attrs: Optional[Dict] = None):        self.tag = tag        self.content = content        self.attrs = attrs or {}        self.children: List['XMLElement'] = []        self.parent: Optional['XMLElement'] = None        def add_child(self, element: 'XMLElement') -> 'XMLElement':        """Add child element"""        element.parent = self        self.children.append(element)        return element        def add_element(self,                     tag: str,                    content: Optional[str] = None,                    attrs: Optional[Dict] = None) -> 'XMLElement':        """Create και add child element"""        child = XMLElement(tag, content, attrs)        return self.add_child(child)        @contextmanager    def add_container(self,                       tag: str,                      attrs: Optional[Dict] = None) -> Iterator['XMLElement']:        """Context manager για nested elements"""        container = self.add_element(tag, attrs=attrs)        try:            yield container        finally:            pass        def to_xml(self) -> ET.Element:        """Convert to ElementTree element"""        elem = ET.Element(self.tag, self.attrs)                if self.content:            elem.text = self.content                for child in self.children:            elem.append(child.to_xml())                return elem        def to_string(self, pretty: bool = True) -> str:        """Generate XML string"""        elem = self.to_xml()                if pretty:            self._indent(elem)                return ET.tostring(elem, encoding='unicode')        def _indent(self, elem: ET.Element, level: int = 0):        """Add pretty printing indentation"""        i = "\n" + level * "  "        if len(elem):            if not elem.text or not elem.text.strip():                elem.text = i + "  "            if not elem.tail or not elem.tail.strip():                elem.tail = i            for child in elem:                self._indent(child, level + 1)            if not child.tail or not child.tail.strip():                child.tail = i        else:            if level and (not elem.tail or not elem.tail.strip()):                elem.tail = iclass XMLStructure:    """High-level XML structure builder"""        def __init__(self, root_tag: str = "Root"):        self.root = XMLElement(root_tag)        self._current = self.root        def add_element(self,                     tag: str,                    content: Optional[str] = None,                    attrs: Optional[Dict] = None) -> XMLElement:        """Add element to current context"""        return self._current.add_element(tag, content, attrs)        @contextmanager    def add_container(self,                      tag: str,                      attrs: Optional[Dict] = None) -> Iterator[XMLElement]:        """Add container element"""        container = self._current.add_element(tag, attrs=attrs)        old_current = self._current        self._current = container                try:            yield container        finally:            self._current = old_current        def to_string(self, pretty: bool = True) -> str:        """Generate XML string"""        # Add XML declaration        xml_str = self.root.to_string(pretty)        return '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>\n' + xml_strclass InDesignXML:    """    InDesign XML workflow manager.        Handles import, structure mapping, και automatic layout.    """        def __init__(self, document: 'InDesignDocument'):        self.doc = document        def import_structure(self,                          xml_structure: XMLStructure,                         merge: bool = False):        """        Import XML structure into InDesign document.                Args:            xml_structure: XML structure to import            merge: Merge with existing structure ή replace        """        # Save XML to temp file        import tempfile        xml_content = xml_structure.to_string()                with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(            mode='w', suffix='.xml', delete=False, encoding='utf-8'        ) as f:            f.write(xml_content)            xml_path = f.name                # Import via script        script = f'''        var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{self.doc.name}");        var xmlFile = new File("{xml_path.replace('\\', '/')}");                // Import XML        doc.importXML(xmlFile);                // Associate with structure        var root = doc.xmlElements[0];        root.markupTag = doc.xmlTags.add("Root");                "Imported";        '''                self.doc.bridge.execute(script)                # Cleanup        import os        os.unlink(xml_path)        def map_tags_to_styles(self, mapping: Dict[str, str]):        """        Map XML tags to paragraph styles.                Args:            mapping: Dict of {xml_tag: paragraph_style_name}        """        for tag, style in mapping.items():            script = f'''            var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{self.doc.name}");            var rule = doc.xmlImportMaps.add(                doc.xmlTags.itemByName("{tag}"),                doc.paragraphStyles.itemByName("{style}")            );            '''            self.doc.bridge.execute(script)        def layout_automatically(self,                              template_page: int = 1,                             flow_to_new_pages: bool = True):        """        Automatically layout XML content using placeholder frames.                InDesign will flow XML content into tagged frames.        """        script = f'''        var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{self.doc.name}");                // Get XML elements        var root = doc.xmlElements[0];                // Find placeholder frames (tagged with matching XML tags)        for (var i = 0; i < doc.pages.length; i++) {{            var page = doc.pages[i];            var frames = page.textFrames;                        for (var j = 0; j < frames.length; j++) {{                var frame = frames[j];                if (frame.associatedXMLElement) {{                    // Frame is already associated                    continue;                }}                                // Try to match by tag                var tag = frame.label;  // Use frame label as tag hint                if (tag) {{                    var elements = root.evaluateXPathExpression("//" + tag);                    if (elements.length > 0) {{                        elements[0].placeIntoFrame(page, frame.geometricBounds);                    }}                }}            }}        }}                // Flow to new pages if needed        {'doc.xmlElements[0].xmlItems[-1].insertTextAsContent("\\r", XMLElementPosition.ELEMENT_END);' if flow_to_new_pages else ''}                "Laid out";        '''                self.doc.bridge.execute(script)        def export_structure(self, output_path: str):        """Export document structure back to XML"""        script = f'''        var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{self.doc.name}");        var file = new File("{output_path.replace('\\', '/')}");        doc.exportFile(ExportFormat.XML, file);        "Exported";        '''                self.doc.bridge.execute(script)        def create_tagged_text(self,                            content: str,                           style_mappings: Dict[str, str]) -> str:        """        Create InDesign Tagged Text format.                This is a special format for importing styled text.        """        # Tagged Text header        header = "<ASCII-WIN>\n<Version:16><FeatureSet:InDesign-Roman>"                # Process content with style tags        processed = content        for style, tag in style_mappings.items():            # This is simplified - real implementation would parse            processed = processed.replace(                f"<{style}>",                f"<pstyle:{tag}>"            )                return header + "\n" + processedclass ResearchXMLBuilder:    """    Builder για research article XML structures.    """        def __init__(self):        self.structure = XMLStructure("Article")        def add_metadata(self,                     title: str,                     authors: List[str],                     abstract: str,                     keywords: List[str]):        """Add article metadata"""        with self.structure.add_container("FrontMatter") as fm:            fm.add_element("Title", title)                        with fm.add_container("Authors") as authors_elem:                for author in authors:                    authors_elem.add_element("Author", author)                        fm.add_element("Abstract", abstract)                        with fm.add_container("Keywords") as kw:                for keyword in keywords:                    kw.add_element("Keyword", keyword)        def add_section(self,                    title: str,                    content: List[str],                    figures: Optional[List[Dict]] = None):        """Add body section"""        with self.structure.add_container("Section", attrs={"title": title}) as sec:            for paragraph in content:                sec.add_element("Paragraph", paragraph)                        if figures:                with sec.add_container("Figures") as figs:                    for fig in figures:                        fig_elem = figs.add_element(                            "Figure",                            attrs={                                "id": fig.get('id', ''),                                "caption": fig.get('caption', '')                            }                        )                        fig_elem.add_element("ImagePath", fig.get('path', ''))        def add_references(self, references: List[Dict]):        """Add bibliography"""        with self.structure.add_container("BackMatter") as bm:            with bm.add_container("References") as refs:                for i, ref in enumerate(references, 1):                    ref_elem = refs.add_element(                        "Reference",                        attrs={"id": f"ref{i}"}                    )                    ref_elem.add_element("Authors", ", ".join(ref.get('authors', [])))                    ref_elem.add_element("Title", ref.get('title', ''))                    ref_elem.add_element("Year", str(ref.get('year', '')))                    ref_elem.add_element("Journal", ref.get('journal', ''))        def get_structure(self) -> XMLStructure:        """Get completed structure"""        return self.structure
4. InDesign Server/Headless (indesign_server.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""indesign_server.py - Server-side InDesign AutomationΛειτουργίες:------------1. InDesign Server integration (headless)2. Batch processing queue3. REST API για remote rendering4. Template-based generation5. PDF generation service6. Monitoring και loggingΑπαιτήσεις:------------ Adobe InDesign Server (licensed)- Ή: InDesign με visible=false automationΟδηγίες Χρήσης:--------------->>> from indesign_server import InDesignServer, JobQueue>>> >>> # Start server>>> server = InDesignServer(port=8080)>>> server.start()>>> >>> # Queue job>>> job = server.queue_job(>>>     template="article.indd",>>>     data={"title": "New Article", "content": "..."},>>>     output="output.pdf">>> )>>> >>> # Check status>>> print(job.status)  # pending, processing, completed, failed"""import threadingimport queueimport jsonimport timefrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Callable, Anyfrom dataclasses import dataclass, fieldfrom datetime import datetimefrom enum import Enumimport loggingimport tempfilefrom pathlib import Pathlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)class JobStatus(Enum):    PENDING = "pending"    PROCESSING = "processing"    COMPLETED = "completed"    FAILED = "failed"    CANCELLED = "cancelled"@dataclassclass RenderJob:    """Job για rendering"""    id: str    template: str    data: Dict[str, Any]    output_format: str  # pdf, idml, jpeg, etc.    output_path: str    status: JobStatus = JobStatus.PENDING    created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)    started_at: Optional[datetime] = None    completed_at: Optional[datetime] = None    error_message: Optional[str] = None    priority: int = 5  # 1-10, lower = higher priority        def to_dict(self) -> Dict:        return {            "id": self.id,            "template": self.template,            "status": self.status.value,            "created": self.created_at.isoformat(),            "started": self.started_at.isoformat() if self.started_at else None,            "completed": self.completed_at.isoformat() if self.completed_at else None,            "error": self.error_message        }class InDesignServer:    """    Server για headless InDesign processing.        Can run as standalone service ή integrated σε larger application.    """        def __init__(self,                 max_workers: int = 2,                 poll_interval: float = 1.0):        self.max_workers = max_workers        self.poll_interval = poll_interval                self.job_queue: queue.PriorityQueue = queue.PriorityQueue()        self.jobs: Dict[str, RenderJob] = {}        self.active_jobs: Dict[str, threading.Thread] = {}                self.is_running = False        self.worker_threads: List[threading.Thread] = []                self.callbacks: Dict[str, List[Callable]] = {            'job_completed': [],            'job_failed': [],            'job_started': []        }        def start(self):        """Start server"""        self.is_running = True                # Start worker threads        for i in range(self.max_workers):            worker = threading.Thread(                target=self._worker_loop,                name=f"Worker-{i}",                daemon=True            )            worker.start()            self.worker_threads.append(worker)                logger.info(f"InDesign Server started with {self.max_workers} workers")        def stop(self):        """Stop server gracefully"""        self.is_running = False                # Wait for workers to finish current jobs        for worker in self.worker_threads:            worker.join(timeout=30)                logger.info("InDesign Server stopped")        def _worker_loop(self):        """Worker thread main loop"""        while self.is_running:            try:                # Get job from queue (blocking with timeout)                priority, job_id = self.job_queue.get(timeout=self.poll_interval)                job = self.jobs.get(job_id)                                if not job or job.status != JobStatus.PENDING:                    continue                                # Process job                self._process_job(job)                            except queue.Empty:                continue            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"Worker error: {e}")        def _process_job(self, job: RenderJob):        """Process single job"""        try:            job.status = JobStatus.PROCESSING            job.started_at = datetime.now()            self._trigger_callback('job_started', job)                        # Create InDesign instance (or reuse)            from indesign_core import InDesignBridge                        bridge = InDesignBridge()                        # Open template            doc = bridge.open_document(job.template)                        # Update content with data            self._update_document(doc, job.data)                        # Export            if job.output_format == "pdf":                doc.export_pdf(job.output_path)            elif job.output_format == "idml":                doc.export_idml(job.output_path)            elif job.output_format == "epub":                doc.export_epub(job.output_path)                        doc.close(save=False)                        # Success            job.status = JobStatus.COMPLETED            job.completed_at = datetime.now()            self._trigger_callback('job_completed', job)                    except Exception as e:            logger.error(f"Job {job.id} failed: {e}")            job.status = JobStatus.FAILED            job.error_message = str(e)            job.completed_at = datetime.now()            self._trigger_callback('job_failed', job)        def _update_document(self,                          doc: 'InDesignDocument',                         data: Dict[str, Any]):        """Update document with data"""        # Find text frames by label και update content        for key, value in data.items():            if isinstance(value, str):                # Simple text replacement                script = f'''                var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}");                var frames = doc.textFrames;                                for (var i = 0; i < frames.length; i++) {{                    if (frames[i].label === "{key}") {{                        frames[i].contents = "{value.replace('"', '\\"')}";                    }}                }}                '''                doc.bridge.execute(script)                        elif isinstance(value, dict) and value.get('type') == 'image':                # Image replacement                script = f'''                var doc = app.documents.itemByName("{doc.name}");                var frames = doc.rectangles;  // Image frames                                for (var i = 0; i < frames.length; i++) {{                    if (frames[i].label === "{key}") {{                        var imgFile = new File("{value['path'].replace('\\', '/')}");                        frames[i].place(imgFile);                        frames[i].fit(FitOptions.PROPORTIONALLY);                    }}                }}                '''                doc.bridge.execute(script)        def queue_job(self,                  template: str,                  data: Dict[str, Any],                  output_path: str,                  output_format: str = "pdf",                  priority: int = 5) -> RenderJob:        """        Add job to queue.                Args:            template: Path to .indd template            data: Data για template population            output_path: Where to save output            output_format: Export format            priority: Lower number = higher priority                Returns:            RenderJob object        """        import uuid                job_id = str(uuid.uuid4())        job = RenderJob(            id=job_id,            template=template,            data=data,            output_format=output_format,            output_path=output_path,            priority=priority        )                self.jobs[job_id] = job        self.job_queue.put((priority, job_id))                logger.info(f"Queued job {job_id}: {template} -> {output_path}")                return job        def get_job_status(self, job_id: str) -> Optional[RenderJob]:        """Get job status"""        return self.jobs.get(job_id)        def cancel_job(self, job_id: str) -> bool:        """Cancel pending job"""        job = self.jobs.get(job_id)        if job and job.status == JobStatus.PENDING:            job.status = JobStatus.CANCELLED            return True        return False        def list_jobs(self,                   status: Optional[JobStatus] = None) -> List[RenderJob]:        """List jobs, optionally filtered by status"""        jobs = list(self.jobs.values())        if status:            jobs = [j for j in jobs if j.status == status]        return sorted(jobs, key=lambda j: j.created_at, reverse=True)        def on(self, event: str, callback: Callable):        """Register event callback"""        if event in self.callbacks:            self.callbacks[event].append(callback)        def _trigger_callback(self, event: str, job: RenderJob):        """Trigger callbacks for event"""        for callback in self.callbacks.get(event, []):            try:                callback(job)            except Exception as e:                logger.error(f"Callback error: {e}")class RESTAPIServer:    """    REST API wrapper για InDesignServer.        Provides HTTP endpoints για remote access.    """        def __init__(self, indesign_server: InDesignServer, port: int = 8080):        self.indd_server = indesign_server        self.port = port                try:            from flask import Flask, request, jsonify            self.flask = Flask            self.request = request            self.jsonify = jsonify            self.app = Flask(__name__)            self._setup_routes()        except ImportError:            raise ImportError("Flask required for REST API: pip install flask")        def _setup_routes(self):        """Setup Flask routes"""                @self.app.route('/health', methods=['GET'])        def health():            return self.jsonify({"status": "ok", "workers": self.indd_server.max_workers})                @self.app.route('/jobs', methods=['POST'])        def create_job():            data = self.request.json                        job = self.indd_server.queue_job(                template=data['template'],                data=data.get('data', {}),                output_path=data['output_path'],                output_format=data.get('format', 'pdf'),                priority=data.get('priority', 5)            )                        return self.jsonify({"job_id": job.id, "status": job.status.value}), 202                @self.app.route('/jobs/<job_id>', methods=['GET'])        def get_job(job_id):            job = self.indd_server.get_job_status(job_id)            if not job:                return self.jsonify({"error": "Job not found"}), 404                        return self.jsonify(job.to_dict())                @self.app.route('/jobs', methods=['GET'])        def list_jobs():            status = self.request.args.get('status')            if status:                status = JobStatus(status)                        jobs = self.indd_server.list_jobs(status)            return self.jsonify([j.to_dict() for j in jobs])                @self.app.route('/jobs/<job_id>/cancel', methods=['POST'])        def cancel_job(job_id):            success = self.indd_server.cancel_job(job_id)            if success:                return self.jsonify({"message": "Job cancelled"})            return self.jsonify({"error": "Cannot cancel job"}), 400        def start(self):        """Start Flask server"""        # Start InDesign server        self.indd_server.start()                # Start Flask (blocking)        self.app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=self.port)        def stop(self):        """Stop server"""        self.indd_server.stop()# Example usage για headless generationdef batch_generate_pdfs(template: str,                        data_list: List[Dict],                        output_dir: str,                        max_workers: int = 2):    """    Generate multiple PDFs from data using server.    """    server = InDesignServer(max_workers=max_workers)    server.start()        jobs = []    for i, data in enumerate(data_list):        output_path = f"{output_dir}/output_{i:03d}.pdf"        job = server.queue_job(template, data, output_path, priority=5)        jobs.append(job)        # Wait for completion    while any(j.status in [JobStatus.PENDING, JobStatus.PROCESSING] for j in jobs):        time.sleep(1)        server.stop()        # Report results    completed = sum(1 for j in jobs if j.status == JobStatus.COMPLETED)    failed = sum(1 for j in jobs if j.status == JobStatus.FAILED)        return {"completed": completed, "failed": failed}
5. Unified InDesign CLI (cli_indesign.py)
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""cli_indesign.py - Unified CLI for InDesign automation"""import clickfrom rich.console import Consolefrom rich.table import Tablefrom rich.progress import Progress, SpinnerColumn, TextColumnconsole = Console()@click.group()def indesign():    """Adobe InDesign automation commands"""    pass@indesign.command("connect")def connect():    """Test connection to InDesign"""    from indesign_core import InDesignBridge        try:        bridge = InDesignBridge()        console.print("[green]✓ Connected to InDesign[/green]")                # Get version info        if bridge.platform.value == "win32":            version = bridge.app.Version            console.print(f"Version: {version}")            except Exception as e:        console.print(f"[red]✗ Cannot connect: {e}[/red]")@indesign.command("article")@click.argument("output")@click.option("--title", required=True)@click.option("--authors", required=True, help="Comma-separated")@click.option("--abstract", default="")@click.option("--columns", type=click.Choice(["1", "2"]), default="2")@click.option("--template", help="Base template file")def create_article(output, title, authors, abstract, columns, template):    """Create academic article document"""    from indesign_core import InDesignBridge    from indesign_templates import abstract=abstract,        keywords=[]    )        tmpl = ArticleTemplate(        columns=int(columns),        page_size=PageSize.A4    )        doc = tmpl.create(bridge, metadata)    doc.save(output)        console.print(f"[green]Created article: {output}[/green]")@indesign.command("poster")@click.argument("output")@click.option("--title", required=True)@click.option("--authors", {output}[/green]")@indesign.command("catalog")@click.argument("data_file")@click.argument("output")@click.option("--template", help="Template document")@click.option("--items-per-page", default=4)def {output}[/green]")@indesign.command("xml-import")@click.argument("xml_file")@click.argument("document")@click.option("--map-styles", is_flag=True, help="Auto-map XML tags to styles")def mm")def export_document(document, output, format, preset, bleed):    """Export InDesign document"""    from indesign_core import InDesignBridge        bridge = InDesignBridge()    doc = bridge.open_document(document)        with Progress(        SpinnerColumn(),        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),        console=console    ) as progress:        task = doc.export_idml(output)        elif format == "epub":            doc.export_epub(output)                progress.update(task, completed=True)        console.print(f"[green]Exported: {output}[/green]")@indesign.command("server")@click.option("--port", default=8080)@click.option("--workers", default=2)def start_server(port, workers):    """Start InDesign Server for headless http://localhost:{port}/jobs/<job_id>")        try:        api_server.start()    except KeyboardInterrupt:        api_server.stop()        console.print("[yellow]Server stopped[/yellow]")@indesign.command("batch")@click.argument("template")@click.argument("data_file")@click.argument("output_dir")@click.option("--format", default="pdf")@click.option("--workers", default=2)def batch_process(template, data_file, output_dir, format, workers):    """Batch process multiple documents"""    from indesign_server import batch_generate_pdfs    import json        data_list = json.loads(Path(data_file).read_text())        console.print(f"Processing {len(data_list)} documents...")        results = batch_generate_pdfs(        template=template,        data_list=data_list,        output_dir=output_dir,        max_workers=workers    )        console.print(f"[green]Completed: {results['completed']}, Failed: {results['failed']}[/green]")@indesign.command("check")@click.argument("document")def check_document(document):    """Check document for style consistency"""    from indesign_core import checker.check_document(doc)        # Display results    for category, issues in results.items():        if issues:            console.print(f"\n[bold]{category.upper()}[/bold]")            for issue in issues:                color = "red" if issue['type'] == 'error' else "yellow"                console.print(f"  [{color}]{issue['type']}[/{color}]: {issue['message']}")        if not any(results.values()):        console.print("[green]✓ No issues found[/green]")if __name__ == "__main__":    indesign()

Θέλεις να προσθέσω κάποιο άλλο feature (π.χ. integration με specific journal templates, automatic figure sizing, ή interactive PDF features) ή να εμβαθύνω σε κάποιο από τα υπάρχοντα;

δώσε μου ό,τι χρειάζεται για να συνεχίσω σε άλλο chat.

Θα σου δώσω ένα πλήρες summary με όλα τα modules, τις εξαρτήσεις, και έναν οδηγό γρήγορης εκκίνησης για να συνεχίσεις σε άλλο chat.
📦 Complete Module Structure
manus_win11_framework/├── Core System│   ├── ai_router.py              # AI model selection & cost optimization│   ├── notifications.py          # Telegram/Slack alerts│   ├── state_manager.py          # SQLite persistence & resume│   ├── agent_core.py             # Base agent (v1)│   └── agent_core_v2.py          # Enhanced agent with security/plugins/memory│├── Security & Extensions│   ├── security.py               # Sandboxed execution, PII filtering│   ├── plugins.py                # Plugin system with hooks│   ├── memory.py                 # Vector memory & RAG│   └── performance.py            # Performance monitoring│├── Scientific Research│   ├── reproducibility.py        # Experiment tracking & provenance│   ├── data_validator.py         # Scientific data validation│   ├── literature.py             # Citation management│   ├── domains/│   │   ├── physics.py            # Physics calculations│   │   ├── biology.py            # Bioinformatics│   │   └── mathematics.py        # Symbolic math│   └── collaboration.py          # Multi-researcher workflows│├── External Integrations│   ├── jupyter_integration.py    # Jupyter notebooks & widgets│   ├── zotero_integration.py     # Zotero sync│   ├── overleaf_integration.py   # LaTeX/Overleaf sync│   ├── arxiv_integration.py      # arXiv search/download│   ├── git_integration.py        # Research repositories│   └── dashboard.py              # Web monitoring dashboard│├── Knowledge Management│   └── obsidian_integration.py   # Obsidian vault sync│├── Publishing & DTP│   ├── publishing.py             # Multi-format document builder│   ├── pandoc_bridge.py          # Universal document converter│   ├── latex_advanced.py         # Beamer, posters, TikZ│   ├── typst_integration.py      # Modern typesetting│   ├── indesign_core.py          # InDesign COM/AppleScript bridge│   ├── indesign_templates.py     # Article/poster/catalog templates│   ├── indesign_xml.py           # XML workflows│   └── indesign_server.py        # Headless InDesign server│└── CLI    ├── cli.py                    # Base CLI    ├── cli_extensions.py         # Advanced commands    ├── cli_research.py           # Research workflow CLI    ├── cli_research_unified.py   # Unified research CLI    ├── cli_publishing.py         # Publishing CLI    └── cli_indesign.py           # InDesign CLI

🚀 Quick Start Guide
1. Environment Setup
# Create projectmkdir manus_researchcd manus_researchpython -m venv venv# Activatevenv\Scripts\activate  # Windowssource venv/bin/activate  # Mac/Linux# Install dependenciespip install -r requirements.txt# Create structuremkdir -p {cache,memory,experiments,plugins,output}
2. Configuration (.env)
# AI APIs (at least one required)KIMI_API_KEY=your_key_hereDEEPSEEK_API_KEY=your_key_hereANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your_key_hereOPENAI_API_KEY=your_key_here# Notifications (optional)TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN=your_tokenTELEGRAM_CHAT_ID=your_chat_idSLACK_WEBHOOK_URL=your_webhook# Budget & SettingsDAILY_AI_BUDGET=10.0AGENT_DEFAULT_TEMPERATURE=0.7# External ToolsZOTERO_API_KEY=your_keyZOTERO_LIBRARY_ID=your_library_idOVERLEAF_GIT_URL=https://git.overleaf.com/...# PathsOBSIDIAN_VAULT_PATH=~/Documents/Obsidian/ResearchINDESIGN_TEMPLATES_PATH=./templates
3. Basic Usage Examples
# === CORE AGENT ===from agent_core_v2 import EnhancedAgentCore, EnhancedAgentConfigfrom ai_router import TaskTypeconfig = EnhancedAgentConfig(    project_id="experiment_001",    description="Quantum state analysis",    daily_budget=5.0,    enable_security=True,    enable_memory=True,    plugin_dirs=["./plugins"])agent = EnhancedAgentCore(config)# Run with planawait agent.execute_plan([    {        "name": "analyze_data",        "type": TaskType.ANALYSIS,        "description": "Analyze quantum measurements",        "prompt": "Analyze this dataset for entanglement patterns...",        "checkpoint": True,        "input_prompt": "Review analysis approach?"    }])
# === REPRODUCIBILITY ===from reproducibility import ReproducibilityManager, ExperimentConfigrm = ReproducibilityManager("./experiments")with rm.create_experiment(ExperimentConfig(    title="Bell State Tomography",    description="Full quantum state reconstruction",    tags=["quantum", "tomography"],    random_seed=42)) as exp:        # All operations tracked automatically    result = exp.execute(process_quantum_data, raw_data)    exp.record_artifact("density_matrix", result.rho)        # Generate methods section    methods = exp.generate_methods()
# === OBSIDIAN INTEGRATION ===from obsidian_integration import ObsidianVaultvault = ObsidianVault("~/Documents/Obsidian/Research")# Generate from experimentvault.generate_from_experiment("experiment_001")# Create knowledge graphvault.generate_knowledge_graph("Quantum ML")# Create daily notefrom obsidian_integration import DailyNotevault.create_note(DailyNote())
# === PUBLISHING ===from publishing import DocumentBuilder, DocumentMetadata, OutputFormatdoc = DocumentBuilder(    metadata=DocumentMetadata(        title="Quantum Machine Learning",        authors=["A. Researcher", "B. Scientist"],        abstract="We demonstrate..."    ),    template="academic")doc.add_section("Introduction", "Quantum computing...")doc.add_figure("results.png", "Main results", label="fig:main")# Multi-format outputdoc.build(OutputFormat.PDF_LATEX, "paper.pdf")doc.build(OutputFormat.HTML, "paper.html")doc.build(OutputFormat.EPUB, "paper.epub")
# === INDESIGN AUTOMATION ===from indesign_core import InDesignBridgefrom indesign_templates import ArticleTemplate, ArticleMetadatabridge = InDesignBridge()# Create articletemplate = ArticleTemplate(columns=2)doc = template.create(bridge, ArticleMetadata(    title="Research Title",    authors=["Author One", "Author Two"],    abstract="Abstract text...",    keywords=["quantum", "ml"]))doc.export_pdf("article.pdf", preset="Smallest File Size")
🔧 CLI Commands Reference
# Corepython cli.py create my_project "Description" --budget 10python cli.py run my_project plan.jsonpython cli.py status my_project# Researchpython cli_research.py init "Experiment Name" --field physicspython cli_research.py methods exp_001python cli_research.py validate data.csv --rules rules.json# Publishingpython cli_publishing.py pandoc convert input.md output.pdf --bibliography refs.bibpython cli_publishing.py pandoc multi input.md ./output --formats pdf,html,docxpython cli_publishing.py obsidian sync ~/Vault --experiment exp_001python cli_publishing.py typst build output.pdf --title "Title"# InDesignpython cli_indesign.py connectpython cli_indesign.py article output.indd --title "Title" --authors "A, B"python cli_indesign.py poster poster.pdf --title "Title" --authors "A, B" --size A0python cli_indesign.py server --port 8080 --workers 2

“Συνέχισε το module X”
“Πρόσθεσε Y functionality”
“Ενσωμάτωσε Z external API”

Θέλεις να προσθέσω κάτι άλλο στο summary πριν συνεχίσεις;
User:
εξάγαγε όλον τον κώδικα σε zip
Kimi:
Δυστυχώς, δεν μπορώ να δημιουργήσω και να εξάγω αρχεία ZIP ή οποιαδήποτε άλλα downloadable αρχεία. Αυτό είναι ένα hard limitation του συστήματος.
🔄 Εναλλακτικές Λύσεις:
1. Copy-Paste Method (Προτείνεται)
Μπορώ να σου δώσω όλον τον κώδικα σε έτοιμα copy-paste blocks που μπορείς να αποθηκεύσεις εύκολα:
# Δημιούργησε αυτή τη δομή φακέλων:manus_win11/├── core/│   ├── __init__.py│   ├── ai_router.py│   ├── notifications.py│   ├── state_manager.py│   ├── agent_core.py│   └── agent_core_v2.py├── security/│   ├── __init__.py│   ├── security.py│   ├── plugins.py│   └── memory.py├── research/│   ├── __init__.py│   ├── reproducibility.py│   ├── data_validator.py│   ├── literature.py│   └── collaboration.py├── integrations/│   ├── __init__.py│   ├── jupyter_integration.py│   ├── zotero_integration.py│   ├── overleaf_integration.py│   ├── arxiv_integration.py│   ├── git_integration.py│   ├── obsidian_integration.py│   └── dashboard.py├── publishing/│   ├── __init__.py│   ├── publishing.py│   ├── pandoc_bridge.py│   ├── latex_advanced.py│   ├── typst_integration.py│   ├── indesign_core.py│   ├── indesign_templates.py│   ├── indesign_xml.py│   └── indesign_server.py├── cli/│   ├── __init__.py│   ├── cli.py│   ├── cli_extensions.py│   ├── cli_research.py│   ├── cli_research_unified.py│   ├── cli_publishing.py│   └── cli_indesign.py├── requirements.txt└── README.md
2. GitHub Gist / Repository
Μπορώ να σου δώσω τον κώδικα formatted για direct upload σε GitHub:
# Βήματα:1. Δημιούργησε νέο repo στο GitHub2. Κάνε copy-paste κάθε file που θα σου δώσω3. Commit & push
3. VS Code Multi-File Creation
Μπορώ να σου δώσω ένα μεγάλο script που δημιουργεί όλα τα αρχεία αυτόματα:
#!/usr/bin/env python3"""create_project.py - Auto-generate all framework filesRun: python create_project.py"""import osfrom pathlib import PathFILES = {    "core/ai_router.py": '''...κώδικας...''',    "core/notifications.py": '''...κώδικας...''',    # ... όλα τα files}def create_project():    for filepath, content in FILES.items():        path = Path(filepath)        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)        path.write_text(content, encoding='utf-8')        print(f"Created: {filepath}")if __name__ == "__main__":    create_project()
🚀 Τι προτιμάς;
Πες μου:
“Δώσε μου όλον τον κώδικα σε copy-paste blocks”
Θα σου δώσω κάθε file ξεχωριστά, έτοιμο για αποθήκευση
“Φτιάξε το auto-generation script”
Ένα Python script που δημιουργεί όλα τα αρχεία με ένα run
“Δώσε μου συγκεκριμένα modules”
Μόνο τα βασικά (core + ένα integration) για αρχή
“Δώσε μου link για download”
Μπορώ να σε κατευθύνω σε εναλλατικές λύσεις (GitHub, κλπ)
Ποια επιλογή προτιμάς;
